
-----title
西安（长安县） (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b06af1cdaaf44118994f925b671d7283_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b06af1cdaaf44118994f925b671d7283");'><span id='b06af1cdaaf44118994f925b671d7283_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=720')">709-720年</a>，1-12岁</div><div id='b06af1cdaaf44118994f925b671d7283' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=709&endYear=709')">709年</a>　是年颜真卿生于京兆长安县敦化坊祖宅，排行第七。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=710&endYear=710')">710年</a>　是年在长安祖宅。弟颜允生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=711&endYear=711')">711年</a>　是年在长安祖宅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=712&endYear=712')">712年</a>　是年父颜惟贞遇疾而卒，时年约四十三。殷夫人（颜真卿之母）当携孤寄居于通化坊之娘家，依舅氏殷践猷而养育之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=713&endYear=716')">713-716年</a>　寄居于通化坊之娘家，依舅氏殷践猷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=717&endYear=717')">717年</a>　舅氏授秘书省学士，奉召偕韦述等二十人于秘阁刊正典籍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=718&endYear=718')">718年</a>　十月间，舅氏殷践猷徙入丽正殿充丽正殿直学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=719&endYear=719')">719年</a>　依舅氏殷践猷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=720&endYear=720')">720年</a>　舅氏殷践猷在曹州司法参军、丽正殿直学士任上修检《群书四录》，综治经部。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='f742f06d8020409ba5b567463407c6f1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f742f06d8020409ba5b567463407c6f1");'><span id='f742f06d8020409ba5b567463407c6f1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=742')">734-742年</a>，26-34岁</div><div id='f742f06d8020409ba5b567463407c6f1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　是年颜真卿举进士第。试《梓材赋》、《武库诗》，登甲科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　是年颜真卿娶房州刺史京兆韦景骏之孙、太子中舍人韦迪之女。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=734&endYear=734')">734年</a>　是年颜真卿在京兆有书。作品：《雁塔题名》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=735&endYear=735')">735年</a>　是年颜真卿偕萧颖士、李华、赵骅、柳芳、殷寅、陆据、邵轸始作开元八士之交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　季春，经吏部铨选试《三命判》入高等，举拔萃科。授朝散郎、秘书省著作局校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　是年颜真卿始与高适结交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=736&endYear=736')">736年</a>　是年颜真卿始编纂《韵海镜源》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年1月</a>　是年正月，应相州刺史张嘉祐之请为相州周太师尉迟公祠庙撰铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=737&endYear=737')">737年7月5日</a>　是年，姑母颜真定卒于其子殷成己尉氏县尉官舍，年八十四。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年1月</a>　正月，赴东京参预姑母颜真定葬礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=738&endYear=738')">738年</a>　母殷夫人卒，年六十余，颜真卿兄弟丁内忧，去职守丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=739&endYear=739')">739年</a>　是年活动不详，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=740&endYear=740')">740年</a>　偃师县丞堂兄春卿卒于长安，临终诿其子女于真卿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=741&endYear=741')">741年</a>　是年冬日，为润州刺史、江南东道采访使徐峤正书其所撰夫人王琳墓志。作品：《唐故赵郡君太原王氏墓志铭》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=742&endYear=742')">742年9月18日</a>　颜真卿以前资官由扶风郡太守崔琇荐举，入勤政务本楼参加“博学文词秀逸”制科考试，上第。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='fc874cfe810a4c3e93e8099c8653aced_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc874cfe810a4c3e93e8099c8653aced");'><span id='fc874cfe810a4c3e93e8099c8653aced_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=747')">746-747年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='fc874cfe810a4c3e93e8099c8653aced' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=746')">746年4月</a>　四月间，颜真卿以清白为关内道黜陟使王鉷荐举，授通直郎，陟长安县尉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=746&endYear=746')">746年</a>　是年在长安县尉任，为元大谦之妻罗婉顺撰写墓志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　自长安县尉迁御史台监察御史，秋日，巡复诸陵，寻充河东、朔方军试复屯交兵使。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4139e2c5048c483b96ba6df1c0f372de_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4139e2c5048c483b96ba6df1c0f372de");'><span id='4139e2c5048c483b96ba6df1c0f372de_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=752')">749-752年</a>，41-44岁</div><div id='4139e2c5048c483b96ba6df1c0f372de' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　返京，奏劾金吾将军李延业曾召蕃客内宴引驾仗不报事，从而出之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年8月</a>　八月，迁殿中侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　为高适诗集作四言诗数白字并序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　撰有《郭虚己碑》并正书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　撰有《郭虚己墓志》并正书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　撰有《郭揆碑》，并正书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年12月</a>　十二月，颜真卿再入御史台为侍御史。是时仲兄允南为左补阙，冬至朝贺，同行登殿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=750&endYear=750')">750年</a>　侍御史任上为臧怀亮夫人任氏撰有墓志。作品：《臧怀亮暨夫人任氏墓志》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=751&endYear=751')">751年</a>　季春，颜真卿自侍御史改兵部员外郎，掌判南曹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=752&endYear=752')">752年</a>　应西京千福寺楚金禅师之请，正书岑勋《千福寺多宝塔碑》徐浩题额。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='49bc5fe6e99c40bdbb976e6cf59bb059_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("49bc5fe6e99c40bdbb976e6cf59bb059");'><span id='49bc5fe6e99c40bdbb976e6cf59bb059_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='49bc5fe6e99c40bdbb976e6cf59bb059' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>代韦陟为御史大夫，有让表。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>西京收复，有司署祝文称“嗣皇帝”，即告礼仪使崔器遽奏改之，中旨宣劳。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>又鉴于太庙毁，奏请筑坛。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7775c2fd936f454d8f44b96a88797b93_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7775c2fd936f454d8f44b96a88797b93");'><span id='7775c2fd936f454d8f44b96a88797b93_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>，52岁</div><div id='7775c2fd936f454d8f44b96a88797b93' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年闰4月19日</a>　此日，因改元晋爵县公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年7月</a>　本月中旬，擘窠大书《天下放生池碑》，随表进奉，再求肃宗御书题额。既许，未及下，会十九日玄宗自兴庆宫移居西内，颜真卿首率百僚上表，请问起居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年7月</a>　不日，又因与御史中丞敬羽语及政事，被告忤旨，被贬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年8月16日</a>　八月十六日出贬蓬州长史。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bca7c4674c13419e903ae3485366fe3d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bca7c4674c13419e903ae3485366fe3d");'><span id='bca7c4674c13419e903ae3485366fe3d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=766')">762-766年</a>，54-58岁</div><div id='bca7c4674c13419e903ae3485366fe3d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年5月</a>　此月，召拜为利州刺史。因羌贼围城，不得至任，乃追赴上都。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年11月</a>　月初，归至西京，会仲兄国子司业允南病剧。不十日，即逝，年六十九。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年12月16日</a>　葬允南于祖茔，撰书神道碑志述之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=762&endYear=762')">762年12月</a>　此月，京兆尹户部侍郎判度支刘晏举以自代，除户部侍郎。有表谢。作品：《谢户部侍郎表》<div id='poem_1366747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366747' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_1_1366747_comment'></div>以臣为户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366747_comment'></div>荣宠自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366747_comment'></div>感戴交集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366747_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366747_comment'></div>臣闻地官之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366747_comment'></div>邦教是资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366747_comment'></div>侍郎之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366747_comment'></div>非贤不授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366747_comment'></div>况臣资性愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366747_comment'></div>行能无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366747_comment'></div>频以疏拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366747_comment'></div>获罪朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366747_comment'></div>五年之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366747_comment'></div>三贬官次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366747_comment'></div>先朝皇极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366747_comment'></div>犹佐藩条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366747_comment'></div>官阶勋封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366747_comment'></div>尽蒙黜削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366747_comment'></div>待罪三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366747_comment'></div>分从遐弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366747_comment'></div>属陛下以聪明睿哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366747_comment'></div>嗣圣登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366747_comment'></div>恩宥<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1366747", 1366747, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>广覃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366747_comment'></div>授臣利州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366747_comment'></div>诏书始下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366747_comment'></div>才涉旬朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366747_comment'></div>不遗易忘之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366747_comment'></div>忽奉待诏之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366747_comment'></div>生死骨肉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366747_comment'></div>受赐已深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366747_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1366747", class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366747_comment'></div>寤寐无宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366747_comment'></div>圣泽频繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366747_comment'></div>叨戴斯授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366747_comment'></div>循涯省分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366747_comment'></div>盈量则多。<div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年3月</a>　此月，改吏部侍郎，寻复阶银青光禄大夫。有谢表。作品：《谢吏部侍郎表》<div id='poem_1366742' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366742' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366742?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢吏部侍郎表</a><span class='authorDate'>（763年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · id='poem_sentence_1_1366742_comment'></div>以臣为吏部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366742_comment'></div>又奉某月日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366742_comment'></div>加臣银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366742_comment'></div>浃辰之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366742_comment'></div>殊泽荐至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366742_comment'></div>恭承宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366742_comment'></div>戴荷交驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366742_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366742_comment'></div>窃以国之所急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366742_comment'></div>必在官人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366742_comment'></div>铨综之司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366742_comment'></div>非贤弗授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366742_comment'></div>伏揆虚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366742_comment'></div>祗惧实深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366742_comment'></div>常恐上尘<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1366742", 1366742, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>则哲</span>之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366742_comment'></div>下负窃位之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366742_comment'></div>未酬万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366742_comment'></div>再沐恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366742_comment'></div>宠命忽临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366742_comment'></div>旧阶旋复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366742_comment'></div>叨荣既甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366742_comment'></div>宥过何深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366742_comment'></div>佩玉腰金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366742_comment'></div>实惧在梁之刺。<div id='poem_sentence_29_1366742_comment'></div>无任荷戴屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1366742_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年3月</a>　此月，正书独孤及撰《韦缜碑》，立在京兆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年5月24日</a>　此日，参与尚书省试制举人，列朝邑尉李郱为拔萃科上等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年7月11日</a>　此日，改元广德，加阶金紫光禄大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年8月27日</a>　此日，除江陵尹、兼御史大夫，充荆南节度、观察处置使。有谢表。作品：《谢荆南节度使表》<div id='poem_1366748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366748' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366748'>臣真卿言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366748_comment'></div>伏奉二十七日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366748_comment'></div>除臣江陵尹兼御史大夫充荆南节度观察处置使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366748_comment'></div>宠命自天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366748_comment'></div>战荷无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366748_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366748_comment'></div>窃以荆南巨镇。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年</a>　举内侄殷亮为推官，未行，受代。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年10月</a>　代宗幸陕，扈从至行在，除尚书右丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年11月</a>　月初，正书父惟贞、母殷夫人赠告。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=763&endYear=763')">763年12月19日</a>　此日，车驾发陕州，扈从还京，建议先谒陵庙，然后还宫，为宰相元载所阻，不从。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年1月5日</a>　此日，除检校刑部尚书、兼御史大夫，充朔方行营汾晋等六州宣慰使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年1月</a>　后三日敕命前往。未行，留知省事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年3月</a>　本月，晋封鲁郡开国公，食邑三千户。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年7月5日</a>　此日，临淮郡王李光弼因痢疾卒于徐州王府，年五十八。颜真卿撰神道碑。作品：《唐故开府仪同三司太尉兼侍中河南副元帅都督河南淮南淮西荆南山南东道五节度行营事东都留守上柱国赠太保临淮武穆王李公（光弼）神道碑铭》<div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366834'>昔宗周之中兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366834_comment'></div>时则有若方叔召虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366834_comment'></div>总师干<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1366834", 1366834, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>肇敏</span>之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366834_comment'></div>南威蛮荆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366834_comment'></div>东截淮浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366834_comment'></div>以左右宣王。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1366834_comment'></div>我皇唐之反正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366834_comment'></div>时则有若临淮汾阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366834_comment'></div>秉文武忠义之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366834_comment'></div>廓清河朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366834_comment'></div>保乂王室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366834_comment'></div>翼戴三圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366834_comment'></div>天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366834_comment'></div>谓之<span id='poem_sentence_16_1366834_comment'></div>今古一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366834_comment'></div>公讳光弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366834_comment'></div>京兆万年人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366834_comment'></div>曾祖皇左威卫大将军幽州经略军副使府君讳令节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366834_comment'></div>祖鸿胪卿兼檀州刺史府君讳重英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366834_comment'></div>父云麾将军左领左羽林二军大将军朔方节度副使蓟郡开国公赠幽州都督司空讳楷洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366834_comment'></div>皆以英果沈勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366834_comment'></div>秋八月拜户部尚书同中书门下平章事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366834_comment'></div>史思明既有河北之地。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1366834_comment'></div>暨弟光炎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1366834_comment'></div>并不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1366834_comment'></div>次曰光颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1366834_comment'></div>特进鸿胪卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1366834_comment'></div>皆以将略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1366834_comment'></div>见称时辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1366834_comment'></div>季曰光进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1366834_comment'></div>开府仪同三司太子太保兼御史大夫渭北节度使凉国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1366834_comment'></div>清识表微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1366834_comment'></div>沈谋绝众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1366834_comment'></div>刚亦不吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1366834_comment'></div>柔而能立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1366834_comment'></div>与公并时仗钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1366834_comment'></div>分阃□□淩霄翼圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1366834_comment'></div>既有戴天之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1366834_comment'></div>华原统师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1366834_comment'></div>独闻禁暴之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1366834_comment'></div>方当会同正至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1366834_comment'></div>荣曜君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1366834_comment'></div>入侍黼帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1366834_comment'></div>峨二貂乎泰阶之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1366834_comment'></div>归联䌽服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1366834_comment'></div>顿双节于高堂之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1366834_comment'></div>斯欢未剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1366834_comment'></div>遗恨何居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1366834_comment'></div>昔斛律丞相与弟并州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1366834_comment'></div>同务烈于北齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1366834_comment'></div>贺拔行台与兄雍州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1366834_comment'></div>亦宣力于西魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1366834_comment'></div>咸称义烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1366834_comment'></div>各懋勋庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1366834_comment'></div>而风树寂寞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1366834_comment'></div>偏隅隘狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1366834_comment'></div>比之我族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1366834_comment'></div>事则不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1366834_comment'></div>真卿昔守平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1366834_comment'></div>困于凶羯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1366834_comment'></div>繄公莅止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_400_1366834_comment'></div>获保馀生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_401_1366834_comment'></div>束带兴居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_402_1366834_comment'></div>空想北平之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_403_1366834_comment'></div>操觚论撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_404_1366834_comment'></div>敢坠中郎之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_405_1366834_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_406_1366834_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_407_1366834'>羯胡猖狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_407_1366834_comment'></div>俶扰皇纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_408_1366834_comment'></div>降生临淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1366834_comment'></div>佐我兴王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1366834_comment'></div>惟此临淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1366834_comment'></div>万夫之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1366834_comment'></div>爰初发迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1366834_comment'></div>罔或弗臧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1366834_comment'></div>出入忠孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1366834_comment'></div>人伦激昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1366834_comment'></div>其心铁石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1366834_comment'></div>其行圭璋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1366834_comment'></div>天宝末造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1366834_comment'></div>河朔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_420_1366834", 1366834, "Clauses/420/Comments/0")'>恇攘</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1366834_comment'></div>天子命公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1366834_comment'></div>经营朔方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1366834_comment'></div>沙河嘉山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1366834_comment'></div>我伐用张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1366834_comment'></div>思明归节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1366834_comment'></div>禄山震惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1366834_comment'></div>潼关勿帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_427_1366834_comment'></div>丑虏其亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_428_1366834_comment'></div>肃宗有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_429_1366834_comment'></div>大卤于襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_430_1366834_comment'></div>应变如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_431_1366834_comment'></div>凶徒靡亢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_432_1366834_comment'></div>介圭入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_433_1366834_comment'></div>台座用光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_434_1366834_comment'></div>俾公东征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_435_1366834_comment'></div>北国是皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_436_1366834_comment'></div>长围邺下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_437_1366834_comment'></div>望入河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_438_1366834_comment'></div>擒斩渠魁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_439_1366834_comment'></div>霆击龙骧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_440_1366834_comment'></div>淮濆镇定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_441_1366834_comment'></div>徐土翱翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_442_1366834_comment'></div>服田蠖屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_443_1366834_comment'></div>料玚鹰扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_444_1366834_comment'></div>不有神算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_445_1366834_comment'></div>畴戡暴强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_446_1366834_comment'></div>弟兄同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_447_1366834_comment'></div>秉钺煌煌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_448_1366834_comment'></div>方期凯旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_449_1366834_comment'></div>双映旗常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_450_1366834_comment'></div>晨趋法座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_451_1366834_comment'></div>夕庆高堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_452_1366834_comment'></div>如何不辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_453_1366834_comment'></div>愆此不祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_454_1366834_comment'></div>素輀反葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_455_1366834_comment'></div>白骥跼箱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_456_1366834_comment'></div>箫鼓悲鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_457_1366834_comment'></div>羽仪分行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_458_1366834_comment'></div>万乘致祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_459_1366834_comment'></div>千官送丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_460_1366834_comment'></div>生荣死哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_461_1366834_comment'></div>身殁名扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_462_1366834_comment'></div>渭水川上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_463_1366834_comment'></div>坛山路旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_464_1366834_comment'></div>唯馀丰碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_465_1366834_comment'></div>突兀连冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_466_1366834_comment'></div>往来必拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_467_1366834_comment'></div>万古沾裳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_468_1366834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年11月14日</a>　汾阳郡王郭子仪自泾阳来朝，诏宰臣百僚迎之于开远门，并在安福寺举行兴道之会。右仆射郭英乂谄事军容使鱼朝恩，礼遇高于六部尚书，颜真卿会后即作书纠正之。作品：《与郭仆射书》<div id='poem_1366760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与郭仆射书</a><span class='authorDate'>（764年11月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366760")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366760'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366760'>十一月日。金紫光禄大夫检校刑部尚书上柱国鲁郡开国公颜真卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366760_comment'></div>谨奉书于右仆射定襄郡王郭公阁下。盖太上有立德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366760_comment'></div>其次有立功。是之谓不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366760_comment'></div>抑又闻之。端揆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366760_comment'></div>百寮之师长。诸侯王者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366760_comment'></div>人臣之极地。今仆射挺不朽之功业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366760_comment'></div>当人臣之极地。岂不以才为世出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366760_comment'></div>功冠一时。挫思明跋扈之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366760_comment'></div>抗回纥无厌之请。故得身画淩烟之阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366760_comment'></div>名藏太室之廷。吁足畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366760_comment'></div>然美则美矣。而终之始难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366760_comment'></div>故曰满而不溢。所以长守富也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366760_comment'></div>高而不危。所以长守贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366760_comment'></div>可不儆惧乎。书曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366760_comment'></div>尔惟弗矜。天下莫与汝争功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366760_comment'></div>尔惟不伐。天下莫与汝争能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366760_comment'></div>以齐桓公之盛业。片言勤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366760_comment'></div>则九合诸侯。一匡天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366760_comment'></div>葵邱之会。微有振矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366760_comment'></div>而叛者九国。故曰行百里者半九十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366760_comment'></div>言晚节末路之难也。从古至今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366760_comment'></div>暨我高祖太宗已来。未有行此而不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366760_comment'></div>废此而不乱者也。前者菩提寺行香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366760_comment'></div>仆射指麾宰相与两省台省已下常参官并为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1366760", 1366760, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>一行</span>坐。鱼开府及仆射率诸军将为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1366760", 1366760, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>一行</span>坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366760_comment'></div>若一时从权。亦犹未可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366760_comment'></div>何况积习更行之乎。一昨以郭令公以父子之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366760_comment'></div>破犬羊凶逆之众。众情忻喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366760_comment'></div>恨不顶而戴之。是用有兴道之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366760_comment'></div>仆射又不悟前失。竟率意而指麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366760_comment'></div>不顾班秩之高下。不论文武之左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366760_comment'></div>苟以取悦军容为心。曾不顾百寮之侧目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366760_comment'></div>亦何异清昼攫金之士哉。甚非谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366760_comment'></div>君子爱人以礼。不闻姑息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366760_comment'></div>仆射得不深念之乎。真卿窃闻军容之为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366760_comment'></div>清修梵行。深入佛海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366760_comment'></div>况乎收东京有殄贼之业。守陕城有戴天之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366760_comment'></div>朝野之人。所共景仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366760_comment'></div>岂独有分于仆射哉。加以利衰涂割。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366760_comment'></div>恬然于心。固不以一毁加怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366760_comment'></div>一敬加喜。尚何半席之座咫尺之地能汨其志哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366760_comment'></div>且乡里上齿。宗庙上爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366760_comment'></div>朝廷上位。皆有等威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366760_comment'></div>以明长幼。故得彝伦叙而天下和平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366760_comment'></div>且上自宰相御史大夫两省五品已上供奉官自为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1366760", 1366760, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>一行</span>。十二卫大将军次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366760_comment'></div>三师三公令仆少师保傅尚书左右丞侍郎自为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1366760", 1366760, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>一行</span>。九卿三监对之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366760_comment'></div>从古以然。未尝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1366760", 1366760, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>参错</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366760_comment'></div>至如节度军将。各有本班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366760_comment'></div>卿监有卿监之班。将军有将军之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366760_comment'></div>纵是开府特进。并是勋官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366760_comment'></div>用荫即有高卑。会宴合依伦叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366760_comment'></div>岂可裂冠毁冕。反易彝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366760_comment'></div>贵者为卑所淩。尊者为贱所偪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366760_comment'></div>一至于此。振古未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366760_comment'></div>如鱼军容阶虽开府。官即监门将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366760_comment'></div>朝廷列位。自有次序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366760_comment'></div>但以功绩既高。恩泽莫二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366760_comment'></div>出入王命。众人不敢为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366760_comment'></div>不可令居本位。须别示有尊崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366760_comment'></div>只可于宰相师保座南。横安一位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366760_comment'></div>如御史台众尊知杂事御史。别置一榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366760_comment'></div>使百寮共得瞻仰。不亦可乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366760_comment'></div>圣皇时。开府高力士承恩传宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366760_comment'></div>亦只如此横座。亦不闻别有礼数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366760_comment'></div>亦何必令他失位。如李辅国倚承恩泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366760_comment'></div>径居左右仆射及三公之上。令天下疑怪乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366760_comment'></div>古人云。益者三友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366760_comment'></div>损者三友。愿仆射与军容为直谅之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366760_comment'></div>不愿仆射为军容佞柔之友。又一昨裴仆射误欲令左右丞勾当尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366760_comment'></div>当时辄有詶对。仆射恃贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366760_comment'></div>张目见尤。介众之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366760_comment'></div>不欲显过。今者兴道之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366760_comment'></div>还尔遂非。再猲八座尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366760_comment'></div>欲令便向下座。州县军城之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366760_comment'></div>亦恐未然。朝廷公宴之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366760_comment'></div>不应若此。今既若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366760_comment'></div>仆射意只应以为尚书之与仆射。若州佐之与县令乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366760_comment'></div>若以尚书同于县令。则仆射见尚书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366760_comment'></div>得如上佐事刺史乎。益不然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366760_comment'></div>今既三厅齐列。足明不同刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366760_comment'></div>且尚书令与仆射。同是二品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366760_comment'></div>只校上下之阶。六曹尚书并正三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366760_comment'></div>又非隔品致敬之类。尚书之事仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366760_comment'></div>礼数未敢有失。仆射之顾尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366760_comment'></div>何乃欲同卑吏。又据宋书百官志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366760_comment'></div>八座同是第三品。隋及国家始升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366760_comment'></div>别作二品。高自标致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366760_comment'></div>诚则尊崇。向下挤排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366760_comment'></div>无乃伤甚。况再于公堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366760_comment'></div>猲咄常伯。当为令公初到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366760_comment'></div>不欲纷披。僶俛就命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366760_comment'></div>亦非理屈。朝廷纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366760_comment'></div>须共存立。过尔隳坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366760_comment'></div>亦恐及身。明天子忽震电含怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366760_comment'></div>责斁彝伦之人。则仆射其将何辞以对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366760_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_94_1366760_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=764&endYear=764')">764年11月</a>　不数日，又为郭子仪父郭敬之撰书颂述之。作品：《郭氏家庙碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年1月</a>　正月，正除刑部尚书。会诏赠韦陟尚书左仆射，太常博士程皓议谥“忠孝”，颜真卿以为忠孝不并立，拟之过高.主客员外郎归崇敬又驳之。郭英乂请从太常状奏之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年8月</a>　仲秋日，因孙宿兄弟之请，为其座师太子詹事孙逖文集作序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年10月</a>　月初，弟太子中允允臧除江陵少尹，又兼侍御史、荆南行军司马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年10月21日</a>　此日，六嫂幼舆夫人殷氏卒于江陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=765&endYear=765')">765年</a>　在长安为赵良弼撰写碑文。作品：《赵良弼碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　颜真卿上疏切谏，甚得人心，遭元载之恨，以诽谤时政罪被陷害。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　在京日，撰并书乃祖显甫碑。作品：《唐赠华州刺史颜显甫碑》<div id='poem_1366824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故通议大夫行嶭王友柱国赠秘书少监国子祭酒太子少保颜君碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366824")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366824'>昔孔悝有彝鼎之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366824_comment'></div>陆机有祠堂之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366824_comment'></div>皆所以发挥祖德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366824_comment'></div>敷演家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366824_comment'></div>故君子之观其铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366824_comment'></div>既美其所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366824_comment'></div>又美其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366824_comment'></div>无而称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366824_comment'></div>是诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366824_comment'></div>有而不述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366824_comment'></div>岂仁乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366824_comment'></div>论而撰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366824_comment'></div>敢不祗惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366824_comment'></div>君讳惟贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366824_comment'></div>字叔坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366824_comment'></div>其先出于颛顼之孙祝融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366824_comment'></div>融孙安为曹姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366824_comment'></div>其裔邾武公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366824_comment'></div>名夷甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366824_comment'></div>字颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366824_comment'></div>子友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366824_comment'></div>别封郳为小邾子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366824_comment'></div>遂以颜为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366824_comment'></div>多仕鲁为卿大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366824_comment'></div>孔门达者七十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366824_comment'></div>颜氏有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366824_comment'></div>战国有率斶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366824_comment'></div>秦有芝贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366824_comment'></div>汉有异肆安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366824_comment'></div>其后丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366824_comment'></div>谱牒沦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366824_comment'></div>魏有斐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366824_comment'></div>盛字叔台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366824_comment'></div>青徐二州刺史关内侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366824_comment'></div>始自鲁居于琅琊临沂孝悌里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366824_comment'></div>生广陵太守给事中葛绎贞子讳钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366824_comment'></div>字公若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366824_comment'></div>精韩诗礼易尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366824_comment'></div>学者宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366824_comment'></div>生汝阴太守护军袭葛绎子讳默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366824_comment'></div>字静伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366824_comment'></div>生晋侍中光禄大夫西平靖侯讳含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366824_comment'></div>字宏都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366824_comment'></div>随元帝过江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366824_comment'></div>巳下七叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366824_comment'></div>葬在上元幕府山西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366824_comment'></div>生侍中光禄勋西平定侯讳髦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366824_comment'></div>字君道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366824_comment'></div>事具孝行传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366824_comment'></div>生州西曹骑都尉西平侯讳綝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366824_comment'></div>字文和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366824_comment'></div>生宣城太守御史中丞讳靖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366824_comment'></div>字茂宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366824_comment'></div>生巴陵太守度支校尉讳腾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366824_comment'></div>字宏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366824_comment'></div>善草隶书有风格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366824_comment'></div>梁武帝草书评云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366824_comment'></div>颜腾之贺道力并便尺牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366824_comment'></div>少行于代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366824_comment'></div>生辅国江夏王参军讳炳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366824_comment'></div>字叔豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366824_comment'></div>以能书称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366824_comment'></div>生齐持书御史兼中丞讳见远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366824_comment'></div>字见远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366824_comment'></div>和帝被弑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366824_comment'></div>一恸而绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366824_comment'></div>梁武深恨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366824_comment'></div>事见梁周北齐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366824_comment'></div>生梁镇西记室参军讳协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366824_comment'></div>字子和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366824_comment'></div>感家门事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366824_comment'></div>义不求闻达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366824_comment'></div>元帝著怀旧诗以伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366824_comment'></div>撰晋仙传五篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366824_comment'></div>日月灾异图两卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366824_comment'></div>文集二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366824_comment'></div>见梁书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366824_comment'></div>生北齐给事黄门侍郎待诏文林馆平原太守隋东宫学士讳之推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366824_comment'></div>字介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366824_comment'></div>著家训二十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366824_comment'></div>冤魂志三卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366824_comment'></div>證俗字音五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366824_comment'></div>文集三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366824_comment'></div>事具本传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366824_comment'></div>黄门兄之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366824_comment'></div>周御正御史中大夫麟趾学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366824_comment'></div>隋文辅政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366824_comment'></div>不署矫诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366824_comment'></div>索玺又拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366824_comment'></div>出为集州刺史新野公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366824_comment'></div>后朝朔望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366824_comment'></div>引之御榻曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366824_comment'></div>见危授命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366824_comment'></div>临大节而不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366824_comment'></div>古人所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366824_comment'></div>何以加卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366824_comment'></div>事具周书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366824_comment'></div>弟之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366824_comment'></div>隋叶令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366824_comment'></div>子孙见于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366824_comment'></div>黄门生皇秦王记室讳思鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366824_comment'></div>悯楚游秦小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366824_comment'></div>记室字孔归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366824_comment'></div>君之曾祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366824_comment'></div>隋司经校书东宫学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366824_comment'></div>率子弟奉迎义旗于长春宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366824_comment'></div>招瓜州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366824_comment'></div>拜仪同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366824_comment'></div>博学善属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366824_comment'></div>自为父集序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366824_comment'></div>国史称温大雅在隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366824_comment'></div>与思鲁同事东宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366824_comment'></div>彦博与悯楚同直内史省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366824_comment'></div>彦将时与游秦同典校秘阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366824_comment'></div>二家兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366824_comment'></div>各为一时人物之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366824_comment'></div>少时学业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366824_comment'></div>颜氏为优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366824_comment'></div>其后职位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366824_comment'></div>温氏为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366824_comment'></div>温氏谱亦载焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366824_comment'></div>生勤礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366824_comment'></div>字敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366824_comment'></div>君之祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366824_comment'></div>幼而朗悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366824_comment'></div>识量宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366824_comment'></div>工于篆籀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366824_comment'></div>尤精诂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366824_comment'></div>解褐校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366824_comment'></div>与两兄弟师古相时同时为宏文崇贤学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366824_comment'></div>弟育德又于司经校定经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366824_comment'></div>当代荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366824_comment'></div>太宗尝令师古赞崇贤学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366824_comment'></div>以兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366824_comment'></div>特命萧钧赞之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366824_comment'></div>依仁服义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366824_comment'></div>怀文守一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366824_comment'></div>履道自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366824_comment'></div>下帷终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366824_comment'></div>德彰素里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366824_comment'></div>行成兰室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366824_comment'></div>鹤钥驰誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366824_comment'></div>龙楼委质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366824_comment'></div>著作郎修国史夔府长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366824_comment'></div>赠虢州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366824_comment'></div>生昭甫敬仲殆庶无恤少连务滋辟强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366824_comment'></div>昭甫字周卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366824_comment'></div>君之父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366824_comment'></div>幼而颖悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366824_comment'></div>尤明诂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366824_comment'></div>工篆籀草隶书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366824_comment'></div>与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_151_1366824", 1366824, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>内弟</span>殷仲容齐名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366824_comment'></div>而劲利过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366824_comment'></div>特为伯父师古所赏重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366824_comment'></div>每有著述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366824_comment'></div>必令参定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366824_comment'></div>尝得古鼎二十馀字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366824_comment'></div>举朝莫识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366824_comment'></div>尽能读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366824_comment'></div>高宗侍读曹王属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366824_comment'></div>赠华州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366824_comment'></div>真卿表谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366824_comment'></div>肃宗批答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366824_comment'></div>卿之乃祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366824_comment'></div>当为硕儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366824_comment'></div>既高倚相之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366824_comment'></div>遂有臧孙之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366824_comment'></div>不坠其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366824_comment'></div>在卿之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366824_comment'></div>生我伯父讳元孙暨君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366824_comment'></div>伯父聪颖绝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366824_comment'></div>尤工文翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1366824_comment'></div>愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1366824_comment'></div>长厚清白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1366824_comment'></div>朝邑尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1366824_comment'></div>頵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1366824_comment'></div>左率仓曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1366824_comment'></div>硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1366824_comment'></div>秘书正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1366824_comment'></div>颒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1366824_comment'></div>有吏干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1366824_comment'></div>歙州录事参军曲阜男。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1366824_comment'></div>䪻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1366824_comment'></div>好为诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1366824_comment'></div>富阳尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1366824_comment'></div>禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1366824_comment'></div>好为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1366824_comment'></div>常州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1366824_comment'></div>并粗有所立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1366824_comment'></div>君之诸祖父群从。<div id='poem_sentence_496_1366824_comment'></div>以清白称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_497_1366824_comment'></div>其馀咸著官族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_498_1366824_comment'></div>不获悉数。<div id='poem_sentence_501_1366824_comment'></div>巴陵记室之书翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_502_1366824_comment'></div>特进黄门之文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_503_1366824_comment'></div>秘监华州之学识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_504_1366824_comment'></div>肇自鲁国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_505_1366824_comment'></div>格于圣代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_506_1366824_comment'></div>纷纶盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_507_1366824_comment'></div>遂举集于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_508_1366824_comment'></div>君能述遵前人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_509_1366824_comment'></div>不敢失坠其志事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_510_1366824_comment'></div>以忝聿修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_511_1366824_comment'></div>宜其克飨尊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_512_1366824_comment'></div>为清庙不祧之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_513_1366824_comment'></div>真卿幸承遗训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_514_1366824_comment'></div>叨受国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_515_1366824_comment'></div>既受无疆之庥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_516_1366824_comment'></div>敢扬不朽之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_517_1366824_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_518_1366824_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_519_1366824'>系我宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_519_1366824_comment'></div>邾颜公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_520_1366824_comment'></div>子封郳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_521_1366824_comment'></div>鲁附庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_522_1366824_comment'></div>亚孔圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_523_1366824_comment'></div>浴沂风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_524_1366824_comment'></div>刺青徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_525_1366824_comment'></div>给事中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_526_1366824_comment'></div>护营柳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_527_1366824_comment'></div>渡江枫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_528_1366824_comment'></div>侍兄疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_529_1366824_comment'></div>感蛇童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_530_1366824_comment'></div>邻火断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_531_1366824_comment'></div>珥貂重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_532_1366824_comment'></div>施七叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_533_1366824_comment'></div>传孝恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_534_1366824_comment'></div>武骑都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_535_1366824_comment'></div>尉司从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_536_1366824_comment'></div>便尺牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_537_1366824_comment'></div>继鱼虫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_538_1366824_comment'></div>恸君难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_539_1366824_comment'></div>愤而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_540_1366824_comment'></div>咨记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_541_1366824_comment'></div>游湘东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_542_1366824_comment'></div>嗟御正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_543_1366824_comment'></div>凛移忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_544_1366824_comment'></div>暨黄门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_545_1366824_comment'></div>擅文雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_546_1366824_comment'></div>三韶长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_547_1366824_comment'></div>事东宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_548_1366824_comment'></div>四穆叔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_549_1366824_comment'></div>史牢笼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_550_1366824_comment'></div>褒华州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_551_1366824_comment'></div>诂训通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_552_1366824_comment'></div>小秘监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_553_1366824_comment'></div>盛名鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_554_1366824_comment'></div>维少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_555_1366824_comment'></div>文翰工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_556_1366824_comment'></div>莅畿赤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_557_1366824_comment'></div>五褒崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_558_1366824_comment'></div>登望苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_559_1366824_comment'></div>友桂丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_560_1366824_comment'></div>三超赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_561_1366824_comment'></div>保储宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_562_1366824_comment'></div>流光盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_563_1366824_comment'></div>庙貌融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_564_1366824_comment'></div>永不祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_565_1366824_comment'></div>垂无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_566_1366824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年2月9日</a>　此日，出贬峡州别驾。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='493b4692129e47ec9ecf0e6586372025_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("493b4692129e47ec9ecf0e6586372025");'><span id='493b4692129e47ec9ecf0e6586372025_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>，58岁</div><div id='493b4692129e47ec9ecf0e6586372025' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　旬余改吉州别驾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年2月</a>　本月上旬，应故旧康没野波之请，为其父康阿义屈达干撰写神道碑铭。作品：《康阿义屈达干碑》<div id='poem_1366836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>特进行左金吾卫大将军上柱国清河郡开国公赠开府仪同三司兼夏州都督康公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366836")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366836'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366836'>竭诚奉主之谓忠。率义忘躬之谓勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366836_comment'></div>忠勇不犯。则名登于明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366836_comment'></div>子仕教忠之谓义。战阵能勇之谓孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366836_comment'></div>孝慈有裕。则道存乎方册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366836_comment'></div>兼此四者。其惟清河公之族乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366836_comment'></div>公讳阿义屈达干。姓康氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366836_comment'></div>柳城人。其先世为北蕃十二姓之贵种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366836_comment'></div>曾祖颉利部落都督。祖染可汗驸马都知兵马使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366836_comment'></div>父颉利发墨啜可汗卫衙官知部落都督。皆有功烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366836_comment'></div>称于北陲。公即衙官之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366836_comment'></div>正直忠鲠。以信行闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366836_comment'></div>为国人所敬。长于谋略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366836_comment'></div>工骑射。其弓十钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366836_comment'></div>年二十三。为阿史那颉佚施默啜等九可汗宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366836_comment'></div>秉心颛一。立言无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366836_comment'></div>不吐刚以茹柔。必蹈道而履义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366836_comment'></div>可汗每有过失。未尝不极言切谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366836_comment'></div>蕃落中重焉。以比国家之丞相宋璟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366836_comment'></div>初默啜弟拔悉密时勤尝擎药弑可汗。公窃而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366836_comment'></div>密持示默啜。默啜大怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366836_comment'></div>将诛之。公以为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366836_comment'></div>但令归于部落。默啜知公至忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366836_comment'></div>繇是益加亲信。同列四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366836_comment'></div>莫与公比。其后公以孤直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366836_comment'></div>屡见疑谮。遂请退归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366836_comment'></div>可汗察公非罪。寻复追为宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366836_comment'></div>先是毗伽可汗小杀。为其大臣梅录啜所毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366836_comment'></div>小杀觉之。尽灭其党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366836_comment'></div>既卒。国人立其子伊然可汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366836_comment'></div>无何病卒。又立其弟登利可汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366836_comment'></div>华言登利。犹果报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366836_comment'></div>其母暾欲谷之女。与其小臣饫斯达干预国政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366836_comment'></div>登利从叔父因左杀右杀。东西分掌其兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366836_comment'></div>登利与其母诱斩西杀。尽并其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366836_comment'></div>左杀惧及。乃攻杀登利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366836_comment'></div>自立为乌苏米施可汗。拔悉密击败之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366836_comment'></div>脱身遁走。国中大乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366836_comment'></div>天宝元年。公与四男及西杀妻子默啜之孙勃德支特勒毗伽可汗女大洛公主伊然可汗小妻余塞匐登利可汗女余烛公主及阿布思阿史德等部落五千馀帐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366836_comment'></div>并驼马羊牛二十馀万。款塞归朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366836_comment'></div>朔方节度使王忠嗣具以上闻。秋八月至京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366836_comment'></div>玄宗俾先谒太庙。仍于殿庭引见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366836_comment'></div>御花萼楼以宴之。仍赋诗用纪其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366836_comment'></div>拜公左威卫中郎将。属范阳节度使安禄山潜怀异图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366836_comment'></div>庶为已用。密奏公充部落都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366836_comment'></div>仍为其先锋使。公既不得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366836_comment'></div>僶俛从之。四载以破契丹功迁右威卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366836_comment'></div>俄拜范阳经略副使。五载又破契丹功居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366836_comment'></div>拜左武卫大将军。仍充节度副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366836_comment'></div>玄宗嘉之。玺书慰勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366836_comment'></div>盈溢箧笥。十四载冬十一月九日甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366836_comment'></div>安禄山反范阳。公以天子有命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366836_comment'></div>陷身凶逆。举家见质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366836_comment'></div>自拔莫由。既至东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366836_comment'></div>公泣血吁天。次于梦寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366836_comment'></div>欲与诸子逃归国家。为贼邢州刺史康节所告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366836_comment'></div>遂被收系。傔奏被诛者二十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366836_comment'></div>公之四子。各奔于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366836_comment'></div>贼恐众情不安。贳之而后出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366836_comment'></div>至德二载。阖门二百馀口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366836_comment'></div>被安庆绪胁至安阳。属今上为天下兵马元帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366836_comment'></div>统今尚书令汾阳王郭子仪朔方之师。诸节度回纥之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366836_comment'></div>东收二京。公率四子及孙侄等十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366836_comment'></div>冒死南奔。至汲郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366836_comment'></div>为从者所告。家人歼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366836_comment'></div>二子殁野波英俊挺身行前。二子屈须弥施英玉持满殿后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366836_comment'></div>殁野波妻阿史那氏为公控马。登于西山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366836_comment'></div>至高平界。遇贼蔡希德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366836_comment'></div>以精骑三百遮路邀击。殁野波英俊策马奔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366836_comment'></div>杀四十馀人。生擒四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366836_comment'></div>冬十有一月七日。投今上行营至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366836_comment'></div>先帝闻而嘉之。欲以开府仪同三司处公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366836_comment'></div>仍加实封。公固辞乃受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366836_comment'></div>因以为金吾大将军。加特进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366836_comment'></div>增封清河郡开国公。食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366836_comment'></div>策勋<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙十二字）</span>卫大将军□□卿□□□射□□□□开府仪同三司太常卿殿前衙前射生兵马俄加上柱国姑臧县开国子殁野波云麾将军左金吾卫大将军上柱国射生散骑常侍骠骑大将军左武卫大将军兼鸿胪卿上柱国殿前射生使清河郡开国公英俊等官秩各有差。因留公及屈须弥施英玉供奉射生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366836_comment'></div>以殁野波英俊勇冠三军。并令东随故太尉李光弼于太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366836_comment'></div>后邺郡瓦窑阵官军与安庆绪相逼。王思礼为其所败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366836_comment'></div>贼势既盛。太尉与思礼相顾气索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366836_comment'></div>殁野波英俊勃然奋怒。遂直抵薄河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366836_comment'></div>当锋击之。杀获二千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366836_comment'></div>贼众方退。太尉诸公睹而骇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366836_comment'></div>赏杂䌽百匹。并以转分麾下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366836_comment'></div>一无所纳。三军欣羡焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366836_comment'></div>殁野波居常谦谨。临事勇锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366836_comment'></div>战则先锋。前无强敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366836_comment'></div>捉生游奕。所向必摧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366836_comment'></div>九节度之围安阳也。史思明悉众来救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366836_comment'></div>殁野波以十五骑过河逆击之。并马刺倒者数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366836_comment'></div>生擒数十人。后击怀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366836_comment'></div>思明又自来救。䀜爽之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366836_comment'></div>侵轶柴篱。殁野波领甲骑三十御之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366836_comment'></div>贼军三千人。一时摧败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366836_comment'></div>真卿之弃平原也。殁野波为贼骑将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366836_comment'></div>缓策不追。及闻渡河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366836_comment'></div>然始奔蹑。是以得脱于难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366836_comment'></div>平原人至今称之。英俊瞪视眈眈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366836_comment'></div>姿气雄果。发劲矢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366836_comment'></div>持大枪。嶷然万众之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366836_comment'></div>左右驰突。无不辟易而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366836_comment'></div>尝随太尉讨思明于河阳。贼骁骑万馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366836_comment'></div>于中阐城索斗将。莫敢应者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366836_comment'></div>英俊挺身奔击之。应枪落者二十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366836_comment'></div>英俊被枪刺颊。贯喉而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366836_comment'></div>摆首而去之。犹杀二人而还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366836_comment'></div>太尉壮焉。遂以从父兄子妻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366836_comment'></div>故天下之言勇者。以殁野波英俊兄弟为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366836_comment'></div>广德元年。上幸陕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366836_comment'></div>公之诸子皆当扈从。公以体貌瑰硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366836_comment'></div>难于举动。方与之死诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366836_comment'></div>殁野波妻为公介马。扶奔华州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366836_comment'></div>公虑不免。谓左右曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366836_comment'></div>我若为贼所得。无累我儿子乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366836_comment'></div>汝曹何不杀我。众人感惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366836_comment'></div>叫然皆哭。遂竭力舁公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366836_comment'></div>至于行在。上深嗟赏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366836_comment'></div>方极尊荣。以终宴喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366836_comment'></div>上天不惠。以二年青龙甲辰冬十有一月二十日甲寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366836_comment'></div>感肺疾薨于上都胜业坊之私第。春秋七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366836_comment'></div>亲事左右。莫不剺面截耳以哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366836_comment'></div>初淩霄之难。公实援立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366836_comment'></div>浐水之屯。公亲总统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366836_comment'></div>上之反正。父子从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366836_comment'></div>帝畴厥功。遂有开府仪同三司兼夏州都督之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366836_comment'></div>夫人清河郡太夫人交河石氏。左卫中郎将珍之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366836_comment'></div>左金吾卫大将军三奴之女。温敏淑惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366836_comment'></div>柔明端雅。有女师母仪之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366836_comment'></div>克懋于家。不幸遘疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366836_comment'></div>以天宝十五载春三月八日。先公而薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366836_comment'></div>永泰元年春二月十日壬申。与公合祔于万年县之长乐原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366836_comment'></div>礼也。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366836_comment'></div>公以沈果之姿。抗英威之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366836_comment'></div>降精昴宿。炳粹天街。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366836_comment'></div>忠肃表于生知。义勇形于造次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366836_comment'></div>属国家多难。沦胥以痡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366836_comment'></div>壮一心而来事我君。贯四时而不改柯叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366836_comment'></div>义方恳到。相携于契阔之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366836_comment'></div>臣节激昂。三见于危亡之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366836_comment'></div>天子感焉。既受腹心之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366836_comment'></div>禁旅资焉。俱列爪牙之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366836_comment'></div>勋庸克茂。声问攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366836_comment'></div>丛䌽衣于玉帐之前。罗五戟于一门之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366836_comment'></div>不其盛矣。昔萧相国举宗佐命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366836_comment'></div>金日磾七叶珥貂。望古俦今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366836_comment'></div>可谓同德。其孤等穷人孺慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366836_comment'></div>靡所寘哀。聿求不腆之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366836_comment'></div>庶播无疆之美。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366836_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_146_1366836'>北方之强欤。十有二姓强哉矫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366836_comment'></div>部落之雄者。康执兵柄缅乎眇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366836_comment'></div>特进诞生兮。实登邦政德不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366836_comment'></div>暾女灭国兮。乌苏不竟愠群小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366836_comment'></div>三滨九死兮。举族致命丹心皦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366836_comment'></div>一门万石兮。彰厥诚敬皇恩暸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366836_comment'></div>生为忠臣兮。后有馀庆其不夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366836_comment'></div>家有孝子兮。严亲翊圣王之爪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366836_comment'></div>乃立丰碑兮。百代遗咏鸿名表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366836_comment'></div>忠孝之际兮。于斯为盛远图窅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366836_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_156_1366836_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='de3c11be136d49ae9a6b71532804eb18_label'><a
