ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年11月14日</a>　此日，迁伯父元孙夫妇柩归葬长安祖茔，并撰书志述之。作品：《颜元孙碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　又有与夫人帖。作品：《与夫人帖》<div id='poem_1366776' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366776' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366776?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与夫人帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（772年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366776")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366776_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366776'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366776'>真卿顿首。奉承十四日迁厝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366776_comment'></div>承问悲慕。不能自胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366776_comment'></div>惟攀慕不及。摧毁何堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366776_comment'></div>痛当柰何。痛当柰何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366776_comment'></div>凝寒。惟动静支适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366776_comment'></div>儿子等保侍真卿。离官已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366776_comment'></div>事须十间前至郑州。汴州已来专奉侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366776_comment'></div>一日只拟一驿。计过大事后发犹恐迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366776_comment'></div>必望知此缓急。勿迟滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366776_comment'></div>足下不来。义无独去之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366776_comment'></div>必请矜此狼狈。所望今到汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366776_comment'></div>水下不愁河冻。书祭器等先下船去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366776_comment'></div>真卿十一日且发东京。伫望早来早来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366776_comment'></div>谨不次。真卿顿首夫人阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366776_comment'></div>十一月八日。问讯颂翙蒙郎郎和奴光严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366776_comment'></div>深远忆。或至十三日得发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366776_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1366776_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年11月26日</a>　起家为湖州刺史，十一月二十六日，撰书。作品：《元结墓表》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='aa3fecd36335446c8335e6e073a3f9fe_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa3fecd36335446c8335e6e073a3f9fe");'><span id='aa3fecd36335446c8335e6e073a3f9fe_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=783')">777-783年</a>，69-75岁</div><div id='aa3fecd36335446c8335e6e073a3f9fe' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年8月25日</a>　此日，除刑部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年11月20日</a>　有献所著《韵海镜源》三百六十卷，诏藏于集贤书院及秘阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年11月24日</a>　此日，友婿杭州刺史杜济自常州归葬万年县，撰书神道碑及墓志颂述之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=778&endYear=778')">778年1月15日</a>　此日，三上表乞许致仕，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=778&endYear=778')">778年2月</a>　本月，充使谒拜昭陵，过瑶台寺，有诗志其事。作品：《使瑶台寺有怀圆寂上人》<div id='poem_51063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/51063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>使过瑶台寺有怀圆寂上人</a><span class='authorDate'>（778年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_51063")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_51063_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_51063'>并序：真卿昔以天宝元年尉醴泉，亟过瑶台寺圆寂上人院。秩满，迁监察御史，巡覆诸陵，而上人已去此寺（而上人已离此寺）。大历十三年春二月，以刑部尚书谒拜昭陵，慨然有怀。</div><div id='poem_preface_51063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_51063'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_51063'>上人居此寺，不出三十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_51063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_51063'>万法元无著<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作灵法尽无染）</span>，一心唯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_51063", 51063, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>趣禅</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_51063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_51063'>忽纡尘外轸，远访区中<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作世间）</span>缘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_51063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_51063'>及尔不复见，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_51063", 51063, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>支提</span>犹岌<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作岿）</span>然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_51063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_51063'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_51063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=778&endYear=778')">778年</a>　奉敕正书杨绾《李抱玉碑》，立在长安县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=778&endYear=778')">778年3月</a>　本月，改为吏部尚书。撰书以志其立碑始末。作品：《宋璟碑侧记》<div id='poem_1366803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故太尉广平文贞公宋公神道碑侧记</a><span class='authorDate'>（778年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366803")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366803'>初公任监察御史。持服于沙河县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366803_comment'></div>属突厥寇赵定州。河朔凶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366803_comment'></div>邢州刺史黄文轨投艰于公。公以父母之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366803_comment'></div>金革无避。及贼至城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366803_comment'></div>公为晓陈祸福。其徒有素闻公威名者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366803_comment'></div>乃相率而去之。开元末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366803_comment'></div>安西都护赵含章冒于货贿。多以金帛赂遗朝廷之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366803_comment'></div>九品以上。悉皆有名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366803_comment'></div>其后节度范阳。事方发觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366803_comment'></div>有司具以上闻。玄宗切责名品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366803_comment'></div>将加黜削。公一无所受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366803_comment'></div>乃进谏焉。玄宗纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366803_comment'></div>遂御花萼楼。一切释放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366803_comment'></div>举朝皆谢。公衣冠俨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366803_comment'></div>独立不拜。翌日入奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366803_comment'></div>玄宗谓公曰。古人以清白遗子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366803_comment'></div>乃卿一人而已。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366803_comment'></div>含章之贿。偶不至臣门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366803_comment'></div>非不受也。玄宗深嘉叹之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366803_comment'></div>前碑阙焉。故略述于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366803_comment'></div>公第三子浑之为中丞也。方欲陈乞御制碑颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366803_comment'></div>未果而中受谴责。旋羯胡作乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366803_comment'></div>事竟不成。真卿时忝监察殿中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366803_comment'></div>为中丞属吏。故公孙俨泣请真卿论撰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366803_comment'></div>昭义军节度观察使尚书左仆射兼御史大夫平阳郡王嶭公曰嵩。以文武忠义之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366803_comment'></div>为国保障。上慕公之德业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366803_comment'></div>叹尚无穷。次嘉俨之恳诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366803_comment'></div>崇竖莫致。乃命屯田郎中权邢州刺史封演。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366803_comment'></div>购他山之石。曳以百牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366803_comment'></div>僝刻字之工。成乎半岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366803_comment'></div>磨砻既毕。建立斯崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366803_comment'></div>远近嗟称。古今荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366803_comment'></div>虽大贤为德。树善庸限于存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366803_comment'></div>而小子何知。附骥托迹于阶序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366803_comment'></div>真卿刺湖州之日。因成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366803_comment'></div>请俨刻其侧而志之。未及雕镌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366803_comment'></div>而第六子衡。因谪居沙州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366803_comment'></div>参佐戎幕。河陇失守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366803_comment'></div>介于吐蕃。以功累拜工部郎中兼御史河西节度行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366803_comment'></div>与节度周鼎保守燉煌。仅十馀岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366803_comment'></div>遂有中丞常侍之拜。恩命未达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366803_comment'></div>而吐蕃围城。兵尽矢穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366803_comment'></div>为贼所陷。吐蕃素闻太尉名德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366803_comment'></div>曰。唐天子我之舅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366803_comment'></div>衡之父。舅贤相也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366803_comment'></div>落魄如此。岂可留乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366803_comment'></div>遂赠以驼马。送还于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366803_comment'></div>大历十二年十一月。以二百骑尽室护归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366803_comment'></div>士君子伟之。乃古来所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366803_comment'></div>上欲特加超奖。且命待制于侧门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366803_comment'></div>十三年春三月。吏部尚书颜真卿记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366803_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_51_1366803_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年5月12日</a>　此日，以吏部尚书充礼仪使，处置山陵事。闰五月，上奏，从之。作品：《请除禫服奏》《请除素练听政奏》<div id='poem_1366750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请除禫服奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（779年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366750")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366750'>哀号在疚。开辟所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366750_comment'></div>诚恳尚违。庶僚增惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366750_comment'></div>伏见百辟。并已释除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366750_comment'></div>事既合权。礼无独异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366750_comment'></div>不可以吉凶兼制。臣子殊仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366750_comment'></div>伏乞奉顾命之文。节因心之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366750_comment'></div>顺时即吉。屈已临朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366750_comment'></div>则万姓心安。四方事集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366750_comment'></div>臣典司仪注。不敢轻移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366750_comment'></div>冒犯宸严。无任恳迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366750_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1366750_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1366751' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366751' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366751?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请除素练听政奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（779年5月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366751")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366751_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366751'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366751'>孝德动天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366751_comment'></div>事踰前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366751_comment'></div>德音俯降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366751_comment'></div>感咽载深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366751_comment'></div>臣伏守遗诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366751_comment'></div>礼从易月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366751_comment'></div>祥禫变除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366751_comment'></div>仪注皆备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366751_comment'></div>若陛下未忍即吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366751_comment'></div>更服练巾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366751_comment'></div>则遗诏不得奉行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366751_comment'></div>群僚无以觐见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366751_comment'></div>伏乞俯顺人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366751_comment'></div>仰遵先旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366751_comment'></div>实大孝不亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366751_comment'></div>万方幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366751_comment'></div>臣职在典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366751_comment'></div>愚守如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366751_comment'></div>无任恳迫之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1366751_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年6月</a>　本月，正书程浩《马璘新庙碑》，韩秀实隶书题额，立于京兆马氏新庙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年7月</a>　本月，上状请取初谥为定。作品：《请复七圣谥号状》<div id='poem_1366753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请复七圣谥号状</a><span class='authorDate'>（779年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366753")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366753'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366753'>谨按礼记曰。先王谥以尊名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366753_comment'></div>节以一惠。故行出于己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366753_comment'></div>而名生于人。使夫善者劝而恶者惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366753_comment'></div>而虞夏之质。殷周之文至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366753_comment'></div>而禹汤文武之君。咸以一字为谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366753_comment'></div>言文则不称武。言武则不称文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366753_comment'></div>岂圣德所不优乎。盖群臣称其至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366753_comment'></div>是以子不得议父。臣不得议君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366753_comment'></div>天子崩。则臣下制谥于南郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366753_comment'></div>明受之于天也。诸侯薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366753_comment'></div>则太子赴告于天子。明受之于君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366753_comment'></div>至于周室卑。大朴散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366753_comment'></div>谥始以两字为重。人或以虚美为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366753_comment'></div>汉承战国馀烈。参而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366753_comment'></div>君臣易名。事归至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366753_comment'></div>少不以为贬。多不以为褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366753_comment'></div>虽美众所归。可一言而尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366753_comment'></div>魏晋以降。盖不足徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366753_comment'></div>圣唐钦明。宪章周汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366753_comment'></div>爰初创业。顺考古道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366753_comment'></div>高祖谥大武。用汉制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366753_comment'></div>太宗谥曰文。行周道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366753_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1366753", 1366753, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>名正理顺</span>。垂之无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366753_comment'></div>上元中。政在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1366753", 1366753, "Clauses/47/Comments/0")'>宫壸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366753_comment'></div>乱名改作。始建神尧文武大圣之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366753_comment'></div>盖非高宗之所获已。暨元宗之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366753_comment'></div>奸臣窃柄。析言而乱旧法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366753_comment'></div>轻议以改鸿名。遂广累圣之谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366753_comment'></div>有加至十一字者。皇帝则悉有大圣之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366753_comment'></div>皇后则皆有顺圣之名。使言之者惑于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366753_comment'></div>行之者异于古。非旧制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366753_comment'></div>其后剑门下罪已之诏。叙高祖以下累圣悉用旧谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366753_comment'></div>则元宗悔既往之失。亦已明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366753_comment'></div>宝应中。二圣山陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366753_comment'></div>有司请谥。事不师古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366753_comment'></div>变而行权。去古质而尚浮华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366753_comment'></div>舍旧名而广新谥。谓一名不足以节惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366753_comment'></div>乃十倍于古焉。而累圣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1366753", 1366753, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>谥名</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366753_comment'></div>悉以字多者为定。是废高祖太宗之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366753_comment'></div>岂曰爱君。今制谥非古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366753_comment'></div>人皆知之。有司因循其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366753_comment'></div>而无敢言者。假使当今守之而不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366753_comment'></div>后人议之以为非。然所失岂不大哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366753_comment'></div>何者。臣子之于君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366753_comment'></div>莫不欲广其美称。先王制礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366753_comment'></div>不敢过也。故至敬无文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366753_comment'></div>至文尚质。质之数极于一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366753_comment'></div>尧舜之美。足以彰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366753_comment'></div>文之数极于二。孝文孝景之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366753_comment'></div>亦已明矣。质则近古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366753_comment'></div>文则近今。此高祖太宗所以更用其法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366753_comment'></div>后王所宜守之法也。非天下之至圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366753_comment'></div>其孰能定之。此天皇所以兴圣主而正鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366753_comment'></div>太宗所以待孝孙而修废典。微臣所以守经义而崇圣朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366753_comment'></div>陛下宜奉天心。继先太宗之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366753_comment'></div>使子孙蒙其法。而万代守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366753_comment'></div>此天下之能事也。臣愚以为高祖以下累圣谥号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366753_comment'></div>悉宜取初谥为定。谨按旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366753_comment'></div>宜上高祖为武皇帝。太宗为文皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366753_comment'></div>高宗为天皇大帝。中宗为孝和皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366753_comment'></div>睿宗为圣真皇帝。其二圣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1366753", 1366753, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>谥名</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366753_comment'></div>字数太广。有逾古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366753_comment'></div>臣愚请择其美称而正之。谨按谥法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366753_comment'></div>秉德不回曰孝。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1366753", 1366753, "Clauses/127/Comments/0")'>照临</span>四方曰明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366753_comment'></div>宜上玄宗为孝明皇帝。又按谥法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366753_comment'></div>圣善周闻曰宣。宜上肃宗为孝宣皇帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366753_comment'></div>仍准汉魏及国朝故事。于尚书省议定奏御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366753_comment'></div>夫文敝则救之以质。至敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366753_comment'></div>名惑而反之于正。至明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366753_comment'></div>祖作之而孙述之。至孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366753_comment'></div>三者备矣。然后能立天下之大本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366753_comment'></div>正天下之大名。建天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1366753", 1366753, "Clauses/143/Comments/0")'>大业</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366753_comment'></div>能事毕矣。伏惟皇帝陛下详择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366753_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_73_1366753_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年9月</a>　本月，上《亲陵异于诸陵状》，请元陵上食异于泰陵、建陵，以遵远近之制。从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年10月</a>　本月，代宗神主将祔，上《论元皇帝祧迁状》，请迁元皇帝于西夹室，以准礼合祔。从之。<div id='poem_1366754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论元皇帝祧迁状</a><span class='authorDate'>（779年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366754")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366754'>王制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366754_comment'></div>天子七庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366754_comment'></div>三昭三穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366754_comment'></div>与太祖之庙而七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366754_comment'></div>又礼器云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366754_comment'></div>有以多为贵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366754_comment'></div>天子七庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366754_comment'></div>又伊尹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366754_comment'></div>七世之庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366754_comment'></div>可以观德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366754_comment'></div>此经典之明證也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366754_comment'></div>七庙之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366754_comment'></div>则曰去祧为坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366754_comment'></div>去坛为墠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366754_comment'></div>故历代儒者制<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>迭毁</span>之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366754_comment'></div>皆亲尽宜毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366754_comment'></div>伏以太宗文皇帝七代之祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366754_comment'></div>高祖神尧皇帝国朝首祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366754_comment'></div>万叶所承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366754_comment'></div>太祖景皇帝受命于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366754_comment'></div>始封于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366754_comment'></div>元本皆在不毁之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366754_comment'></div>代祖元皇帝地非开统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366754_comment'></div>亲在七庙之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366754_comment'></div>代宗皇帝升祔有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366754_comment'></div>元皇帝神主礼合<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>祧迁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366754_comment'></div>或议者以祖宗之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366754_comment'></div>难于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>迭毁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366754_comment'></div>昔汉朝近古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366754_comment'></div>不敢以私灭公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366754_comment'></div>故前汉十二帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366754_comment'></div>为祖宗者四而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366754_comment'></div>至后汉渐违经意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366754_comment'></div>子孙以推美为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366754_comment'></div>自光武已下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366754_comment'></div>皆有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>庙号</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366754_comment'></div>则祖宗之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366754_comment'></div>莫不建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366754_comment'></div>安帝信谗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366754_comment'></div>害大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366754_comment'></div>废太子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366754_comment'></div>及崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366754_comment'></div>无上宗之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366754_comment'></div>后自建武以来无毁者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366754_comment'></div>因以陵号称宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366754_comment'></div>至桓帝失德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366754_comment'></div>尚有宗号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366754_comment'></div>故初平中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366754_comment'></div>左中郎蔡邕以和帝以下功德无殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366754_comment'></div>而有过差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366754_comment'></div>不应为宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366754_comment'></div>及馀非宗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366754_comment'></div>追尊三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366754_comment'></div>皆奏毁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366754_comment'></div>是知祖有功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366754_comment'></div>宗有德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366754_comment'></div>存至公之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366754_comment'></div>非其人不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366754_comment'></div>盖三代立礼之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366754_comment'></div>自东汉已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366754_comment'></div>则此道丧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366754_comment'></div>魏明帝自称烈祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366754_comment'></div>论者以为逆自称祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366754_comment'></div>故近代此名悉为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>庙号</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366754_comment'></div>未有子孙践祚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366754_comment'></div>而不祖宗先王者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366754_comment'></div>以此明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366754_comment'></div>则不得独据两字而为不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>祧迁</span>之證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366754_comment'></div>假令传祚百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366754_comment'></div>岂可上崇百代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366754_comment'></div>以为孝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366754_comment'></div>请依三昭三穆之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366754_comment'></div>永为通典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366754_comment'></div>宝应二年升祔玄宗肃宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366754_comment'></div>则献祖懿祖已从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_74_1366754", 1366754, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>迭毁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366754_comment'></div>伏以代宗睿文孝皇帝卒哭而祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366754_comment'></div>则合上迁一室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366754_comment'></div>元皇帝代数已远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366754_comment'></div>其神主准礼当祧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366754_comment'></div>至禘祫之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366754_comment'></div>然后飨祀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_80_1366754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年</a>　有《元陵注》一卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年</a>　撰书曾祖《颜勤礼碑》，追立于万年先茔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年</a>　赠和州刺史张敬因碑，立于许州墓左。作品：《赠和州刺史张敬因碑》<div id='poem_1366820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晋侍中右光禄大夫本州大中正西平靖侯颜公大宗碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366820")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366820'>公讳含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366820_comment'></div>字宏都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366820_comment'></div>琅琊临沂人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366820_comment'></div>其先出于邾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366820_comment'></div>颜公子友封于郳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366820_comment'></div>是为小邾子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366820_comment'></div>为鲁附庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366820_comment'></div>居于邹邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366820_comment'></div>因以命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366820_comment'></div>孔门达者八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366820_comment'></div>曰路回辛骄祖哙仆何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366820_comment'></div>次有丁阖叔子率躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366820_comment'></div>秦有芝贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366820_comment'></div>汉有肆异安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366820_comment'></div>魏有斐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366820_comment'></div>盛字叔台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366820_comment'></div>青徐二州刺史关内侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366820_comment'></div>始自鲁居琅琊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366820_comment'></div>代传恭孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366820_comment'></div>故号所居为孝悌里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366820_comment'></div>生钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366820_comment'></div>字公若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366820_comment'></div>明韩诗礼易尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366820_comment'></div>多所通说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366820_comment'></div>学者宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366820_comment'></div>历大中大夫东莞广陵太守葛绎贞子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366820_comment'></div>生默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366820_comment'></div>字静伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366820_comment'></div>晋汝阴太守护军将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366820_comment'></div>生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366820_comment'></div>少有操行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366820_comment'></div>以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366820_comment'></div>兄畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366820_comment'></div>咸宁中死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366820_comment'></div>托梦当复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366820_comment'></div>发棺而气息甚微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366820_comment'></div>阖家营视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366820_comment'></div>母妻不能无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366820_comment'></div>公乃绝弃人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366820_comment'></div>躬亲侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366820_comment'></div>足不出户者十有三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366820_comment'></div>次嫂樊氏失明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366820_comment'></div>须髯蛇胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366820_comment'></div>寻求不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366820_comment'></div>忽有青衣童子持囊授公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366820_comment'></div>乃蛇胆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366820_comment'></div>寻出户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366820_comment'></div>化成青鸟飞去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366820_comment'></div>东海王越以为太傅参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366820_comment'></div>元帝过江。<div id='poem_sentence_51_1366820_comment'></div>公以儒素笃行补太子中庶子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366820_comment'></div>迁黄门侍郎本州大中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366820_comment'></div>封西平县侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366820_comment'></div>拜侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366820_comment'></div>除吴郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366820_comment'></div>公所历简而有恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366820_comment'></div>明而能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366820_comment'></div>然以威风御下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366820_comment'></div>王导叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366820_comment'></div>颜公在事。<div id='poem_sentence_63_1366820_comment'></div>复为侍中国子祭酒光禄勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366820_comment'></div>以年老逊位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366820_comment'></div>成帝美其素行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366820_comment'></div>就加右光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366820_comment'></div>门施行马。<div id='poem_sentence_70_1366820_comment'></div>固辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366820_comment'></div>时论者欲为王导降礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366820_comment'></div>冯怀以问于公。<div id='poem_sentence_75_1366820_comment'></div>向冯祖思问佞于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366820_comment'></div>我有邪德乎。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366820_comment'></div>非圣不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366820_comment'></div>众咸服焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366820_comment'></div>郭璞尝欲为公筮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366820_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366820_comment'></div>自有性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366820_comment'></div>无劳蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366820_comment'></div>桓温求婚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366820_comment'></div>以其盛满不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366820_comment'></div>因诫子孙曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366820_comment'></div>自今任官不可过二千石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366820_comment'></div>婚姻勿贪世家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366820_comment'></div>或问群士优劣。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366820_comment'></div>卞望之之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366820_comment'></div>馀则吾不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366820_comment'></div>致仕二十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366820_comment'></div>年九十二薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366820_comment'></div>谥曰靖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_590_1366820_comment'></div>庶竭罔极之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_591_1366820_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_592_1366820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_593_1366820'>铄吾祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_593_1366820_comment'></div>渡江浦。<div id='poem_sentence_601_1366820_comment'></div>謺规矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_602_1366820_comment'></div>毣鸾皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_603_1366820_comment'></div>炳龙虎。<div id='poem_sentence_616_1366820_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年</a>　奏请改诸州博士为文学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=779&endYear=779')">779年</a>　奏请停“千秋”之节。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年3月1日</a>　此日，因东都高祖、太宗、高宗三庙木主多忘缺未袝，上表请造之以袝。诏下，议而不决，乃罢。是议至宣宗朝遂行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年</a>　于敦化坊高祖颜思鲁故宅建颜氏家庙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年6月</a>　本月，在长安撰颜氏家庙碑以志之。作品：《颜氏家庙碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年10月</a>　本月，又撰书铭石立于庙前。作品：《碑后记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年10月</a>　本月，又撰书铭石立于庙前。集贤院学士李阳冰为之篆额。作品：《碑额阴记》<div id='poem_1366802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞御书题额恩敕批答碑阴记</a><span class='authorDate'>（780年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1366802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366802'>肃宗皇帝恩许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366802_comment'></div>既有斯答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366802_comment'></div>御劄垂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366802_comment'></div>而真卿以疏拙蒙谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366802_comment'></div>粤若来八月既望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366802_comment'></div>贬授蓬州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366802_comment'></div>暨今上即位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366802_comment'></div>宝应元年夏五月拜利州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366802_comment'></div>属羌贼围城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366802_comment'></div>不得入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366802_comment'></div>恩敕追赴上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366802_comment'></div>为今尚书前相国彭城公刘公晏所让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366802_comment'></div>授尚书户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366802_comment'></div>二年春三月改吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366802_comment'></div>广德元年秋八月拜江陵尹兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366802_comment'></div>充荆南节度观察处置等使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366802_comment'></div>未行受代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366802_comment'></div>转尚书右丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366802_comment'></div>以招谕太师中书令仆固怀恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366802_comment'></div>不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366802_comment'></div>遂知府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366802_comment'></div>永泰二年春二月贬峡州别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366802_comment'></div>旬馀移贬吉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366802_comment'></div>大历三年夏五月蒙除抚州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366802_comment'></div>六年闰三月代到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366802_comment'></div>秋八月至上元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366802_comment'></div>尔来十有六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366802_comment'></div>困于疏愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366802_comment'></div>累蒙窜谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366802_comment'></div>其所置碑石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366802_comment'></div>迄今委诸岩麓之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366802_comment'></div>未遑崇树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366802_comment'></div>七年秋九月归自东京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366802_comment'></div>起家蒙除湖州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366802_comment'></div>来年春正月至任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366802_comment'></div>州东有苕霅两溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366802_comment'></div>溪左有放生池焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366802_comment'></div>即我宝应元圣文武皇帝所置也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366802_comment'></div>州西有白鹤山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366802_comment'></div>山多乐石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366802_comment'></div>于是采而斲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366802_comment'></div>命吏干磨砻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366802_comment'></div>家僮镌刻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366802_comment'></div>建于州之骆驼桥东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366802_comment'></div>盖以抒臣下追远之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366802_comment'></div>昭先帝生成之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366802_comment'></div>额既未立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366802_comment'></div>追思莫达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366802_comment'></div>客或请先帝所赐敕书批答中诸事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366802_comment'></div>以缉而勒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366802_comment'></div>真卿从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366802_comment'></div>勒愿斯毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366802_comment'></div>瞻慕不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366802_comment'></div>遂志诸碑阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366802_comment'></div>庶乎乾象昭回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366802_comment'></div>与宇宙而终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366802_comment'></div>天文焕发。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年8月22日</a>　此日，除太子少师，仍充礼仪使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=780&endYear=780')">780年12月2日</a>　此日，奉敕与博士及光禄卿李涵诸人详定公主、郡县主出降仪，改初唐以来，公主下降，舅姑皆降礼答拜之陋习。有奏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年9月</a>　本月，上《庙享议》，请以晋蔡谟等议为定。从之。<div id='poem_1366755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1366755'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366755'>议者或云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366755_comment'></div>献祖懿祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366755_comment'></div>亲远庙迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366755_comment'></div>不当祫享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366755_comment'></div>宜永閟于西夹室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366755_comment'></div>又议者云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366755_comment'></div>二祖宜同祫享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366755_comment'></div>与太祖并列昭穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366755_comment'></div>而空太祖东向之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366755_comment'></div>又议者云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366755_comment'></div>二祖若同祫享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366755_comment'></div>即太祖之位永不得正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366755_comment'></div>宜奉迁二祖神主祔藏于德明皇帝庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366755_comment'></div>臣伏以三议俱未为允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366755_comment'></div>且礼经残缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366755_comment'></div>既无明据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366755_comment'></div>儒者能比方义类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366755_comment'></div>斟酌取中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366755_comment'></div>则可举而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366755_comment'></div>盖叶于正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366755_comment'></div>伏惟太祖景皇帝以受命始封之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366755_comment'></div>处百代不迁之庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366755_comment'></div>配天崇享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366755_comment'></div>是极尊严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366755_comment'></div>且至禘祫之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366755_comment'></div>暂居昭穆之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366755_comment'></div>屈已伸孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366755_comment'></div>敬奉祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366755_comment'></div>缘<span id='poem_sentence_40_1366755_comment'></div>行祫祭之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366755_comment'></div>夫祫合也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366755_comment'></div>故公羊传曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366755_comment'></div>大事者何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366755_comment'></div>祫也。<div class='inline' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>　在长安有文。作品：《朝会有故去乐议》<div id='poem_1366756' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366756' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366756?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝会有故去乐议</a><span class='authorDate'>（781年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1366756'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366756'>周礼大司乐职云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366756_comment'></div>诸侯薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366756_comment'></div>令去乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366756_comment'></div>大臣死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366756_comment'></div>令弛悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366756_comment'></div>郑注云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366756_comment'></div>去谓藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366756_comment'></div>弛谓释下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366756_comment'></div>是知哀轻者则释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366756_comment'></div>哀重者则藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366756_comment'></div>又按庾蔚之礼论云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366756_comment'></div>晋元后秋崩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366756_comment'></div>武帝咸宁元年享万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366756_comment'></div>不设乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366756_comment'></div>永嘉元年冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366756_comment'></div>惠帝三年丧制未终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366756_comment'></div>司徒左长史江统议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366756_comment'></div>二年正会不宜作乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366756_comment'></div>又章皇后哀限未终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366756_comment'></div>后主已入庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366756_comment'></div>博士徐乾议曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366756_comment'></div>周景王有后嫡子之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366756_comment'></div>既葬除服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366756_comment'></div>叔向犹议其宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366756_comment'></div>今不宜悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366756_comment'></div>宋书礼志云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366756_comment'></div>晋武帝已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366756_comment'></div>国有大丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366756_comment'></div>废乐三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366756_comment'></div>又按江都集礼说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366756_comment'></div>晋博士孔恢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366756_comment'></div>朝廷遏密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366756_comment'></div>悬而不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366756_comment'></div>恢以为宜都去悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366756_comment'></div>设乐为作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366756_comment'></div>不作则不宜悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366756_comment'></div>孟献子禫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366756_comment'></div>悬而不乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366756_comment'></div>自是应作耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366756_comment'></div>故夫子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366756_comment'></div>献子加于人一等矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366756_comment'></div>非谓不应作而犹悬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366756_comment'></div>国丧尚近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366756_comment'></div>谓金石不可陈于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366756_comment'></div>又徐广晋史曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366756_comment'></div>闻乐不怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366756_comment'></div>故申情于遏密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366756_comment'></div>谅闇夺服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366756_comment'></div>虑政事之荒废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366756_comment'></div>是故秉权通以变常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366756_comment'></div>量轻重以降差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366756_comment'></div>臣以周礼去乐之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366756_comment'></div>宋志终丧之證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366756_comment'></div>徐广之论宁戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366756_comment'></div>孔恢之说禫悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366756_comment'></div>理既可凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366756_comment'></div>事又故实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366756_comment'></div>伏请三年未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366756_comment'></div>都不设悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366756_comment'></div>如有齐衰丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366756_comment'></div>及遇大臣薨殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366756_comment'></div>则量轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366756_comment'></div>悬而不作。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1366756_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=781&endYear=781')">781年</a>　本年，正书李舟《王密德政碑》，李阳冰篆额，徐浩书敕书，十月立在明州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=782')">782年闰1月25日</a>　此日，上奏，请每至释奠，奏轩悬之乐。敕所司施行。作品：《请定武成庙释奠奏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=782')">782年8月27日</a>　德宗以姻亲，将委以相位，为权臣所忌。此日，改太子太师。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=782')">782年</a>　太师任上，委门人左辅元编集《礼乐集》，凡十卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=782')">782年</a>　正书李华《元德秀墓碣》，李阳冰篆额。明年秋日，立于河南伊阳。时人以墓主、文章、书法、篆额并四绝，号《四绝碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=782&endYear=782')">782年3月5日</a>　此日，从兄颜杲卿加赠司徒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年1月17日</a>　此日，奉命赴许州宣慰李希烈。诏下，举朝失色。永平等军节度都统、检校司徒、平章事李勉闻之，密表请留。又遣使追截于途，未果。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b3771a680b2848b79f146069df579d3d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b3771a680b2848b79f146069df579d3d");'><span id='b3771a680b2848b79f146069df579d3d_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年10月21日</a>　此日，赴饶州途中，道出东京，有文祭告于伯父颜元孙墓前。作品：《祭伯父文》<div id='poem_1366849' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366849' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366849?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭伯父豪州刺史文</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年10月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366849")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366849_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366849'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366849'>维乾元元年岁次戊戌十月庚子朔廿一日庚申。第十三侄男银青光禄大夫使持节饶州诸军事饶州刺史上轻车都尉丹阳县开国侯真卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366849_comment'></div>敢昭告于亡伯故朝议大夫豪州刺史府君之灵曰。日者羯胡禄山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366849_comment'></div>侵扰河洛。生灵涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366849_comment'></div>兵甲靡夷。二兄杲卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366849_comment'></div>任常山郡太守。忠义愤发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366849_comment'></div>首开土门。擒斩逆竖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366849_comment'></div>挫其凶慝。先盖授卫尉卿兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366849_comment'></div>城孤援绝。身陷贼庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366849_comment'></div>圣朝哀荣。褒赠太子太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366849_comment'></div>甥侄八人。季明卢逖等被贼害者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366849_comment'></div>并赠五品京官。嫂及儿女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366849_comment'></div>皆被<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1366849", 1366849, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>拘囚</span>。睿略昭宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366849_comment'></div>宇宙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1366849", 1366849, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>清廓</span>。脱于贼手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366849_comment'></div>并得归京。真卿比在平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366849_comment'></div>遭罹凶逆。与杲卿同心协德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366849_comment'></div>亦著微诚。二圣悯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366849_comment'></div>授户部侍郎河北采访招讨使。又迁工部宪部二尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366849_comment'></div>再兼御史大夫。出为同蒲饶三州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366849_comment'></div>圣恩锡类。大父赠华州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366849_comment'></div>兄弟儿侄。尽蒙国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366849_comment'></div>允南授膳部郎中。允臧授侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366849_comment'></div>威明试太仆丞。頍受太子洗马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366849_comment'></div>顶授协律郎。颎授秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366849_comment'></div>至东京得申拜扫。又方远辞违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366849_comment'></div>伏增感咽。谨以清酌庶羞之奠。<div class='inline' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　本年返京途经洛阳，为洛阳令李构撰文。作品：《李侍御写真赞》<div id='poem_1366809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　本年，洛下偶逢书僧怀素，相与论书，甚见款洽。且为之撰写序称述之。作品：《怀素上人草书歌行序》<div id='poem_1366786' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366786' class='poemTitle href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366786")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366786_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366786'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366786'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1366786", 1366786, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>开士</span>怀素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366786_comment'></div>僧中之英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366786_comment'></div>气概通疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366786_comment'></div>性灵豁畅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366786_comment'></div>精心草圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366786_comment'></div>积有岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366786_comment'></div>江岭之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366786_comment'></div>其名大著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366786_comment'></div>故吏部尚书韦公陟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366786_comment'></div>睹其笔力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366786_comment'></div>勖以有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366786_comment'></div>今礼部侍郎张公谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366786_comment'></div>赏其不羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366786_comment'></div>引共游处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366786_comment'></div>兼好事者同作歌以赞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366786_comment'></div>动盈卷轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366786_comment'></div>夫草稿之作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366786_comment'></div>起于汉代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366786_comment'></div>杜度崔瑗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366786_comment'></div>始以妙闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366786_comment'></div>迨乎伯英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366786_comment'></div>尤擅其美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366786_comment'></div>羲献兹降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366786_comment'></div>虞陆相承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366786_comment'></div>口诀手授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366786_comment'></div>以至于吴郡张旭长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366786_comment'></div>虽姿性颠逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366786_comment'></div>超绝古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366786_comment'></div>而楷法精详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366786_comment'></div>特为真正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366786_comment'></div>某早岁尝接游居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366786_comment'></div>屡蒙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1366786", 1366786, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>激劝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366786_comment'></div>告以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1366786", 1366786, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>笔法</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366786_comment'></div>资质劣弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366786_comment'></div>又婴物务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366786_comment'></div>不能恳习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366786_comment'></div>迄用无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366786_comment'></div>追思一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366786_comment'></div>何可复得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366786_comment'></div>忽见师作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366786_comment'></div>纵横不群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366786_comment'></div>迅疾骇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366786_comment'></div>若还旧观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366786_comment'></div>向使师得亲承善诱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366786_comment'></div>亟揖规模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366786_comment'></div>则入室之宾。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　次洛阳，追立伯母殷履直夫人颜真定碑碣于万安山王宝原。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='29d535afca644767a5d01a9e83b6ab02_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>　至洛阳，东都留守兼河南尹郑叔则劝留，未允，毅然赴许州。<br /></div>

-----title
定边（朔方）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='41ba28c5f2564935b643c28f76a9e288_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("41ba28c5f2564935b643c28f76a9e288");'><span id='41ba28c5f2564935b643c28f76a9e288_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=749')">747-749年</a>，39-41岁</div><div id='41ba28c5f2564935b643c28f76a9e288' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　至五原郡理冤狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　长子颇约生于本年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=747&endYear=747')">747年</a>　结交于鲜于仲通。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年8月</a>　八月仲秋，以监察御史充河西、陇右军试复屯交兵使。岑参作诗壮行之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=748&endYear=748')">748年</a>　结识鲁炅于陇右节度使哥舒翰座上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=749&endYear=749')">749年</a>　春日，再以监察御史充河东、朔方军试复屯交兵使。使河东时，劾奏郑氏兄弟母亡二十九年未葬失礼。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
平原
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b8882ce96c5b45ac82be5c06478908bc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b8882ce96c5b45ac82be5c06478908bc");'><span id='b8882ce96c5b45ac82be5c06478908bc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=755')">753-755年</a>，45-47岁</div><div id='b8882ce96c5b45ac82be5c06478908bc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=753&endYear=753')">753年6月</a>　本年春，有诏补尚书省郎官十余人出守州牧，颜真卿为平原郡太守。六月赴任，岑参有诗为壮行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　至郡，与郡人封绍、高筼及族弟颜浑等人始修《韵海镜源》条目。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　季冬，河北采访使、东平王安禄山判官殿中侍御史平冽，监察御史阎宽、李史鱼，右金吾胄曹宋謇巡按至郡，颜真卿迎之于境，相与狎游安德县东北之东方朔庙，见其开元八年原刺史韩思复所立画赞碑，磨损不堪，于是援翰重书，复刊于石，并撰碑阴记志之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=754&endYear=754')">754年</a>　荐引处士张镐，入为左拾遗，凡三年，位至宰相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　颜真卿知其节度安禄山必反，初夏即遣亲客蹇昂奏状，状留禁中不报。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年12月</a>　本月上旬，颜真卿因安禄山反，河朔尽陷，遂遣本郡司兵李平乘驷间道驰报。尝得封常清书并募捕逆贼牒散发河北诸郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年12月</a>　颜真卿先是预备战事，范阳反后，即招募勇士，以为讨逆贼之计。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年12月18日</a>　至此日，执杀安禄山来使段子光，会清池尉贾载、盐山尉穆宁共斩伪署景城太守刘道玄，传首平原。颜真卿即召贾载、穆宁及清河尉张澹诣郡计事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年12月18日</a>　是时，饶阳太守卢全诚、济南太守李随、清河长史王怀忠、景城司马李暐、邺郡太守王焘及河间法李奂各以众归，共推颜真卿为盟主，军事皆禀焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　有诏北海太守贺兰进明率精锐五千济河为助。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=755&endYear=755')">755年</a>　颜真卿令外甥卢逖赴常山郡联络太守堂兄颜杲卿。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
河北
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c2a68975a59e4e8a95346ff4503ed64c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c2a68975a59e4e8a95346ff4503ed64c");'><span id='c2a68975a59e4e8a95346ff4503ed64c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>，48岁</div><div id='c2a68975a59e4e8a95346ff4503ed64c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年1月15日</a>　此日，颜真卿因守城拜户部侍郎，兼本郡防御使，即以景城长史李晖为副使，李铣、贾载、沈震为判官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年3月29日</a>　此日，又加河北采访处置使，乃以王延昌为判官，张澹为支使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　始结交魏郡太守河北采访使李光弼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年3月</a>　三月间，清河客李萼为郡人乞师于颜真卿。颜真卿结纳李萼意见，联结清河郡，并以平原、清河、博平三郡之兵收复魏郡。由是军声大振。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　让堂邑之功于贺兰进明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　是时，平卢游弈使刘正臣将谋范阳举旗反正，颜真卿遣判官贾载越海遗军资十余万，以子颇为质信，坚其意志。王玄志、田神功、董秦、侯希逸、李正己、许杲卿等将并偕刘正臣归顺于平原。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　初，颜真卿闻河北节度使李光弼出井陉，即敛军还平原，以待光弼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　闻郭子仪、李光弼引兵西入井陉，真卿始复区处河北军事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年6月27日</a>　潼关失守，驾幸蜀郡，颜真卿命脚力人张云子间道上表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　后又遣招讨判官李铣相继赴行在，潜至灵武。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年7月12日</a>　此日，皇太子李亨即位，尊玄宗为上皇，改元至德。颜真卿即散布诸郡宣奉，并上《皇帝即位贺上皇表》<div id='poem_1366739' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366739' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366739?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝即位贺上皇表</a><span class='authorDate'>（756年7月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a id='poem_sentence_1_1366739_comment'></div>伏承贼陷潼关。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366739_comment'></div>驾幸蜀郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366739_comment'></div>李光弼郭子仪等正围博陵郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366739_comment'></div>臣不胜悲愤之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366739_comment'></div>遂遣脚力人张云子间道上表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366739_comment'></div>犹恐不达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366739_comment'></div>又差招讨判官信都郡武邑县主簿李铣相继间行。<div class='inline' 1366739, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>上皇</span>天帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366739_comment'></div>臣及官吏僧道耆寿百姓等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366739_comment'></div>蹈舞抃跃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366739_comment'></div>不胜感咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366739_comment'></div>其张云子回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366739_comment'></div>皇帝授臣工部尚书兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366739_comment'></div>其李铣回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366739_comment'></div>又授臣银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366739_comment'></div>顾以庸微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366739_comment'></div>频叨宠命。<div
