class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366739_comment'></div>苍生贾勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366739_comment'></div>丰镐河洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366739_comment'></div>指期可平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366739_comment'></div>伏愿陛下垂拱颐神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366739_comment'></div>以睹廓清之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366739_comment'></div>臣官守有限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366739_comment'></div>不获随例阙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366739_comment'></div>无任恳款悲恋之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1366739_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年7月12日</a>　行牒招李萼以求赡济之略。先是李萼因颜真卿让功于贺兰进明而辞去。至是，复诣平原，为之谋集军资。有文。作品：《访求清河行人李华（萼）牒》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年</a>　撰有《修书帖》<div id='poem_1366782' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366782' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366782?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修书帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（756年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366782")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366782_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366782'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366782'>贼军未平。使仆不愤见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366782_comment'></div>故先修书。但召诸子弟与语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366782_comment'></div>不具。真卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366782_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1366782_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年11月22日</a>　十一月，叛将史思明攻陷河间、景城诸郡。又遣其将康没野波攻平原。颜真卿谋于众，知孤军不敌，乃于二十二日弃郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=756&endYear=756')">756年11月</a>　十一月，颜真卿渡河，经广陵、丹阳诸郡，各与采访使李希言、李成式计会竟未果。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d874012ed00447f9803418b919a9272b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d874012ed00447f9803418b919a9272b");'><span id='d874012ed00447f9803418b919a9272b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='d874012ed00447f9803418b919a9272b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>　是年颜真卿由荆襄北趋行在，次襄阳，会肃宗使中官曹日昇来宣慰。因南阳为贼所围已数月，路绝不得入。颜真卿偕中官冯廷瓌为之劝说太守魏仲犀派骑护送入城，以致宣命，且返襄阳取粮，南阳因是遂久守不陷。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cff14d6b3c6349129a7d2bebec518a2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cff14d6b3c6349129a7d2bebec518a2b");'><span id='cff14d6b3c6349129a7d2bebec518a2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='cff14d6b3c6349129a7d2bebec518a2b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>　经邓州内乡县，草书二嫂允南夫人陈氏碑。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
十堰
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='06a9f36f68cd41e68fcc95417544ecdc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("06a9f36f68cd41e68fcc95417544ecdc");'><span id='06a9f36f68cd41e68fcc95417544ecdc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='06a9f36f68cd41e68fcc95417544ecdc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>　行次武当，授宪部尚书，有让表。作品：《让宪部尚书表》<div id='poem_1366740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>让宪部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（757年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366740")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366740'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366740'>臣真卿言。臣闻无功受赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366740_comment'></div>为善不劝。有罪不罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366740_comment'></div>为恶罔辨。陛下尅复之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366740_comment'></div>匪朝伊夕。至如赏罚二柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366740_comment'></div>事在必行。苟或不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366740_comment'></div>于何取则。臣以愚懦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366740_comment'></div>叨守平原。属逆贼安禄山背叛圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366740_comment'></div>扰犯河洛。臣堂兄杲卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366740_comment'></div>以常山太守首开土门。臣与河北诸郡因之固守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366740_comment'></div>人臣本分。夫有何功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366740_comment'></div>上皇授臣户部侍郎兼知招讨采访等使。已失人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366740_comment'></div>缘贼未灭。遂不敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366740_comment'></div>又令李光弼郭子仪贺兰进明等与臣计会。同讨凶逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366740_comment'></div>三数月间。河北向定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366740_comment'></div>属潼关失守。大驾西巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366740_comment'></div>光弼等却入土门。诸郡危逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366740_comment'></div>陛下御极。又录臣无功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366740_comment'></div>宠以非次。常伯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1366740", 1366740, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>亚相</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366740_comment'></div>一时猥集。兄允南弟允臧等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366740_comment'></div>连荣台省。一男三侄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366740_comment'></div>皆授好官。在臣一门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366740_comment'></div>叨幸斯极。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1366740", 1366740, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>殒身碎首</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366740_comment'></div>无以上报。臣常使判官钜鹿郡南和县丞贾载侄男永王府典军广成及行官邓昌珍杨神功裴法成等十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366740_comment'></div>将䌽物绢帛。相继渡海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366740_comment'></div>与刘正臣计会。共和两蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366740_comment'></div>正臣等尅期南来。行已有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366740_comment'></div>属逆贼史思明尹子奇等乘其未至。悉力急攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366740_comment'></div>诸郡无援。相次陷没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366740_comment'></div>皆由臣孱懦无谋。致此颠沛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366740_comment'></div>诚合殉命危难。死守孤城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366740_comment'></div>以为归罪阙庭。愈于受擒<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1366740", 1366740, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>贼手</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366740_comment'></div>所以僶俛偷生过河。缘刘正臣使杨神功将牒与臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366740_comment'></div>索兵马及盘瓶锦帐。令应接奚契丹等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366740_comment'></div>不与其勾当。伏恐陛下贻忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366740_comment'></div>又恩敕先超授吴郡司士郑毓乐安郡太守。令于江淮南两道度僧道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366740_comment'></div>取钱与臣召募士马。令应接河北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366740_comment'></div>臣由此未获即赴行在。遂至广陵丹阳等郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366740_comment'></div>各与采访使计会。竟不得兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366740_comment'></div>即累奉圣旨。许臣入奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366740_comment'></div>行至武当郡。又奉恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366740_comment'></div>除臣宪部尚书。兼令使者送告身与臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366740_comment'></div>捧戴殊私。不任惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366740_comment'></div>陛下纵含宏善贷。不忍明刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366740_comment'></div>在臣腼冒至深。胡颜自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366740_comment'></div>臣忝为大臣。系国休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366740_comment'></div>损臣益国。臣受其益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366740_comment'></div>损国益臣。臣受其损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366740_comment'></div>若受任失守。还朝屡迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366740_comment'></div>示国无刑。于臣大损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366740_comment'></div>非敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1366740", 1366740, "Clauses/98/Comments/0")'>外饰</span>。实披至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366740_comment'></div>又臣名节虽微。任位颇重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366740_comment'></div>为政之体。必在律人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366740_comment'></div>恩先逮下。罚当从上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366740_comment'></div>今罪一人。则万人惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366740_comment'></div>若怙于宠。四海何瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366740_comment'></div>伏愿陛下重贬臣一官。以示天宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366740_comment'></div>使天下知有必行之法。则知有必赏之令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366740_comment'></div>宠荣过于尚书远矣。无任恳悃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366740_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_58_1366740_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宝鸡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='63b79025115d4df5bd50d58214b38564_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("63b79025115d4df5bd50d58214b38564");'><span id='63b79025115d4df5bd50d58214b38564_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='63b79025115d4df5bd50d58214b38564' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年4月</a>　四月至凤翔。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e6cf952e62874e9f95cd282d97d6f622_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6cf952e62874e9f95cd282d97d6f622");'><span id='e6cf952e62874e9f95cd282d97d6f622_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='e6cf952e62874e9f95cd282d97d6f622' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>　玄宗闻真卿至凤翔，遣驿马送至相见。其后，真卿扈从肃宗还西京，改司封郎中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年12月15日</a>　以蜀郡扈从之臣，赐爵金乡县开国男，散官加正议大夫。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
大荔
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c70d82eaa1e44181b72bd9ddface4870_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c70d82eaa1e44181b72bd9ddface4870");'><span id='c70d82eaa1e44181b72bd9ddface4870_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=757&endYear=757')">757年</a>，49岁</div><div id='c70d82eaa1e44181b72bd9ddface4870' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>颜真卿扈从还京，未几忤旨，出贬同州，有谢表。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>上表称述协律郎郑洵贞白，辟入幕下任录事参军。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
永济
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1f1474a1a02542898cf6727482123a7e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1f1474a1a02542898cf6727482123a7e");'><span id='1f1474a1a02542898cf6727482123a7e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>，50岁</div><div id='1f1474a1a02542898cf6727482123a7e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年3月5日</a>　此日，迁蒲州刺史，充本州防御史。封爵丹阳县开国侯。与将军赵琐计会游奕兵马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年3月18日</a>　此日，至任蒲州。上谢表并谢祖官表，由中官张抱诚奏之。作品：《蒲州刺史谢上表》《谢赠祖官表》<div id='poem_1366744' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366744' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366744?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒲州刺史谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年3月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366744")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366744_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366744'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366744'>臣真卿言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366744_comment'></div>臣今月十一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366744_comment'></div>伏奉五日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366744_comment'></div>除臣使持节蒲州诸军事蒲州刺史充本州防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366744_comment'></div>臣缘同州先无佐官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366744_comment'></div>蒲州书鱼未到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366744_comment'></div>迟回累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366744_comment'></div>不敢赴上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366744_comment'></div>中使张抱诚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366744_comment'></div>奉宣恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366744_comment'></div>令臣与将军赵琐计会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366744_comment'></div>游奕兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366744_comment'></div>昨以十八日至州上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366744_comment'></div>祗承宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366744_comment'></div>伏增感惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366744_comment'></div>中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366744_comment'></div>臣窃以此州之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366744_comment'></div>尧舜所都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366744_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1366744", 1366744, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>表里山河</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366744_comment'></div>古称天险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366744_comment'></div>馀凶未殄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366744_comment'></div>防御是先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366744_comment'></div>况扼秦晋之喉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366744_comment'></div>抚幽并之背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366744_comment'></div>既号股肱之郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366744_comment'></div>实资心膂之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366744_comment'></div>伏惟光天文武大圣孝感皇帝陛下道冠生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366744_comment'></div>恩涵坠履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366744_comment'></div>方建非常之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366744_comment'></div>不遗易忘之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366744_comment'></div>特委大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366744_comment'></div>俾之集事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366744_comment'></div>戴荷殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366744_comment'></div>无忘寝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366744_comment'></div>但臣愚驽有素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366744_comment'></div>智勇缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366744_comment'></div>将以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1366744", 1366744, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>镇遏</span>艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366744_comment'></div>导扬德泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366744_comment'></div>拜命之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366744_comment'></div>以荣为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366744_comment'></div>唯君知臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366744_comment'></div>教其不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366744_comment'></div>勤恤人隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366744_comment'></div>动必以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366744_comment'></div>陛下不以为烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366744_comment'></div>则臣死而获考矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366744_comment'></div>无任感戴屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1366744_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1366749' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366749' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366749?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赠官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年3月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366749")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366749_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366749'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366749'>臣真卿言。伏奉二月十七日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366749_comment'></div>臣亡祖故曹王属曹王晋王侍读先臣昭甫。特蒙圣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366749_comment'></div>超赠使持节华州诸军事华州刺史。天慈锡类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366749_comment'></div>泉壤疏荣。捧戴殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366749_comment'></div>阖门感庆。中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366749_comment'></div>窃以臣亡祖伏膺文儒。克笃前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366749_comment'></div>能读三坟五典八索九邱。特为伯父故秘书监先臣师古之所赏爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366749_comment'></div>师古每有注释。未尝不参预焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366749_comment'></div>又与学士令狐德棻等同侍天皇。得备顾问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366749_comment'></div>有时无命。夭阏盛年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366749_comment'></div>臣亡父故嶭王友先臣惟贞亡伯故濠州刺史先臣元孙等。并襁褓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1366749", 1366749, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>苴麻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366749_comment'></div>孩提未识。养于舅氏殷仲容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366749_comment'></div>以至成立。臣堂兄故卫尉卿兼御史中丞杲卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366749_comment'></div>即元孙之子。及臣兄弟等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366749_comment'></div>幸承贻厥之训。遭遇明圣之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366749_comment'></div>各以微诚。皆蒙殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366749_comment'></div>杲卿虽死。为不朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366749_comment'></div>臣亦何人。屡叨荣禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366749_comment'></div>夙夜祇惧。惭戴已深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366749_comment'></div>不谓霈泽曲沾。褒赠俯及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366749_comment'></div>特蒙加等之礼。实为非常之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366749_comment'></div>感戴屏营。万死非报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366749_comment'></div>无任战荷之至。谨因中使内谒者监张抱诚冒死陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366749_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1366749_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年5月28日</a>　此日，因肃宗追赠颜真卿与其众多家族人员封号和官位，上表谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年9月3日</a>　泉明携其兄季明首梓自河北归长安，途经抚州，颜真卿有文祭之。作品：《祭侄季明文》<div id='poem_1366848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭侄季明文</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年9月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366848")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366848'>维乾元元年岁次戊戌九月庚午朔三日壬申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366848_comment'></div>第十三叔银青光禄大夫使持节蒲州诸军事蒲州刺史上轻车都尉丹阳县开国侯真卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366848_comment'></div>以清酌庶羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366848_comment'></div>祭于亡侄赠赞善大夫季明之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366848_comment'></div>惟尔挺生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366848_comment'></div>夙标幼德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366848_comment'></div>宗庙瑚梿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366848_comment'></div>阶庭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1366848", 1366848, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>兰玉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366848_comment'></div>每慰人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366848_comment'></div>方期戬谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366848_comment'></div>何图逆贼间舋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366848_comment'></div>称兵犯顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366848_comment'></div>尔父竭诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366848_comment'></div>常山作郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366848_comment'></div>余时受命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366848_comment'></div>亦在平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366848_comment'></div>仁兄爱我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366848_comment'></div>俾尔传言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366848_comment'></div>尔既归止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366848_comment'></div>爰开土门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366848_comment'></div>土门既开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366848_comment'></div>凶威大蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366848_comment'></div>贼臣不救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366848_comment'></div>孤城围逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366848_comment'></div>父陷子死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366848_comment'></div>巢倾卵覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366848_comment'></div>天不悔祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366848_comment'></div>谁为荼毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366848_comment'></div>念尔遘残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366848_comment'></div>百身何赎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366848_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366848_comment'></div>吾承天泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366848_comment'></div>移牧河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366848_comment'></div>泉明比者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366848_comment'></div>再陷常山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366848_comment'></div>携尔首榇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366848_comment'></div>及兹同还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366848_comment'></div>抚念摧切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366848_comment'></div>震悼心颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366848_comment'></div>方俟远日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366848_comment'></div>及尔幽宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366848_comment'></div>魂而有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366848_comment'></div>无嗟久客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366848_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366848_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1366848_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>　蒲州任上，有书，杜光泰撰。作品：《马承光碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年10月9日</a>　此日，为酷吏唐旻所诬，改饶州刺史。<br /></div>

-----title
华阴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='754ac127b89045f4930076bd8b3555df_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("754ac127b89045f4930076bd8b3555df");'><span id='754ac127b89045f4930076bd8b3555df_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年</a>，50岁</div><div id='754ac127b89045f4930076bd8b3555df' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=758&endYear=758')">758年10月12日</a>　此日，道出华阴，携王延昌、穆宁、张澹、刘暠、郑镇同谒华岳金天王神祠。有题名。作品：《华岳题名》<div id='poem_1366811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华岳庙题名</a><span class='authorDate'>（758年10月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366811")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366811'>皇唐乾元元年岁次戊戌冬十月戊申。真卿自蒲州刺史蒙恩除饶州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366811_comment'></div>十有二日辛亥。次于华阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366811_comment'></div>与监察御史王延昌大理评事摄监察御史穆宁评事张澹华阴令刘皓主簿郑镇同谒金天王之神祠。颜真卿题记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366811_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1366811_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f8eb5feee46c4655bb4e4e014c6c6d4a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f8eb5feee46c4655bb4e4e014c6c6d4a");'><span id='f8eb5feee46c4655bb4e4e014c6c6d4a_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年6月9日</a>　此日除升州刺史，充浙江西道节度使，兼江宁军使，辟荆南戎昱入幕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　途经金陵，撰文。作品：《与蔡明远书》《邹游帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　秋末至任，有谢表。作品：《谢浙西节度使表》<div id='poem_1366746' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366746' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366746?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢浙西节度使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366746")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366746_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366746'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366746'>臣真卿言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366746_comment'></div>伏奉六月九日恩制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366746_comment'></div>以臣为升州刺史充浙西节度使兼江宁军使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366746_comment'></div>圣德含宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366746_comment'></div>不遗簪履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366746_comment'></div>舍其罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366746_comment'></div>假以麾幢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366746_comment'></div>感戴恩荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366746_comment'></div>死生知报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366746_comment'></div>臣某中谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366746_comment'></div>臣以为全吴旧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366746_comment'></div>分阃重权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366746_comment'></div>煮东海以自资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366746_comment'></div>堑西河而作固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366746_comment'></div>九州天险之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366746_comment'></div>六代帝王之都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366746_comment'></div>是以魏文兴嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366746_comment'></div>甘从南北之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366746_comment'></div>苻坚恃众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366746_comment'></div>爰丧百万之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366746_comment'></div>岂不以形胜是先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366746_comment'></div>腹心斯切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366746_comment'></div>亲贤重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366746_comment'></div>镇遏攸难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366746_comment'></div>矧在庸微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366746_comment'></div>宁堪及此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366746_comment'></div>是以拜命之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366746_comment'></div>以荣为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366746_comment'></div>制书以今月四日至饶州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366746_comment'></div>臣以今日发赴本道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366746_comment'></div>取都统节度观察使李峘处分讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366746_comment'></div>即赴升州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366746_comment'></div>即当缮修甲兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366746_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1366746", 1366746, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>抚循</span>将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366746_comment'></div>观察要害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366746_comment'></div>以备不虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366746_comment'></div>假陛下英武之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366746_comment'></div>遵陛下平明之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366746_comment'></div>一心戮力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366746_comment'></div>上答天慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366746_comment'></div>伏惟陛下察臣愚忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366746_comment'></div>则死且不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366746_comment'></div>无任感戴屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1366746_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=759&endYear=759')">759年</a>　会宣谕使左骁卫郎将史元琮、中使张庭玉奉诏宣布各地放生池至升州，乃撰《天下放生池碑铭》一章，绢写，托之奉进，并乞肃宗御书题额。<div id='poem_1366815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天下放生池碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（759年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366815")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366815'>皇唐七叶。我乾元大圣光天文武孝感皇帝陛下以至圣之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366815_comment'></div>属艰虞之运。无少康一旅之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366815_comment'></div>当禄山强暴之初。乾巩劳谦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366815_comment'></div>励精为理。推诚而万方胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366815_comment'></div>克已而天下归仁。恩信侔于四时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366815_comment'></div>英威达于八表。功庸格天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366815_comment'></div>孝感通神明。故得回纥奚霫契丹大食盾蛮之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366815_comment'></div>扶服万里。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>决命</span>而争先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366815_comment'></div>朔方河东平卢河西陇右安西黔中岭南河南之师。虓𧯘五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366815_comment'></div>推锋而效死。摧元恶如拉朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366815_comment'></div>举两京若拾遗。庆绪遁逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366815_comment'></div>已蒙赤族之戮。思明跧伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366815_comment'></div>行就沸鼎之诛。拯已坠之皇纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366815_comment'></div>据再安之宗社。迎上皇于西蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366815_comment'></div>申子道于中京。一日三朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366815_comment'></div>大明天子之孝。问安视膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366815_comment'></div>不改家人之礼。蒸蒸然翼翼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366815_comment'></div>真帝皇之上仪。诰誓所不及已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366815_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>历选</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/36/Comments/1")'>内禅</span>。生人以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366815_comment'></div>振古及隋。未有如我皇帝者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366815_comment'></div>而犹妪煦万类。动唉四生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366815_comment'></div>乃以乾元二年太岁己亥春三月己丑。端命左骁卫右郎将史元琮中使张庭玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366815_comment'></div>奉明诏。布德音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366815_comment'></div>始于洋州之兴道。洎山南剑南黔中荆南岭南江西浙江西诸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366815_comment'></div>讫于升州之江宁秦淮太平桥。临江带郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366815_comment'></div>上下五里。各置放生池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366815_comment'></div>凡八十一所。盖所以宣皇明而广慈爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366815_comment'></div>易不云乎。信及豚鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366815_comment'></div>书不云乎。暨鸟兽鱼鳖咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366815_comment'></div>古之聪明睿智神武而不杀者。非陛下而谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366815_comment'></div>昔殷汤克仁。犹存一面之网。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366815_comment'></div>汉武垂惠。才致衔珠之答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366815_comment'></div>虽流水救涸。宝胜称名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366815_comment'></div>盖事止于当时。尚介祉于终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366815_comment'></div>岂若我今日动者植者。水居陆居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366815_comment'></div>举天下以为池。罄域中而蒙福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366815_comment'></div>乘陁罗尼加持之力。竭烦恼海生死之津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366815_comment'></div>揆之前古。曾何髣髴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366815_comment'></div>微臣职忝方面。生丁盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366815_comment'></div>受恩寖深。无以上报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366815_comment'></div>谨缘皋陶奚斯歌虞颂鲁之义。述天下放生池碑铭一章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366815_comment'></div>虽不足形容明圣万分之一。亦臣之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>精恳</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366815_comment'></div>敢刻金石。著其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366815_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1366815'>明明皇帝。临下有赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366815_comment'></div>至德光天。乾元启赜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366815_comment'></div>纬武戡乱。经文御历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366815_comment'></div>孝感神明。义形金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366815_comment'></div>仁覆华夏。恩加蛮貊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366815_comment'></div>道冠巍巍。威深<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>虩虩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366815_comment'></div>遘兹多难。克广<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>丕绩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366815_comment'></div>庆绪致诛。思明辟易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366815_comment'></div>人道助顺。天心恶逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366815_comment'></div>扑灭之期。匪朝伊夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366815_comment'></div>乘此宝祚。永广宗祏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366815_comment'></div>业盛君亲。功崇列辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366815_comment'></div>交禅之际。粲然明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366815_comment'></div>迥映来今。孤高往策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366815_comment'></div>去杀流惠。好生立辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366815_comment'></div>率土之滨。临江是宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366815_comment'></div>遂其生性。庇尔鳞翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366815_comment'></div>环海为池。周天布泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366815_comment'></div>致兹忠厚。罔弗怡怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366815_comment'></div>动植依仁。飞沈受获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366815_comment'></div>流水长者。徒称往昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366815_comment'></div>宝胜如来。畴庸允格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366815_comment'></div>德力无竞。慈悲孔硕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366815_comment'></div>相时传闻。尚赖宏益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366815_comment'></div>矧在遭遇。其忘敷锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366815_comment'></div>真卿勒铭。敢告<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1366815", 1366815, "Clauses/137/Comments/0")'>凡百</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366815_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1366815_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4ae1a8d421f84a02b18f9b82553a8fd2_label'><a gray;'>▪</span>春日，送旧友刘太冲西游，撰有序。作品：《送刘太冲序》<div id='poem_1366788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366788?labeling=true' "poem_title_1366788")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366788'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366788'>刘太冲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366788_comment'></div>彭城之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1366788", 1366788, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>华望</span>者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366788_comment'></div>自开府垂明于宋室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366788_comment'></div>泽州考绩于国朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366788_comment'></div>道素相承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366788_comment'></div>世传儒雅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366788_comment'></div>尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366788_comment'></div>夫其果行修洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366788_comment'></div>斯文<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1366788", 1366788, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>彪蔚</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366788_comment'></div>鄂不照乎栘华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366788_comment'></div>龙骥骧乎云路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366788_comment'></div>则公山正礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366788_comment'></div>策高足于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366788_comment'></div>冲与太真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366788_comment'></div>嗣家声于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366788_comment'></div>有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366788_comment'></div>昔予作郡平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366788_comment'></div>拒胡羯而请与从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366788_comment'></div>掌铨吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366788_comment'></div>第甲乙而超升等夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366788_comment'></div>尔来蹉跎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366788_comment'></div>犹屑卑位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366788_comment'></div>虽才不偶命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366788_comment'></div>而德其无邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366788_comment'></div>故冲之西游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366788_comment'></div>斯有望矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366788_comment'></div>江月弦魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366788_comment'></div>秦淮顶潮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366788_comment'></div>君行句溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366788_comment'></div>正及春水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366788_comment'></div>勖哉之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366788_comment'></div>道存何居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366788_comment'></div>鲁郡公颜真卿叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1366788_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>正书晋李阐撰、颜延之铭《颜含碑》作品：《右光禄大夫西平靖侯颜府君碑》<div id='poem_1366820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晋侍中右光禄大夫本州大中正西平靖侯颜公大宗碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366820")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366820'>公讳含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366820_comment'></div>字宏都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366820_comment'></div>琅琊临沂人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366820_comment'></div>其先出于邾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366820_comment'></div>颜公子友封于郳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366820_comment'></div>是为小邾子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366820_comment'></div>为鲁附庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366820_comment'></div>居于邹邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366820_comment'></div>因以命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366820_comment'></div>孔门达者八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366820_comment'></div>曰路回辛骄祖哙仆何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366820_comment'></div>次有丁阖叔子率躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366820_comment'></div>秦有芝贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366820_comment'></div>汉有肆异安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366820_comment'></div>魏有斐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366820_comment'></div>盛字叔台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366820_comment'></div>青徐二州刺史关内侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366820_comment'></div>始自鲁居琅琊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366820_comment'></div>代传恭孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366820_comment'></div>故号所居为孝悌里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366820_comment'></div>生钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366820_comment'></div>字公若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366820_comment'></div>明韩诗礼易尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366820_comment'></div>多所通说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366820_comment'></div>学者宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366820_comment'></div>历大中大夫东莞广陵太守葛绎贞子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366820_comment'></div>生默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366820_comment'></div>字静伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366820_comment'></div>晋汝阴太守护军将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366820_comment'></div>生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366820_comment'></div>少有操行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366820_comment'></div>以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366820_comment'></div>兄畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366820_comment'></div>咸宁中死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366820_comment'></div>托梦当复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366820_comment'></div>发棺而气息甚微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366820_comment'></div>阖家营视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366820_comment'></div>母妻不能无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366820_comment'></div>公乃绝弃人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366820_comment'></div>躬亲侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366820_comment'></div>足不出户者十有三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366820_comment'></div>次嫂樊氏失明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366820_comment'></div>须髯蛇胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366820_comment'></div>寻求不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366820_comment'></div>忽有青衣童子持囊授公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366820_comment'></div>乃蛇胆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366820_comment'></div>寻出户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366820_comment'></div>化成青鸟飞去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366820_comment'></div>东海王越以为太傅参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366820_comment'></div>元帝过江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366820_comment'></div>为丞相祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366820_comment'></div>东宫初建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366820_comment'></div>公以儒素笃行补太子中庶子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366820_comment'></div>迁黄门侍郎本州大中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366820_comment'></div>封西平县侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366820_comment'></div>拜侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366820_comment'></div>除吴郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366820_comment'></div>公所历简而有恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366820_comment'></div>明而能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366820_comment'></div>然以威风御下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366820_comment'></div>王导叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366820_comment'></div>颜公在事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366820_comment'></div>吴人敛手矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366820_comment'></div>未之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366820_comment'></div>复为侍中国子祭酒光禄勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366820_comment'></div>以年老逊位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366820_comment'></div>成帝美其素行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366820_comment'></div>就加右光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366820_comment'></div>门施行马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366820_comment'></div>赐床帐被褥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366820_comment'></div>敕大官四时致膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366820_comment'></div>固辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366820_comment'></div>时论者欲为王导降礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366820_comment'></div>冯怀以问于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366820_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366820_comment'></div>吾闻伐国不问仁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366820_comment'></div>向冯祖思问佞于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366820_comment'></div>我有邪德乎。<div id='poem_sentence_79_1366820_comment'></div>隐伏之奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366820_comment'></div>非圣不诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366820_comment'></div>众咸服焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366820_comment'></div>郭璞尝欲为公筮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366820_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366820_comment'></div>自有性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366820_comment'></div>无劳蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366820_comment'></div>桓温求婚。<div id='poem_sentence_572_1366820_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_573_1366820_comment'></div>吾祖以志行纯粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_574_1366820_comment'></div>感通神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_575_1366820_comment'></div>贻谋子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_576_1366820_comment'></div>奕叶无改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_577_1366820_comment'></div>其后忠义孝悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_578_1366820_comment'></div>文学才业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_579_1366820_comment'></div>布在青史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_580_1366820_comment'></div>粲然可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_581_1366820_comment'></div>非夫德盛流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_582_1366820_comment'></div>何能若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_583_1366820_comment'></div>真卿小子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_584_1366820_comment'></div>惧不克荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_585_1366820_comment'></div>顷自抚州代到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_586_1366820_comment'></div>获展旧山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_587_1366820_comment'></div>虽碑版沈沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_588_1366820_comment'></div>而邱封俨在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_589_1366820_comment'></div>敢扬不朽之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_590_1366820_comment'></div>庶竭罔极之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_591_1366820_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_592_1366820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_593_1366820'>铄吾祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_593_1366820_comment'></div>渡江浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_594_1366820_comment'></div>孝通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_595_1366820_comment'></div>名轶古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_596_1366820_comment'></div>凡七叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_597_1366820_comment'></div>葬白下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_598_1366820_comment'></div>本支分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_599_1366820_comment'></div>源流溥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_600_1366820_comment'></div>世忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_601_1366820_comment'></div>謺规矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_602_1366820_comment'></div>毣鸾皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_603_1366820_comment'></div>炳龙虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_604_1366820_comment'></div>文雎涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_605_1366820_comment'></div>学邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_606_1366820_comment'></div>赫才明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_607_1366820_comment'></div>振区宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_608_1366820_comment'></div>亘今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_609_1366820_comment'></div>难悉数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_610_1366820_comment'></div>嗟末孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_611_1366820_comment'></div>惭下武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_612_1366820_comment'></div>扬耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_613_1366820_comment'></div>愧无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_614_1366820_comment'></div>丰碑立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_615_1366820_comment'></div>百世睹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_616_1366820_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>客次上元日，正书李白《志公像赞》于蒋山寺壁。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游玄武湖，记之。作品：《玄武湖记》<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游玄妙观，写老君赞。作品：《玄妙观老君赞》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='821e12cf837642b6bbceec806e5aff03_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("821e12cf837642b6bbceec806e5aff03");'><span id='821e12cf837642b6bbceec806e5aff03_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>，69岁</div><div id='821e12cf837642b6bbceec806e5aff03' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　历建业，溯江西下。<br /></div>
-----end

武汉

-----title
南部（新政县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ad40f1e534d04542941e67c879983815_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ad40f1e534d04542941e67c879983815");'><span id='ad40f1e534d04542941e67c879983815_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>，52岁</div><div id='ad40f1e534d04542941e67c879983815' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=760&endYear=760')">760年</a>　途经新政县遇故旧成都兵曹鲜于昱，因邀撰《鲜于氏离堆记》颂述其父鲜于仲通。<div id='poem_1366792' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366792' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366792?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鲜于氏离堆记</a><span class='authorDate'>（760年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366792")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366792_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366792'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366792'>阆州之东百馀里。有县曰新政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366792_comment'></div>新政之南数千步。有山曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1366792", 1366792, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>离堆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366792_comment'></div>斗入嘉陵江。直上数百尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366792_comment'></div>形胜缩矗。欹壁峻肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366792_comment'></div>上峥嵘而下回洑。不与众山相连属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366792_comment'></div>是之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1366792", 1366792, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>离堆</span>。东面有石堂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366792_comment'></div>即故京兆尹鲜于君之所开凿也。堂有室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366792_comment'></div>广轮袤丈。萧豁洞敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366792_comment'></div>虚闻江声。彻见群象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366792_comment'></div>人村川坝。若指诸掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366792_comment'></div>堂北磐石之上。有九曲流杯池焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366792_comment'></div>悬源螭首。蹙喷鹤咮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366792_comment'></div>酾渠股引。迾坐环溜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366792_comment'></div>若有良朋。以倾醇酎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366792_comment'></div>堂南有茅斋焉。游于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366792_comment'></div>息于斯。聚宾友于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366792_comment'></div>虚而来者实而归。其斋壁间有诗焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366792_comment'></div>皆君舅著作郎严从君甥殿中侍御史严铣之等美君考槃之所作也。其右有小石廅焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366792_comment'></div>亦可荫而踆据矣。其松竹桂榑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366792_comment'></div>冬青杂树。皆徙他山而栽莳焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366792_comment'></div>其上方有男宫观焉。署之曰景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366792_comment'></div>君弟京兆尹叔明至德一年十月尝任尚书司勋员外郎之所奉置也。君讳向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366792_comment'></div>字仲通。以字行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366792_comment'></div>渔阳人。卓尔坚忮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366792_comment'></div>毅然抗直。易有之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366792_comment'></div>笃实辉光。书不云乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366792_comment'></div>沈潜刚克。君自高曾以降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366792_comment'></div>世以财雄。招徕贤豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366792_comment'></div>施舍不倦。至君继绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366792_comment'></div>其流益光。弱冠以任侠自喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366792_comment'></div>尚未知名。乃慷慨发愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366792_comment'></div>于焉卜筑。养蒙学文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366792_comment'></div>忘寝与食。不四三载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366792_comment'></div>展也大成。著作奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366792_comment'></div>勖以宾荐。无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366792_comment'></div>以进士高第。骤登台省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366792_comment'></div>天宝九载。以益州大都督府长史兼御史中丞持节充剑南节度副大使知节度事剑南山南西道采访处置使入为司农少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366792_comment'></div>遂作京兆尹。以忤杨国忠贬邵阳郡司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366792_comment'></div>十有二载秋八月。除汉阳郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366792_comment'></div>冬十有一月。终于所任官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366792_comment'></div>悲夫。雄图未伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366792_comment'></div>志业已空。葬于县北表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366792_comment'></div>附先茔。礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366792_comment'></div>君之薨也。冢子光禄寺丞昱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366792_comment'></div>匍匐迎丧。星言泣血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366792_comment'></div>自沔溯峡。湍险万重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366792_comment'></div>肩槁足跼。扳笭引舳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366792_comment'></div>凡今几年。皲瘃在目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366792_comment'></div>因心则至。岂无僮仆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366792_comment'></div>暨昱之季。曰尚书都官员外郎炅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366792_comment'></div>克笃前烈。永言孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366792_comment'></div>恳□□志反葬于兹。行道之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366792_comment'></div>孰不跂而。真卿犹子曰纮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366792_comment'></div>从父兄故偃师丞春卿之子也。尝尉阆中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366792_comment'></div>君故旧不遗。与之有忘年之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366792_comment'></div>叔明昱炅亦笃世亲之欢。真卿因之又忝宪司之寮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366792_comment'></div>亟与济南蹇昂。奉以周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366792_comment'></div>益著通家之好。兄允南以司膳司封二郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366792_comment'></div>弟允臧以三院御史。皆与叔明首末联事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366792_comment'></div>我是用饱君之故。乾元改号上元之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366792_comment'></div>秋八月。哉生魄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366792_comment'></div>猥自刑部侍郎以言事忤旨。圣恩全宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366792_comment'></div>贬贰于蓬州。沿嘉陵而路出新政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366792_comment'></div>适会昱以成都兵曹取急归觐。遭我乎贵州之朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366792_comment'></div>留游缔欢。信宿陉岘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366792_comment'></div>感今怀昔。遂援翰而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366792_comment'></div>叔明时刺商州。炅又申掾京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366792_comment'></div>不同<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1366792", 1366792, "Clauses/134/Comments/0")'>跻陟</span>。有恨如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366792_comment'></div>帝唐龙集后壬寅仲夏己卯朔十五日甲午。刻于门序之左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366792_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1366792_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
