-----title
九江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c53cd07f1955418392ff9ee20ec6c19a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c53cd07f1955418392ff9ee20ec6c19a");'><span id='c53cd07f1955418392ff9ee20ec6c19a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=768')">766-768年</a>，58-60岁</div><div id='c53cd07f1955418392ff9ee20ec6c19a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年7月</a>　月初，历江州，上庐山拜晤同愔、熙怡二大师，恵彦、正义和法真诸律师，并题名于东林、西林两寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　至任吉州，御史韩涉、刺史梁乘尝见招，欲游青原山靖居寺，未果。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=766&endYear=766')">766年</a>　撰并正书《鲜于仲通碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年10月26日</a>　此日，偕评事韦甫已以及房澄、陆涓诸人和子侄同游靖居寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年10月</a>　翌日题名于寺，寺僧明则、智清陪焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=767&endYear=767')">767年10月</a>　本年有书帖。作品：《守政帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年</a>　吉州别驾任上，怡然自乐，不以谪守远郡为怀。因法源大师之请，撰文。作品：《天台智者大师画赞》《天台山国清寺壁上大师说法影像并佛顶及维摩四五六祖像》<div id='poem_51061' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51061' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/51061?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天台智者大师画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（768年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_51061")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_51061_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_51061'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_51061'>天台大师俗姓陈，其名智顗华容人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_51061'>隋炀皇帝崇明因，号为智者诚敬申。<div id='poem_sentence_1_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_51061'>师初孕育灵异频，彩烟浮空光照邻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_51061'>尧眉舜目熙若春，禅慧悲智严其身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_51061'>长沙佛前发弘誓，定光菩萨示冥契。<div id='poem_sentence_4_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_51061'>恍如登山临海际，上指伽蓝毕身世。<div id='poem_sentence_5_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_51061'>东谒大苏求真谛，智同灵鹫听法偈。<div id='poem_sentence_6_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_51061'>得宿命通弁无碍，旋陀罗尼华三昧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_51061'>居常西面化在东，八载瓦官阐玄风。<div id='poem_sentence_8_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_51061'>敷演智度发禅蒙，梁陈旧德皆仰崇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_51061'>遂入天台华顶中，因见定光符昔梦。<div id='poem_sentence_10_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_51061'>降魔制敌为法雄，胡僧开道精感通。<div id='poem_sentence_11_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_51061'>又有圣贤垂秘旨，时平国清即名寺。<div id='poem_sentence_12_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_51061'>赎得鱼梁五百里，其中放生讲流水。<div id='poem_sentence_13_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_51061'>后主三礼洞庭里，请为菩萨戒弟子。<div id='poem_sentence_14_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_51061'>炀皇世镇临江涘，金城说会求制止。<div id='poem_sentence_15_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_51061'>香火事讫乃西旋，渚宫听众逾五千。<div id='poem_sentence_16_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_51061'>建立精舍名玉泉，横亘万里皆禀缘。<div id='poem_sentence_17_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_51061'>炀皇启请回法船，非禅不智求弘宣。<div id='poem_sentence_18_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_51061'>遂著《净名精义传》，因令徐柳参其玄。<div id='poem_sentence_19_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_51061'>帝既西趍移象魏，师因东还遂初志。<div id='poem_sentence_20_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_51061'>半山忽与沙门颠，俄倾逡巡偡韬秘。<div id='poem_sentence_21_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_51061'>止观大师名法源，亲事左溪弘度门。<div id='poem_sentence_22_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_51061'>二威灌顶诵师言，同禀思文龙树尊。<div id='poem_sentence_23_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_51061'>荆溪妙乐间生孙，广述祖教补乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_24_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_51061'>写照随形殊好存，源公瞻礼必益敦。<div id='poem_sentence_25_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_51061'>俾余赞述斯讨论，庶几亿载垂后昆。<div id='poem_sentence_26_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_51061'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_51061_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_51061'><span class='label'>按：</span>（《传教大师全集·天台灵应图本传集》卷二，转录自《东南文化》一九九○年六期《天台文化专号》）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_51061_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fdd3a10a16ea4f2f82708db873dc0a75_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fdd3a10a16ea4f2f82708db873dc0a75");'><span id='fdd3a10a16ea4f2f82708db873dc0a75_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>，69岁</div><div id='fdd3a10a16ea4f2f82708db873dc0a75' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　至江州，立《祖碑》于将军庙前。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
抚州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='893bb6ae47814867874272cec879f92e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("893bb6ae47814867874272cec879f92e");'><span id='893bb6ae47814867874272cec879f92e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=771')">768-771年</a>，60-63岁</div><div id='893bb6ae47814867874272cec879f92e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年5月</a>　本月，除抚州刺史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=768&endYear=768')">768年11月5日</a>　此日，弟允臧卒于江陵少尹任上，年五十九。同胞兄弟至是，唯存真卿一人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年</a>　抚州任上，颜真卿公务之暇，乃游赏山水，撰碑记以志之。作品：《桥仙观碑记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年</a>　颜真卿因受邀游赏新修观宇，撰书颂述之。作品：《魏夫人仙坛碑》<div id='poem_1366825' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366825' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366825?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晋紫虚元君领上真司命南岳夫人魏夫人仙坛碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366825")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366825_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366825'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366825'>夫人讳华存。字贤安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366825_comment'></div>任城人。晋司徒剧阳文康公舒之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366825_comment'></div>师于小有清虚真人王裒。裒命中候上仙范邈为立传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366825_comment'></div>其略云。夫人挺琼兰之流映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366825_comment'></div>体自然之灵璞。志逸云霞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366825_comment'></div>明洁鲜蔚。天才卓异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366825_comment'></div>元标幽拔。少读老庄三传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366825_comment'></div>五经百子。无不该览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366825_comment'></div>性乐神仙。味真慕道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366825_comment'></div>少服胡麻散茯苓丸。吐纳气液。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366825_comment'></div>摄生夷静。亲戚往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366825_comment'></div>一无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1366825", 1366825, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>关见</span>。常欲别居閒处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366825_comment'></div>父母不许。年二十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366825_comment'></div>强适太保掾南阳刘君幼彦。生二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366825_comment'></div>璞。遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366825_comment'></div>幼彦后为修武令。夫人心期幽灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366825_comment'></div>精诚苦尽。逮子息粗立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366825_comment'></div>乃离隔室宇。斋于别寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366825_comment'></div>清修百日。忽有太极真人安度明东华大神方诸青童扶桑碧河汤谷神王景林真人小有仙清虚真人王裒来降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366825_comment'></div>裒谓夫人曰。闻子密纬真气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366825_comment'></div>太帝君敕我授子神真之道。青童曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366825_comment'></div>清虚尔之师也。度明曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366825_comment'></div>子苦心求道。道今来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366825_comment'></div>景林曰。虚皇鉴尔勤感太极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366825_comment'></div>已注子于玉札。子其勖哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366825_comment'></div>青童又曰。子不受闻上道内法晨景玉经者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366825_comment'></div>仙道无缘得成也。后日当会阳洛山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366825_comment'></div>尔勤密之矣。王君乃命侍女开玉笈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366825_comment'></div>出太上宝文八素隐身大洞真经高仙羽元等书三十一卷。手授夫人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366825_comment'></div>此皆王君昔遇南极夫人西城真人王方平于阳洛山所受之本经也。山中有洞台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366825_comment'></div>是清虚之别宫。王君至是北向祝誓于夫人曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366825_comment'></div>太上三元。九皇高真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366825_comment'></div>虚微八道。上清玉晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366825_comment'></div>裒为太帝所敕于魏华存。王君又说太极白简青箓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366825_comment'></div>金刻玉文。有得见此三十一卷书者之姓名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366825_comment'></div>凡此宝书。起自清虚真人受太师西城王君紫元夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366825_comment'></div>从是当七人得之。以白玉为简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366825_comment'></div>青玉为字。至夫人为四矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366825_comment'></div>于是景林又授夫人黄庭内景经。令昼夜诵读万遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366825_comment'></div>乃得洞观鬼神。此乃不死之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366825_comment'></div>于是四真吟唱。各命玉女弹琴击鼓吹箫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366825_comment'></div>合节而发歌。歌毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366825_comment'></div>王君乃解语夫人向所授书。存思指归宝经节度行事口诀诸要粗讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366825_comment'></div>徐乃别去。凡二夕一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366825_comment'></div>共会在曲静之中。自此之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366825_comment'></div>王君及西城真人诸元君夫人互有来往。或与隔壁共庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366825_comment'></div>初不骇悟。已而幼彦以暴疾殒世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366825_comment'></div>直天下荒乱。夫人抚养内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366825_comment'></div>傍救穷乏。超群先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366825_comment'></div>乃携细小。径来东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366825_comment'></div>及儿息各大。并处官位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366825_comment'></div>至于守静之思。与日而进也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366825_comment'></div>凡在世八十三年。以成帝咸和九年岁在甲午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366825_comment'></div>王君乃与东华青童来降。与夫人灵药两剂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366825_comment'></div>使顿服之。剋期曾于阳洛宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366825_comment'></div>夫人服药称疾。闭目寝息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366825_comment'></div>饮而不食。七日夜半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366825_comment'></div>太乙元仙遣飙车来迎。夫人用藏景之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366825_comment'></div>托形神剑。化成死骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366825_comment'></div>始终外朗。仙化内逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366825_comment'></div>冥变隐适。从此而绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366825_comment'></div>子璞时为庾司空司马。遐时为陶太尉从事中郎安城太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366825_comment'></div>故夫人自此隐化沦景。须臾至阳洛山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366825_comment'></div>明日。青童君太极四真人清虚王君三天法师张道陵等凡四十七真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366825_comment'></div>降教夫人于隐元之台。王君令夫人清斋五百日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366825_comment'></div>读大洞真经。并分别登真秘奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366825_comment'></div>道陵授以新出明威章奏入静存祝吏兵符箓之诀。众真各标至训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366825_comment'></div>三日而去。道陵所以备教委曲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366825_comment'></div>以夫人在世为女官祭酒。领职理故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366825_comment'></div>夫人遂修斋读经。诵言万过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366825_comment'></div>积十六年。颜如少女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366825_comment'></div>于是龟山九灵太真西王母金阙圣君南极元君乃共来迎。夫人遂白日升晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366825_comment'></div>北诣上清宫玉阙之下。太微天帝中央王老君三素高元君太上玉晨大道君太素三元君扶桑太帝君金阙后圣君各令使者致命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366825_comment'></div>授夫人玉札金文。位为紫虚元君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366825_comment'></div>领上真司命南岳夫人。比秩仙公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366825_comment'></div>使治天台大霍山洞台之中。主下训奉道教授当真仙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366825_comment'></div>而男之高仙曰真人。女曰元君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366825_comment'></div>于是夫人受锡事毕。王母及金阙圣君南极元君各去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366825_comment'></div>使夫人于王屋小有之中。更斋戒三日毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366825_comment'></div>九微元君龟山王母三元夫人冯双礼珠暨诸众仙并降夫人于小有清虚上宫绛房之中。时夫人与王君为宾主焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366825_comment'></div>神肴罗陈。金觞四奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366825_comment'></div>各命侍女陈曲成之钧。九云合节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366825_comment'></div>八音零粲。于是西王母击节而歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366825_comment'></div>歌毕。冯双礼珠弹云璈而答歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366825_comment'></div>馀真人各歌。须臾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366825_comment'></div>司命神仙请隶属及南岳神灵迎官并至。虎旗龙辇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366825_comment'></div>激曜数百里中。西王母诸真乃共与夫人东南行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366825_comment'></div>俱诣天台霍山台。又便道过句曲金坛茅叔申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366825_comment'></div>宴会二日二夕。又共适于霍山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366825_comment'></div>夫人安驾玉宇。然后各别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366825_comment'></div>初王君告夫人曰。学者当去疾除病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366825_comment'></div>因授甘草丸。所谓谷仙方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366825_comment'></div>夫人服之而仙。夫人能隶书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366825_comment'></div>为王君立传。事甚详悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366825_comment'></div>又述青精䭀饭。注黄庭内景经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366825_comment'></div>自后屡降茅山。子璞后至侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366825_comment'></div>蒙使传法于司徒琅琊王舍人杨羲护军长史许穆。穆子玉斧并升仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366825_comment'></div>事具陶宏景真诰。所呼南真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366825_comment'></div>即夫人也。初夫人既渡江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366825_comment'></div>遍游名山。至临川郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366825_comment'></div>临汝水西立坛置精舍。院东百馀步造冢圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366825_comment'></div>又于石井山建立坛场。往来游憩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366825_comment'></div>岁月深久。榛芜沦翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366825_comment'></div>虽备载图经。而略无遗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366825_comment'></div>有唐女道士黄令微。道行高远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366825_comment'></div>八十而有少容。蹀屣而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366825_comment'></div>奔马不及。时人见其颜色殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366825_comment'></div>号曰华姑。闻夫人灵迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366825_comment'></div>长寿二年岁在壬辰冬十月。乃讯于洪州西山道士胡超。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366825_comment'></div>超能通神明。遥指郭南六里乌龟原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366825_comment'></div>有石龟。每犯田苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366825_comment'></div>被人击首析。其处是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366825_comment'></div>姑与道流寻访。见龟在坛中央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366825_comment'></div>其下得尊像油瓮锯刀灯盏之类。俄梦夫人指九曲池于坛南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366825_comment'></div>获之。砖砌犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366825_comment'></div>景云中。睿宗使道士叶善信将绣像幡花来修法事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366825_comment'></div>仍于坛西置洞灵观。度女道士七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366825_comment'></div>开元初。玄宗使醮祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366825_comment'></div>祈祷不绝。每有风雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366825_comment'></div>或闻箫管之声。入室礼谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366825_comment'></div>必须严洁。不尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366825_comment'></div>必有蛇虎惊吼之异。时时有云如乌鸟群飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366825_comment'></div>垂带直下坛上。倏忽不见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366825_comment'></div>西出如向井山。前后非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366825_comment'></div>已而华姑肸蚃间。如有告者曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366825_comment'></div>井山古迹。汝须崇建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366825_comment'></div>俄闻异香从西来。姑行宿洞口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366825_comment'></div>闻钟磬之音。迟明入山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366825_comment'></div>果遇坛殿馀址。遂建立屋宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366825_comment'></div>屡闻仙梵之响。环坛数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366825_comment'></div>有采斫及不精洁者。必有怪异之警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366825_comment'></div>有野鹿中箭。来投华姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366825_comment'></div>姑为拔之。后每斋前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366825_comment'></div>则衔莲藕以献姑。开元九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366825_comment'></div>姑欲上升。告弟子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366825_comment'></div>勿钉吾棺。可以绛纱羃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366825_comment'></div>已而雷霆震击。纱上有孔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366825_comment'></div>大如鸡卵。棺中惟有被覆木简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366825_comment'></div>屋上穿可容人。座前奠瓜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366825_comment'></div>数日生蔓。结实如桃者二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366825_comment'></div>每至忌辰。则风雨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_140_1366825", 1366825, "Clauses/281/Comments/0")'>郁勃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366825_comment'></div>直入室内。玄宗闻而骇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366825_comment'></div>覆视明白。使道士蔡伟编入后仙传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366825_comment'></div>二十九年春三月乙酉。使道士赍龙璧来醮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366825_comment'></div>忽有白鹿自坛东出。至冢间而灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366825_comment'></div>五色仙蛾集坛上。刺史范阳张景佚以为圣德感应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366825_comment'></div>立碑颂述。天宝八载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366825_comment'></div>以夫人得道升仙之所。度女道士二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366825_comment'></div>见修香火。大历三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366825_comment'></div>真卿叨刺是州。言崇礼谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366825_comment'></div>郊郭蒙邃。萑蒲震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366825_comment'></div>女弱曹逃。豺狼窟聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366825_comment'></div>真仪如在。坛殿岿然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366825_comment'></div>瞻仰徘徊。悄焉若失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366825_comment'></div>有仙坛观道士谭仙岩者。修真自远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366825_comment'></div>法侣是宗。请以男官黄道士二七人抽隶洞灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366825_comment'></div>共申洒扫。高行女道士黎琼仙七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366825_comment'></div>萃居坛院。精力住持巳久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366825_comment'></div>率励往来。增修观宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366825_comment'></div>从之。不日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366825_comment'></div>遹暨厥成。仙迹之载崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366825_comment'></div>师之力也。敢备其本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366825_comment'></div>而为颂云。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366825_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_163_1366825'>紫虚元君。维魏夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366825_comment'></div>位列五岳。名高七真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366825_comment'></div>凝华台允。夺志刘嫔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366825_comment'></div>太帝昭恳。清虚降神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366825_comment'></div>群仙毕会。玉笈斯陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366825_comment'></div>服道日损。精心益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366825_comment'></div>蜕形神剑。托驭飙轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366825_comment'></div>适抵阳洛。遄登隐元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366825_comment'></div>黄庭朗咏。白日升晨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366825_comment'></div>西降王母。东过叔申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366825_comment'></div>传法侍中。许杨为邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366825_comment'></div>伊昔南渡。爰居汝滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366825_comment'></div>坛场处所。埋没荒榛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366825_comment'></div>实赖华姑。谂于胡尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366825_comment'></div>果获灵迹。乌龟之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1366825_comment'></div>次寻井山。实叶曩言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1366825_comment'></div>嫣然简解。纱羃空存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1366825_comment'></div>野鹿衔藕。灵瓜吐根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1366825_comment'></div>怪异昭彰。不可殚论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1366825_comment'></div>二圣竦骇。屡崇明禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1366825_comment'></div>于嗟女弱。香火堙沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1366825_comment'></div>真卿刺州。谒拜斯频。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1366825_comment'></div>乃命仙子。增修鼎新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1366825_comment'></div>华姑侍傍。异代同尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1366825_comment'></div>曷表元德。铭功翠珉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1366825_comment'></div>垂诸来裔。坱圠无垠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1366825_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_189_1366825_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年4月8日</a>　是时,旧友吉州靖居寺僧智清主持临川内史谢灵运翻经台,佛迹寺僧什喻并道士谭仙岩修饰栋宇,至四月初八日斯功告竣，颜真卿应邀莅临法会,撰书《谢康乐翻经台记》志述之。<div id='poem_1366793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州宝应寺翻经台记</a><span class='authorDate'>（769年4月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366793")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366793'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366793'>抚州城东南四里有翻经台。宋康乐侯谢公元嘉年初于此翻译涅槃经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366793_comment'></div>因以为号。公讳灵运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366793_comment'></div>陈郡阳夏人也。祖元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366793_comment'></div>晋车骑将军。父瑍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366793_comment'></div>秘书郎。公幼颖悟好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366793_comment'></div>博览群书。文章之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366793_comment'></div>江左莫逮。以袭祖爵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366793_comment'></div>世人宗之。盛称谢康乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366793_comment'></div>初为刘毅卫军从事中郎太子左率。出为永嘉太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366793_comment'></div>郡有名山水。公素爱好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366793_comment'></div>肆意遨游。称疾去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366793_comment'></div>于始宁县修营故墅。傍山带江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366793_comment'></div>尽幽居之美。因著山居赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366793_comment'></div>并自注之。与隐士王宏之等游放为娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366793_comment'></div>有终焉之志。每一诗至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366793_comment'></div>都邑莫不竞写。宿昔之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366793_comment'></div>士庶皆遍。徵为秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366793_comment'></div>再召不赴。太祖使范泰与书敦奖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366793_comment'></div>乃出就职。寻迁侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366793_comment'></div>日夕引见。赏遇甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366793_comment'></div>多疾不朝。赐假东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366793_comment'></div>免官。与从弟惠连东海何长瑜颍川荀道雍泰山羊璿之以文章赏会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366793_comment'></div>时人谓之四友。寻山登赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366793_comment'></div>常著木屐。上则去其前齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366793_comment'></div>下则去其后齿。会稽太守孟顗事佛精恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366793_comment'></div>公谓之曰。得道应须慧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366793_comment'></div>丈人生天应在灵运前。成佛必在灵运后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366793_comment'></div>顗深恨此言。后遂表公有异志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366793_comment'></div>公驰出自陈。太祖知见诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366793_comment'></div>除临川内史。公以昙无谶所翻大涅槃经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366793_comment'></div>语少朴质。不甚流靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366793_comment'></div>品数疏简。初学者难以措怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366793_comment'></div>乃与沙门范惠严顾慧观依旧泥洹经共为润色。勒成三十六卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366793_comment'></div>义理昭畅。质文相宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366793_comment'></div>历代宝之。盛行于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366793_comment'></div>其馀感神徵应。具如高僧传所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366793_comment'></div>邈乎阶扃不改。栋宇具无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366793_comment'></div>真卿叨刺是邦。兹用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1366793", 1366793, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>忾息</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366793_comment'></div>有高行头陀僧智清。绪发洪誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366793_comment'></div>精心住持。请以佛迹寺僧什喻仙台观道士谭仙岩同力增修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366793_comment'></div>指期恢复。自是法堂之遗构克崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366793_comment'></div>先达之高踪不泯。百里而遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366793_comment'></div>四山不逼。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1366793", 1366793, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>三休</span>而上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366793_comment'></div>十地方超。经行之业既崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366793_comment'></div>斗薮之功斯懋。大历已酉岁四月丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366793_comment'></div>都人士庶。相与大会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366793_comment'></div>设严供而落焉。以真卿业于斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366793_comment'></div>见咨纪述。后之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366793_comment'></div>其忘增修乎。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366793_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1366793'>摩诃般若。解脱法身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366793_comment'></div>是则涅槃。众经中尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366793_comment'></div>昙无肇允。严观是因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366793_comment'></div>实赖同德。宏兹法轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366793_comment'></div>谢公发挥。精义入神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366793_comment'></div>理绝史野。文兼郁彬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366793_comment'></div>一垂刊削。百代咸遵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366793_comment'></div>遗迹忽睹。高台嶙峋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366793_comment'></div>载悲徂谢。曷践音尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366793_comment'></div>真卿愀然。悯故孰新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366793_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1366793", 1366793, "Clauses/118/Comments/0")'>檀那</span>衣钵。悉力经纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366793_comment'></div>不日复之。周邦仰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366793_comment'></div>缅怀敦慕。子亦何人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366793_comment'></div>徒愿神交。愧非德邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366793_comment'></div>刻铭金石。永永不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366793_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1366793_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=769&endYear=769')">769年</a>　此日，颜真卿命侄顶、願护扶其弟允臧、六嫂幼舆夫人殷氏灵柩,自江陵归葬于长安万年县祖茔。乔卿之墓亦起于同时。先后撰书仲兄允南、六兄幼舆以及乔卿、允臧诸兄弟神道碑。作品：《允臧碑》《唐国子司业颜允南碑》《颜乔卿碣》《颜幼舆碑》<div id='poem_1366824' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366824' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366824?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故通议大夫行嶭王友柱国赠秘书少监国子祭酒太子少保颜君碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（766年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366824")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366824_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366824'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366824'>昔孔悝有彝鼎之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366824_comment'></div>陆机有祠堂之颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366824_comment'></div>皆所以发挥祖德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366824_comment'></div>敷演家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366824_comment'></div>故君子之观其铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366824_comment'></div>既美其所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366824_comment'></div>又美其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366824_comment'></div>无而称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366824_comment'></div>是诬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366824_comment'></div>有而不述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366824_comment'></div>岂仁乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366824_comment'></div>论而撰之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366824_comment'></div>敢不祗惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366824_comment'></div>君讳惟贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366824_comment'></div>字叔坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366824_comment'></div>其先出于颛顼之孙祝融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366824_comment'></div>融孙安为曹姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366824_comment'></div>其裔邾武公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366824_comment'></div>名夷甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366824_comment'></div>字颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366824_comment'></div>子友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366824_comment'></div>别封郳为小邾子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366824_comment'></div>遂以颜为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366824_comment'></div>多仕鲁为卿大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366824_comment'></div>孔门达者七十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366824_comment'></div>颜氏有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366824_comment'></div>战国有率斶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366824_comment'></div>秦有芝贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366824_comment'></div>汉有异肆安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366824_comment'></div>其后丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366824_comment'></div>谱牒沦亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366824_comment'></div>魏有斐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366824_comment'></div>盛字叔台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366824_comment'></div>青徐二州刺史关内侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366824_comment'></div>始自鲁居于琅琊临沂孝悌里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366824_comment'></div>生广陵太守给事中葛绎贞子讳钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366824_comment'></div>字公若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366824_comment'></div>精韩诗礼易尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366824_comment'></div>学者宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366824_comment'></div>生汝阴太守护军袭葛绎子讳默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366824_comment'></div>字静伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366824_comment'></div>生晋侍中光禄大夫西平靖侯讳含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366824_comment'></div>字宏都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366824_comment'></div>随元帝过江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366824_comment'></div>巳下七叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366824_comment'></div>葬在上元幕府山西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366824_comment'></div>生侍中光禄勋西平定侯讳髦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366824_comment'></div>字君道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366824_comment'></div>事具孝行传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366824_comment'></div>生州西曹骑都尉西平侯讳綝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366824_comment'></div>字文和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366824_comment'></div>生宣城太守御史中丞讳靖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366824_comment'></div>字茂宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366824_comment'></div>生巴陵太守度支校尉讳腾之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366824_comment'></div>字宏道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366824_comment'></div>善草隶书有风格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366824_comment'></div>梁武帝草书评云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366824_comment'></div>颜腾之贺道力并便尺牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366824_comment'></div>少行于代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366824_comment'></div>生辅国江夏王参军讳炳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366824_comment'></div>字叔豹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366824_comment'></div>以能书称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366824_comment'></div>生齐持书御史兼中丞讳见远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366824_comment'></div>字见远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366824_comment'></div>和帝被弑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366824_comment'></div>一恸而绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366824_comment'></div>梁武深恨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366824_comment'></div>事见梁周北齐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366824_comment'></div>生梁镇西记室参军讳协。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366824_comment'></div>字子和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366824_comment'></div>感家门事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366824_comment'></div>义不求闻达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366824_comment'></div>元帝著怀旧诗以伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366824_comment'></div>撰晋仙传五篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366824_comment'></div>日月灾异图两卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366824_comment'></div>文集二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366824_comment'></div>见梁书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366824_comment'></div>生北齐给事黄门侍郎待诏文林馆平原太守隋东宫学士讳之推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366824_comment'></div>字介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366824_comment'></div>著家训二十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366824_comment'></div>冤魂志三卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366824_comment'></div>證俗字音五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366824_comment'></div>文集三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366824_comment'></div>事具本传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366824_comment'></div>黄门兄之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366824_comment'></div>周御正御史中大夫麟趾学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366824_comment'></div>隋文辅政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366824_comment'></div>不署矫诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366824_comment'></div>索玺又拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366824_comment'></div>出为集州刺史新野公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366824_comment'></div>后朝朔望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366824_comment'></div>引之御榻曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366824_comment'></div>见危授命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366824_comment'></div>临大节而不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366824_comment'></div>古人所重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366824_comment'></div>何以加卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366824_comment'></div>事具周书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366824_comment'></div>弟之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366824_comment'></div>隋叶令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366824_comment'></div>子孙见于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366824_comment'></div>黄门生皇秦王记室讳思鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366824_comment'></div>悯楚游秦小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366824_comment'></div>记室字孔归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366824_comment'></div>君之曾祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366824_comment'></div>隋司经校书东宫学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366824_comment'></div>率子弟奉迎义旗于长春宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366824_comment'></div>招瓜州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366824_comment'></div>拜仪同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366824_comment'></div>博学善属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366824_comment'></div>自为父集序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366824_comment'></div>国史称温大雅在隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366824_comment'></div>与思鲁同事东宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366824_comment'></div>彦博与悯楚同直内史省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366824_comment'></div>彦将时与游秦同典校秘阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366824_comment'></div>二家兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366824_comment'></div>各为一时人物之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366824_comment'></div>少时学业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366824_comment'></div>颜氏为优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366824_comment'></div>其后职位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366824_comment'></div>温氏为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366824_comment'></div>温氏谱亦载焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366824_comment'></div>生勤礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366824_comment'></div>字敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366824_comment'></div>君之祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366824_comment'></div>幼而朗悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366824_comment'></div>识量宏远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366824_comment'></div>工于篆籀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366824_comment'></div>尤精诂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366824_comment'></div>解褐校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366824_comment'></div>与两兄弟师古相时同时为宏文崇贤学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366824_comment'></div>弟育德又于司经校定经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366824_comment'></div>当代荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366824_comment'></div>太宗尝令师古赞崇贤学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366824_comment'></div>以兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366824_comment'></div>特命萧钧赞之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366824_comment'></div>依仁服义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366824_comment'></div>怀文守一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366824_comment'></div>履道自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366824_comment'></div>下帷终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366824_comment'></div>德彰素里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366824_comment'></div>行成兰室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366824_comment'></div>鹤钥驰誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366824_comment'></div>龙楼委质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366824_comment'></div>著作郎修国史夔府长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366824_comment'></div>赠虢州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366824_comment'></div>生昭甫敬仲殆庶无恤少连务滋辟强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366824_comment'></div>昭甫字周卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366824_comment'></div>君之父也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366824_comment'></div>幼而颖悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366824_comment'></div>尤明诂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366824_comment'></div>工篆籀草隶书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366824_comment'></div>与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_151_1366824", 1366824, "Clauses/151/Comments/0")'>内弟</span>殷仲容齐名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366824_comment'></div>而劲利过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366824_comment'></div>特为伯父师古所赏重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366824_comment'></div>每有著述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366824_comment'></div>必令参定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366824_comment'></div>尝得古鼎二十馀字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366824_comment'></div>举朝莫识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366824_comment'></div>尽能读之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366824_comment'></div>高宗侍读曹王属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366824_comment'></div>赠华州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366824_comment'></div>真卿表谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366824_comment'></div>肃宗批答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366824_comment'></div>卿之乃祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366824_comment'></div>当为硕儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366824_comment'></div>既高倚相之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366824_comment'></div>遂有臧孙之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366824_comment'></div>不坠其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366824_comment'></div>在卿之门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366824_comment'></div>生我伯父讳元孙暨君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366824_comment'></div>伯父聪颖绝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366824_comment'></div>尤工文翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366824_comment'></div>举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366824_comment'></div>考功郎刘奇特标榜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366824_comment'></div>由是名动海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366824_comment'></div>累迁太子舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366824_comment'></div>玄宗监国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366824_comment'></div>专掌令画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1366824_comment'></div>尝和游苑诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1366824_comment'></div>批云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1366824_comment'></div>孔门称哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1366824_comment'></div>宋室闻贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1366824_comment'></div>翰墨云捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1366824_comment'></div>莫之与先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1366824_comment'></div>历滁沂濠三州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1366824_comment'></div>赠秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1366824_comment'></div>君仁孝友悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1366824_comment'></div>少孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1366824_comment'></div>育舅殷仲容氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1366824_comment'></div>蒙教笔法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1366824_comment'></div>家贫无纸笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1366824_comment'></div>与兄以黄土扫壁本石画而习之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1366824_comment'></div>故特以草隶擅名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1366824_comment'></div>天授元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1366824_comment'></div>糊名考试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1366824_comment'></div>判入高等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1366824_comment'></div>以亲累授衢州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1366824_comment'></div>与盈川令杨炯信安尉桓彦范相得甚欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1366824_comment'></div>又选授洛州温县永昌二尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1366824_comment'></div>每选皆判入高科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1366824_comment'></div>侍郎苏味道以所试示介众曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1366824_comment'></div>选人中乃有如此书判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1366824_comment'></div>嗟叹久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1366824_comment'></div>遂代兄为长安尉太子文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1366824_comment'></div>以清白五为察访使魏奉古等所荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1366824_comment'></div>五邸初开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1366824_comment'></div>盛选僚属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1366824_comment'></div>拜嶭王友柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1366824_comment'></div>伯姊御史大夫张知泰妻鲁郡夫人亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1366824_comment'></div>将葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1366824_comment'></div>数家占君不利临圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1366824_comment'></div>君哭而拒之曰。<div class='inline'
