class='inline' id='poem_sentence_565_1366824_comment'></div>垂无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_566_1366824_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年</a>　抚州刺史任上，因殿中侍御史徐縯之请，为其父徐秀撰神道碑志述之。作品：《朝议大夫徐秀神道碑》<div id='poem_1366838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝议大夫赠梁州都督上柱国徐府君神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（770年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366838")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366838'>自古遭圣明而功不立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366838_comment'></div>都卿相而名不称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366838_comment'></div>盖有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366838_comment'></div>其或荷丕搆而继志不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366838_comment'></div>在下位而能伸其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366838_comment'></div>克扬前烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366838_comment'></div>以承后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366838_comment'></div>其唯徐君乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366838_comment'></div>君讳秀<span class='inlineComment2'>（唐书宰相世系表作琇）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366838_comment'></div>东海郯人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366838_comment'></div>其先出于伯益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366838_comment'></div>实掌舜虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366838_comment'></div>裔孙偃王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366838_comment'></div>躬行仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366838_comment'></div>遂因国命氏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366838_comment'></div>厥后乐以文侍金门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366838_comment'></div>稚以礼优尘榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366838_comment'></div>仙人寄傲于贤圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366838_comment'></div>伟长首冠于应刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366838_comment'></div>英达相仍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366838_comment'></div>有自来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366838_comment'></div>宋有中书侍郎逵之司空羡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366838_comment'></div>兄秘书监钦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366838_comment'></div>钦之子尚书仆射中书令湛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366838_comment'></div>湛之生黄门侍郎聿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366838_comment'></div>聿之生齐太尉孝嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366838_comment'></div>孝嗣生梁侍中绲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366838_comment'></div>绲生陈五兵尚书君敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366838_comment'></div>君敕生丹阳尹温。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366838_comment'></div>自司空巳还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366838_comment'></div>四为上公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366838_comment'></div>五降帝女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366838_comment'></div>尹生隋民部侍郎唐赠秘书监讳恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366838_comment'></div>监生金紫光禄大夫右散骑常侍兼礼部尚书讳筠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366838_comment'></div>尚书生库部郎中万年令太子詹事讳昕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366838_comment'></div>皆以盛德济美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366838_comment'></div>垂于世家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366838_comment'></div>君即詹事第三子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366838_comment'></div>幼而聪悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366838_comment'></div>笃学能属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366838_comment'></div>事继亲以孝称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366838_comment'></div>十馀岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366838_comment'></div>父友凤阁侍郎姚元崇示君五百字诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366838_comment'></div>一览便诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366838_comment'></div>姚公奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366838_comment'></div>因谓纳言狄公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366838_comment'></div>徐子珠华玉洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366838_comment'></div>后但不知命何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366838_comment'></div>年十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366838_comment'></div>为崇文生应举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366838_comment'></div>考功员外郎沈佺期再试东堂壁画赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366838_comment'></div>公援翰立成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366838_comment'></div>沈公骇异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366838_comment'></div>遂擢高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366838_comment'></div>调补幽都县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366838_comment'></div>充相国尚书赵彦昭朔方节度判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366838_comment'></div>以事去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366838_comment'></div>又历蔡州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366838_comment'></div>为御史宋遥关内覆囚判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366838_comment'></div>公锐精鞫讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366838_comment'></div>多所全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366838_comment'></div>宋公以为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366838_comment'></div>公正色谓之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366838_comment'></div>仆从祖父司刑卿天授中<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1366838", 1366838, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>详理</span>冤狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366838_comment'></div>振雪者七十馀家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366838_comment'></div>今子孙犹困于襄陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366838_comment'></div>岂忍以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1366838", 1366838, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>束湿</span>之事以自便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366838_comment'></div>因顿首请去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366838_comment'></div>宋谢而留之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366838_comment'></div>无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366838_comment'></div>或讼冤于执事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366838_comment'></div>召公问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366838_comment'></div>则他判官之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366838_comment'></div>宋欲别白旌公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366838_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366838_comment'></div>仆虽不材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366838_comment'></div>岂可藉人之过以为巳功乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366838_comment'></div>论者休之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366838_comment'></div>户部侍郎徐知仁请为招慰南蛮判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366838_comment'></div>奏课居最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366838_comment'></div>转瀛州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366838_comment'></div>侍御史赵颐贞辟宣慰判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366838_comment'></div>历湖州德清长城润州丹阳三县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366838_comment'></div>天宝二载春二月加朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366838_comment'></div>敕摄新安郡别驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366838_comment'></div>采访使齐浣梁升卿并奏为判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366838_comment'></div>六载秋七月拜临淮郡长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366838_comment'></div>加朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366838_comment'></div>九载夏四月除济南郡司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366838_comment'></div>加朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366838_comment'></div>十二载春三月拜信都郡长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366838_comment'></div>不幸感疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366838_comment'></div>天宝十三载秋七月九日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366838_comment'></div>终于郡之官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366838_comment'></div>春秋七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366838_comment'></div>公先世茔垄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366838_comment'></div>宅于京师少陵原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366838_comment'></div>詹事府君巡按河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366838_comment'></div>薨于洛汭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366838_comment'></div>因葬于缑氏县西南大寇原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366838_comment'></div>公启手足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366838_comment'></div>顾命其子今侍御史演曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366838_comment'></div>吾家代俭约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366838_comment'></div>不欲华众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366838_comment'></div>归全之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366838_comment'></div>其以布车一乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366838_comment'></div>虔祔先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366838_comment'></div>演泣而奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366838_comment'></div>及其葬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366838_comment'></div>茔小无便地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366838_comment'></div>于次东马鞍山下得紫龙饮乳冈之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366838_comment'></div>龟筮从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366838_comment'></div>夫人南阳县君樊氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366838_comment'></div>户部尚书子盖之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366838_comment'></div>袁州刺史文器之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366838_comment'></div>庐江太守季节之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366838_comment'></div>仁孝柔明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366838_comment'></div>娴于礼度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366838_comment'></div>左右图史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366838_comment'></div>雅善琴棋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366838_comment'></div>中外孤弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366838_comment'></div>躬自收视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366838_comment'></div>俾夫远近咸怀安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366838_comment'></div>春秋六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366838_comment'></div>弃堂帐于相州之安阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366838_comment'></div>天宝十五载秋八月十有四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366838_comment'></div>爰遵周公之典而合祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366838_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366838_comment'></div>广德二年春二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366838_comment'></div>皇帝有事于南郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366838_comment'></div>追赠君都督梁州诸军事梁州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366838_comment'></div>夫人南阳郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366838_comment'></div>盖以演簪白笔于赤墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366838_comment'></div>董材赋于巴汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366838_comment'></div>是用有永锡之宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366838_comment'></div>纡褒崇之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366838_comment'></div>哀荣之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366838_comment'></div>不其至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366838_comment'></div>君凡四为纲佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366838_comment'></div>六奉使轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366838_comment'></div>所至之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366838_comment'></div>必闻异绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366838_comment'></div>举天下之政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366838_comment'></div>莫不资折中焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366838_comment'></div>性嗜清贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366838_comment'></div>室无长物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366838_comment'></div>孤茕丛萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366838_comment'></div>皆仰于君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366838_comment'></div>既婴沈痼之疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366838_comment'></div>绵历三载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366838_comment'></div>演请就上国之医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366838_comment'></div>庶其逢吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366838_comment'></div>君曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366838_comment'></div>阖门之资者寸禄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366838_comment'></div>今疾剧命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366838_comment'></div>吾不以一身易百口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366838_comment'></div>竟不从而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366838_comment'></div>识者哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366838_comment'></div>或谓君曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366838_comment'></div>君奉养嫠姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366838_comment'></div>用度万钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366838_comment'></div>□粻诸姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366838_comment'></div>缣才五两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366838_comment'></div>姑见君□□□笑而不答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366838_comment'></div>退谓演曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366838_comment'></div>吾见其抚孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366838_comment'></div>不见其怨德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366838_comment'></div>教义之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366838_comment'></div>有以见其用心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366838_comment'></div>君恬淡寡欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366838_comment'></div>雅好摄生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366838_comment'></div>在新安或指灵叟于洞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366838_comment'></div>君斋心四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366838_comment'></div>冞入其阻而后觌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366838_comment'></div>讯其由来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366838_comment'></div>陈思王东阁祭酒蒋觊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366838_comment'></div>说魏时事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366838_comment'></div>历历可听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1366838_comment'></div>君稽首而蕲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1366838_comment'></div>叟曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1366838_comment'></div>从我乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1366838_comment'></div>必可度世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1366838_comment'></div>君以王事靡盬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1366838_comment'></div>退而辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1366838_comment'></div>比回顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1366838_comment'></div>则为茅草矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1366838_comment'></div>初君上计济南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1366838_comment'></div>展群祖之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1366838_comment'></div>松槚森然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1366838_comment'></div>徽猷莫纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1366838_comment'></div>留居论撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1366838_comment'></div>时日以成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1366838_comment'></div>先德之不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1366838_comment'></div>繄是举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1366838_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1366838_comment'></div>君体聪颖之上姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1366838_comment'></div>恬旷之夷度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1366838_comment'></div>宽明足以济众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1366838_comment'></div>和义足以长人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1366838_comment'></div>口绝莠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1366838_comment'></div>目无还视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1366838_comment'></div>立身先张仲之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1366838_comment'></div>与朋服子路之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1366838_comment'></div>内行可以质神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1366838_comment'></div>清规可以励风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1366838_comment'></div>宜克享<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_205_1366838", 1366838, "Clauses/205/Comments/0")'>胡耇</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1366838_comment'></div>荷天之龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1366838_comment'></div>光辅乎汉之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1366838_comment'></div>高视乎周之列位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1366838_comment'></div>而道之将丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1366838_comment'></div>命不偶时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1366838_comment'></div>屈舆骥于身前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1366838_comment'></div>堕岘碑于殁后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1366838_comment'></div>吁足叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1366838_comment'></div>春秋贵九世卿族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1366838_comment'></div>汉史称七叶珥貂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1366838_comment'></div>陪臣于下士卑僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1366838_comment'></div>绝属于天潢戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1366838_comment'></div>岂比夫登台者四世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1366838_comment'></div>尚主者五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1366838_comment'></div>焜耀于数朝之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1366838_comment'></div>蝉联于百代之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1366838_comment'></div>可同年而语矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1366838_comment'></div>演懿文懋学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1366838_comment'></div>峻节清标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1366838_comment'></div>天宝末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1366838_comment'></div>陷居贼中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1366838_comment'></div>为伪命连辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1366838_comment'></div>辞疾不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1366838_comment'></div>谋使家人与本朝通计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1366838_comment'></div>为部曲所发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1366838_comment'></div>遂遭禁诘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1366838_comment'></div>一日之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1366838_comment'></div>议刑者数焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1366838_comment'></div>俄而官军大至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1366838_comment'></div>贼党奔北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1366838_comment'></div>由是获免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1366838_comment'></div>乾元中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1366838_comment'></div>奉使巴渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1366838_comment'></div>属段子璋搆逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1366838_comment'></div>流辈十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1366838_comment'></div>皆被屠害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1366838_comment'></div>以演高名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1366838_comment'></div>欲留同恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1366838_comment'></div>期之以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1366838_comment'></div>承剑不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1366838_comment'></div>时诸道徵求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1366838_comment'></div>人不堪命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1366838_comment'></div>演至之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1366838_comment'></div>必荷仁信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1366838_comment'></div>如期而毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1366838_comment'></div>则□□□将崇必复之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1366838_comment'></div>宁止当朝之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1366838_comment'></div>碑铭功伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1366838_comment'></div>敢坠斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1366838_comment'></div>其辞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1366838_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_256_1366838'>益为帝虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1366838_comment'></div>偃不异途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1366838_comment'></div>世表东海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1366838_comment'></div>其惟徐乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1366838_comment'></div>或文或武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1366838_comment'></div>或哲或儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1366838_comment'></div>休美后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1366838_comment'></div>厥德不孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1366838_comment'></div>猗那都督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1366838_comment'></div>克懋远图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1366838_comment'></div>邦国四佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1366838_comment'></div>輶轩六徂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1366838_comment'></div>树声长世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1366838_comment'></div>与道为徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1366838_comment'></div>爰觌幽光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1366838_comment'></div>无宁集枯<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙八字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1366838_comment'></div>仁义都尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1366838_comment'></div>彭殇曷殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1366838_comment'></div>所嗟人纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1366838_comment'></div>莫展嘉谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1366838_comment'></div>马鞍山北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1366838_comment'></div>龙乳冈隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1366838_comment'></div>于焉崇祔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1366838_comment'></div>先志靡渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1366838_comment'></div>丰碑崔嵬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1366838_comment'></div>宰树萦纡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1366838_comment'></div>□沾濡□。</div><div id='poem_sentence_282_1366838_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1366838'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_34_1366838_0'>⑴ 宰相世系表云孝嗣生齐侍中绲绲生陈常侍君敷君敷生隋通事舍人荣荣生尚食直长恕恕生春官尚书枝江公筠筠生昕</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1366838_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年4月</a>　本月，为道士谭仙岩书马伏波语。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年5月</a>　本月，为舅氏殷践猷及其子殷摄撰写神道碑铭志述之,并于州采石,正书铭刻,遣使立之于河南新安墓田。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年</a>　为姑表兄弟前抚州刺史张景佚撰书清德颂，立石于城郭。作品：《张景倩清德碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年12月</a>　因宋俨之请为玄宗朝名宰相宋璟撰写神道碑铭。作品：《宋璟碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=770&endYear=770')">770年</a>　在抚州，有崇仁令元子哲遗爱颂。作品：《崇仁令元子哲遗爱颂》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　谢灵运翻经台因观察使魏少游奏请,改宝应寺。至是,修缮一新,律藏院戒坛亦创建竣工,因寺僧智融所请,颜真卿撰文且书以志之。作品：《抚州宝应寺律藏院戎坛记》<div id='poem_1366794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州宝应寺律藏院戒坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366794")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366794'>如来以身口意三业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366794_comment'></div>难调伏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366794_comment'></div>净尸罗以息其内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366794_comment'></div>行住坐卧四威仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366794_comment'></div>摄善心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366794_comment'></div>明布萨以昭其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366794_comment'></div>故曰波罗提木义是汝之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366794_comment'></div>则憍陈如之善来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366794_comment'></div>迦叶波之尚法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366794_comment'></div>诸声闻三归约众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366794_comment'></div>十四年以八敬度尼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366794_comment'></div>羯磨相承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366794_comment'></div>其致一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366794_comment'></div>至汉灵帝建宁元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366794_comment'></div>有北天竺五桑门支法领等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366794_comment'></div>始于长安译出四分戒本兼羯磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366794_comment'></div>与大僧受戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366794_comment'></div>至曹魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366794_comment'></div>有天竺十尼自远而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366794_comment'></div>为尼受具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366794_comment'></div>后秦姚苌宏始十一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366794_comment'></div>有梵僧佛陀耶舍译出四分律本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366794_comment'></div>而关内先行僧祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366794_comment'></div>江南盛行十诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366794_comment'></div>至元魏法聪律师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366794_comment'></div>始阐四分之宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366794_comment'></div>聪传道覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366794_comment'></div>覆传惠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366794_comment'></div>光传云晖愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366794_comment'></div>愿传理隐乐洪云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366794_comment'></div>云传遵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366794_comment'></div>遵传智首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366794_comment'></div>首传道宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366794_comment'></div>宣传洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366794_comment'></div>洪传法励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366794_comment'></div>励传满意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366794_comment'></div>意传法成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366794_comment'></div>成传大亮道宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366794_comment'></div>亮传云一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366794_comment'></div>宾传岸超慧澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366794_comment'></div>澄传慧钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366794_comment'></div>皆口相授受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366794_comment'></div>臻于壸奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366794_comment'></div>钦俗姓徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366794_comment'></div>洪州建昌人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366794_comment'></div>盖汉孺子之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366794_comment'></div>二十二寻师于临川楮山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366794_comment'></div>后五岁削发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366794_comment'></div>隶于高安龙冈寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366794_comment'></div>遂受戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366794_comment'></div>有唐义净则译经上足曰洪州灵杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366794_comment'></div>其秉宣羯磨者曰两京清涤使法慧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366794_comment'></div>钦智度冲深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366794_comment'></div>神用高爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366794_comment'></div>行无权实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366794_comment'></div>身绝开遮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366794_comment'></div>阐律藏而日月光明骋辩才而龙象蹴踏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366794_comment'></div>江岭之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366794_comment'></div>凛然风生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366794_comment'></div>开元末北游京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366794_comment'></div>充东京福先大德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366794_comment'></div>常诵大涅槃经而讲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366794_comment'></div>兼明俱舍论维摩金刚经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366794_comment'></div>每登讲座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366794_comment'></div>其下日有二三千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366794_comment'></div>由是名动辇毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366794_comment'></div>属禄山作乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366794_comment'></div>杖锡南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366794_comment'></div>居于西山洪井双岭之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366794_comment'></div>慕高僧观显之遗踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366794_comment'></div>于寺北创置兰若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366794_comment'></div>山泉之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366794_comment'></div>颇极幽绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366794_comment'></div>钦虽坚持律仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366794_comment'></div>而志在宏济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366794_comment'></div>好读周易左传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366794_comment'></div>下笔成章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366794_comment'></div>著律仪辅演十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366794_comment'></div>尝撰本州龙兴寺戒坛碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366794_comment'></div>颇见称于作者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366794_comment'></div>大历三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366794_comment'></div>真卿忝刺抚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366794_comment'></div>东南四里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366794_comment'></div>有宋侍中临川内史谢灵运翻大涅槃经古台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366794_comment'></div>阶扃俨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366794_comment'></div>轩构摧圯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366794_comment'></div>有高行头陀僧智清者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366794_comment'></div>首事修葺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366794_comment'></div>安居住持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366794_comment'></div>明年秋七月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366794_comment'></div>真卿绩秩将满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366794_comment'></div>有观察使尚书御史大夫赵国魏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366794_comment'></div>愿以我皇帝降诞之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366794_comment'></div>奏为宝应寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366794_comment'></div>仍请山林高行僧三七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366794_comment'></div>冬十月二十三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366794_comment'></div>圣恩允许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366794_comment'></div>于是鼎新轮奂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366794_comment'></div>其兴也勃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366794_comment'></div>乃请止观大师法源法泉襄阳乘觉清源善宏罗浮圆觉佛迹十喻馀杭慧达暨当州海通海岸等同住董修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366794_comment'></div>以资景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366794_comment'></div>佥以为学徒虽增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366794_comment'></div>毗尼未立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366794_comment'></div>明年三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366794_comment'></div>乃请钦登坛而董振铎焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366794_comment'></div>仍俾龙冈道干天台法裔招提智融白马法允衡岳正觉同德义盈香城藏选龙兴藏志开元明彻等同秉法事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366794_comment'></div>于是远近骏奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366794_comment'></div>道场侧塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366794_comment'></div>圣像放光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366794_comment'></div>而龙王不雨者四旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366794_comment'></div>僧尼等三百五十七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366794_comment'></div>而文士正议大夫前卫尉少卿张廷皋脱俗归真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366794_comment'></div>其名曰瑰纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366794_comment'></div>为称首焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366794_comment'></div>又钦比年以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366794_comment'></div>为受具者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366794_comment'></div>凡一万馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366794_comment'></div>江岭湖海之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366794_comment'></div>幅员千馀里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366794_comment'></div>像法于变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366794_comment'></div>此皆钦教道之力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366794_comment'></div>临川在岭隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366794_comment'></div>未尝宏律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366794_comment'></div>于是二众三百馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366794_comment'></div>请法裔敷演而依止之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366794_comment'></div>复有上都资圣寺高德曰还本律主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366794_comment'></div>伟兹能辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366794_comment'></div>深嗟叹而赞美之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366794_comment'></div>请于寺东南置普通无碍禅院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366794_comment'></div>院内立镇海观音道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366794_comment'></div>请善宏居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366794_comment'></div>以开悟心要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366794_comment'></div>云一上足曰智融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366794_comment'></div>精持本事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366794_comment'></div>如会尊众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366794_comment'></div>乃命智光等于普通道场东置律藏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366794_comment'></div>创立戒坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366794_comment'></div>以伫钦公之来仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366794_comment'></div>且施肇纪之不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366794_comment'></div>经营未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366794_comment'></div>坛殿郁兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366794_comment'></div>庶乎渡海浮囊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366794_comment'></div>分毫绝罗刹之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366794_comment'></div>严身璎珞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366794_comment'></div>照耀有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_144_1366794", 1366794, "Clauses/144/Comments/0")'>摩尼</span>之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366794_comment'></div>则入佛位而披伽梨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366794_comment'></div>名香普薰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366794_comment'></div>神足无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366794_comment'></div>其可胜纪而芜绝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366794_comment'></div>有唐大历辛亥岁春三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366794_comment'></div>行抚州刺史鲁郡开国公颜真卿书而志之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_150_1366794_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年4月</a>　本月，在抚州，有南城县麻姑山仙坛记。作品：《抚州南城县麻姑山仙坛记》<div id='poem_1366795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>抚州南城县麻姑山仙坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366795")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366795'>麻姑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366795_comment'></div>葛稚川神仙传云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366795_comment'></div>王远字方平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366795_comment'></div>欲东之括苍山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366795_comment'></div>过吴蔡经家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366795_comment'></div>教其尸解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366795_comment'></div>如蛇蝉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366795_comment'></div>经去十馀年忽还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366795_comment'></div>语家人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366795_comment'></div>七月七日王君当来过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366795_comment'></div>到期日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366795_comment'></div>方平乘羽车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366795_comment'></div>驾五龙各异色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366795_comment'></div>旌旗导从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366795_comment'></div>威仪赫奕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366795_comment'></div>如大将也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366795_comment'></div>既至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366795_comment'></div>坐须臾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366795_comment'></div>引见经父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366795_comment'></div>因遣人与麻姑相闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366795_comment'></div>亦莫知麻姑是何神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366795_comment'></div>言王方平敬报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366795_comment'></div>久不行民间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366795_comment'></div>今来在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366795_comment'></div>想麻姑能暂来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366795_comment'></div>有顷信还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366795_comment'></div>但闻其语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366795_comment'></div>不见所使人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366795_comment'></div>曰麻姑再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366795_comment'></div>不见忽已五百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366795_comment'></div>尊卑有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366795_comment'></div>修敬无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366795_comment'></div>思念久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366795_comment'></div>烦信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366795_comment'></div>承在彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366795_comment'></div>登山颠倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366795_comment'></div>而先被记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366795_comment'></div>当按行蓬莱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366795_comment'></div>今便暂往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366795_comment'></div>如是便还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366795_comment'></div>还即亲观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366795_comment'></div>愿不即去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366795_comment'></div>如此两时间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366795_comment'></div>来时不先闻人马声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366795_comment'></div>既至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366795_comment'></div>从官当半于方平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366795_comment'></div>蔡经亦举家见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366795_comment'></div>是好女子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366795_comment'></div>年十八九许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366795_comment'></div>顶中作髻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366795_comment'></div>馀发垂之至腰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366795_comment'></div>其衣有文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366795_comment'></div>而非锦绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366795_comment'></div>光彩耀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366795_comment'></div>不可名字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366795_comment'></div>皆世所无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366795_comment'></div>得见方平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366795_comment'></div>方平为起立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366795_comment'></div>坐定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366795_comment'></div>各进行厨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366795_comment'></div>金盘玉杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366795_comment'></div>无限美膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366795_comment'></div>多是诸华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366795_comment'></div>而香气达于内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366795_comment'></div>擗麟脯行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑自言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366795_comment'></div>接待以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366795_comment'></div>见东海三为桑田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366795_comment'></div>向间蓬莱水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366795_comment'></div>乃浅于往者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366795_comment'></div>会时略半也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366795_comment'></div>岂将复还为陆陵乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366795_comment'></div>方平笑曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366795_comment'></div>圣人皆言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366795_comment'></div>海中行复扬尘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑欲见蔡经母及妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366795_comment'></div>经弟妇新产数十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑望见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366795_comment'></div>已知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366795_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366795_comment'></div>噫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366795_comment'></div>且止勿前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366795_comment'></div>即求少许米。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366795_comment'></div>便以掷之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366795_comment'></div>堕地即成丹沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366795_comment'></div>方平笑曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366795_comment'></div>姑故年少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366795_comment'></div>吾了不喜复作此曹狡狯变化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑手似鸟爪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366795_comment'></div>蔡经心中念言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366795_comment'></div>背蛘时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366795_comment'></div>得此爪以杷背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366795_comment'></div>乃佳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366795_comment'></div>方平即知经心中念言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366795_comment'></div>即使人牵经鞭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366795_comment'></div>曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366795_comment'></div>麻姑者神人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366795_comment'></div>汝何忽谓其爪可以杷背邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366795_comment'></div>见鞭著经背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366795_comment'></div>亦不见有人持鞭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366795_comment'></div>方平告经曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366795_comment'></div>吾鞭不可妄得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366795_comment'></div>大历三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366795_comment'></div>真卿刺抚州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366795_comment'></div>按图经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366795_comment'></div>南城县有麻姑山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366795_comment'></div>顶有古坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366795_comment'></div>相传云麻姑于此得道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366795_comment'></div>坛东南有池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366795_comment'></div>中有红莲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366795_comment'></div>近忽变碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366795_comment'></div>今又白矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366795_comment'></div>池北下坛傍有杉松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366795_comment'></div>松皆偃盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366795_comment'></div>时闻步虚钟磬之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366795_comment'></div>东南有瀑布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366795_comment'></div>淙下三百馀尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366795_comment'></div>东北有石崇观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366795_comment'></div>高石中犹有螺蚌壳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366795_comment'></div>或以为桑田所变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366795_comment'></div>西北有麻源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366795_comment'></div>谢灵运诗题入华子冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366795_comment'></div>是麻源第三谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366795_comment'></div>恐其处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366795_comment'></div>源口有神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366795_comment'></div>祈雨辄应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366795_comment'></div>开元中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366795_comment'></div>道士邓紫阳于此习道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366795_comment'></div>蒙召入大同殿修功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366795_comment'></div>二十七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366795_comment'></div>忽见虎驾龙车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366795_comment'></div>二人执节于庭中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366795_comment'></div>顾谓其友竹务猷曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366795_comment'></div>此迎我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366795_comment'></div>可为吾奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366795_comment'></div>愿欲归葬本山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366795_comment'></div>仍请立庙于坛侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366795_comment'></div>玄宗从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366795_comment'></div>天宝五载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366795_comment'></div>投龙于瀑布。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366795_comment'></div>石池中有黄龙见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366795_comment'></div>玄宗感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366795_comment'></div>乃命增修仙宇真仪侍从云鹤之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366795_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366795_comment'></div>自麻姑发迹于兹岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366795_comment'></div>南真遗坛于龟源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366795_comment'></div>华姑表异于井山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366795_comment'></div>今女道士黎琼仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366795_comment'></div>年八十而容色益少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366795_comment'></div>曾妙行梦琼仙而餐花绝粒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366795_comment'></div>紫阳侄男曰德诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366795_comment'></div>继修香火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366795_comment'></div>弟子谭仙岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366795_comment'></div>法箓尊严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366795_comment'></div>而史元洞左通元邹郁华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366795_comment'></div>皆清虚服道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366795_comment'></div>非天地气殊异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366795_comment'></div>江山炳灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366795_comment'></div>则曷由纂懿流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366795_comment'></div>若斯之盛者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366795_comment'></div>真卿幸承馀烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366795_comment'></div>敢刻金石而志之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366795_comment'></div>时则六年夏四月也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_164_1366795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年6月</a>　本月，正书旧友容州刺史、本管经略使元结《大唐中兴颂》，立石于祁阳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　同时，撰有碑文，韩择木隶书，代宗篆额。作品：《慈恩寺常住庄地碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　抚州任上，与秀才左辅元、姜如璧诸人，增广《韵海镜源》，成书五百卷。<br /><a href="javascript: -----title
溧水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e02f6c52742c4dada3dc1d59edb1ce41_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e02f6c52742c4dada3dc1d59edb1ce41");'><span id='e02f6c52742c4dada3dc1d59edb1ce41_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>，63岁</div><div id='e02f6c52742c4dada3dc1d59edb1ce41' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　经溧水古烈士左伯桃墓，题旧诗于蒲塘与江州蒲塘同名，遂撰文辨之。作品：《蒲塘辨》<div id='poem_1366810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒲塘辨</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366810")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366810'>土俗所呼博浅水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366810_comment'></div>浦与敷音转尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366810_comment'></div>南有博阳山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366810_comment'></div>土人呼为濮阳山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366810_comment'></div>濮博声讹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366810_comment'></div>水北有历下村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366810_comment'></div>疑古历陵也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1366810_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eb32005c5f1144d59e11e91df32affc2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eb32005c5f1144d59e11e91df32affc2");'><span id='eb32005c5f1144d59e11e91df32affc2_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年</a>　经湖州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='46ddc73092774c7296e9730a9dc5d89a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("46ddc73092774c7296e9730a9dc5d89a");'><span id='46ddc73092774c7296e9730a9dc5d89a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=777')">773-777年</a>，65-69岁</div><div id='46ddc73092774c7296e9730a9dc5d89a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年1月</a>　正月，至任湖州，先后以杭州富阳丞李萼为本州防御副使，前校书郎权器、前大理司直杨昱为判官，委以州事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　于柳家寺造访游龙兴寺诗僧皎然。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　立春后四十五日，例入顾渚山贡茶院主事贡茶事，至谷雨日还郡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　春仲，登临岘山，与皎然及名士陆羽等赋诗联句，有诗并序。作品：《登岘山观李左相石樽联句》<div id='poem_51066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51066' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年10月</a>　至十月，徙修于杼山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　陪同袁高、皎然诸人上骆驼桥玩月，登开元寺观碑。有碑文。作品：《文殊师利菩萨碑》<div id='poem_1366780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文殊帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（773年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366780")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366780'>近作一文殊师利菩萨碑。但欲发扬主上圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366780_comment'></div>盖不近文律耳。今奉呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366780_comment'></div>充<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1366780", 1366780, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>盖酱</span>之用可乎。真卿白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366780_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1366780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　陪同袁高、皎然诸人上骆驼桥玩月，登开元寺观碑。有帖。作品：《文殊帖》<div id='poem_1366780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文殊帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（773年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366780")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366780'>近作一文殊师利菩萨碑。但欲发扬主上圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366780_comment'></div>盖不近文律耳。今奉呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366780_comment'></div>充<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1366780", 1366780, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>盖酱</span>之用可乎。真卿白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366780_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1366780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年12月</a>　十二月，姻亲沈怡新立南齐沈驎士述祖德碑，为之撰书，立石德清沈氏先茔。作品：《吴兴沈氏述祖德记》<div id='poem_1366797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴兴沈氏述祖德记</a><span class='authorDate'>（773年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366797")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366797'>南齐徵士吴兴沈君。名驎士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366797_comment'></div>郡人也。蕴道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366797_comment'></div>晦于邑之馀不溪。家贫无资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366797_comment'></div>以织帘为业。故时人号为织帘先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366797_comment'></div>精于礼传。尝自诂训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366797_comment'></div>宗人吏部郎中渊中书郎约累荐。徵为著作郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366797_comment'></div>高卧不起。名重江表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366797_comment'></div>临终遗教。依皇甫元晏棺中贮孝经一卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366797_comment'></div>穿圹三尺。置棺平土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366797_comment'></div>不设机位。四时地席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366797_comment'></div>元酒而奠。子彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366797_comment'></div>奉而行之。吴郡陆惠晓张融皆为之诔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366797_comment'></div>徵士尝制述祖德碑。立于金鹅山之先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366797_comment'></div>年月淹远。风雨蠹蚀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366797_comment'></div>朽字残文。翳而莫分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366797_comment'></div>乾元中。为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1366797", 1366797, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>盗火</span>所焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366797_comment'></div>碑首毁裂。嵚然将堕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366797_comment'></div>过江二十叶孙御史中丞震。移牒郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366797_comment'></div>请其封葺。或属兵凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366797_comment'></div>旷而莫修。忽有仆树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366797_comment'></div>生于龟腹。盘根抱趾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366797_comment'></div>耸干夹碑。嶷如工造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366797_comment'></div>郁若神化。欹者复正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366797_comment'></div>危而再坚。夫德无名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366797_comment'></div>遇贤而钟庆。神无质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366797_comment'></div>假物以申应。沈氏积善既远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366797_comment'></div>徵士植德既深。天将兴旧族乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366797_comment'></div>吾知沈之复大也。权检校宗事十九叶孙前太庙斋郎怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366797_comment'></div>拜泣松槚。增修旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366797_comment'></div>感先碑之陨覆。惧遗文之残阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366797_comment'></div>乃具他石。传而贰焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366797_comment'></div>崇其本。所以尊先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366797_comment'></div>建其新。所以嗣德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366797_comment'></div>以真卿江南婚姻之旧。中外伯仲之穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366797_comment'></div>谬忝拜刺。见托斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366797_comment'></div>刊诸碑阴。以传无朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366797_comment'></div>因改其树为庆树。以旌其美焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366797_comment'></div>沈氏之故事。具于家谍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366797_comment'></div>今阙而不纪。时有唐大历八年冬十二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366797_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1366797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年1月7日</a>　此日，正书伯父颜元孙《干禄字书》并序之，立石于刺史宅东厅院。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年1月</a>　本月，立去年秋七月二十五日追建并正书乾元三年所撰之《天下放生池碑》于骆驼桥东。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年3月</a>　春三月,《韵海镜源》修毕,从皎然之请,撰书《妙喜寺碑》志其事。<div id='poem_1366816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州乌程县杼山妙喜寺碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（774年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366816")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366816'>州西南杼山之阳。有妙喜寺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366816_comment'></div>梁武帝之所置也。大同七年夏五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366816_comment'></div>帝御寿光阁。会所司奏请置额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366816_comment'></div>帝以东方有妙喜佛国。因以名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366816_comment'></div>旧置在州西金斗山。唐太宗文皇帝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1366816", 1366816, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>升极</span>之六年春二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366816_comment'></div>移于此山。山高三百尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366816_comment'></div>周回一千二百步。盖昔夏杼南巡之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366816_comment'></div>今山有夏王村。山西北有夏驾山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366816_comment'></div>皆后杼所幸之地也。晋吴兴太守张元之吴兴疏云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366816_comment'></div>乌程有墟名东张。地形高爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366816_comment'></div>山阜四周。即此山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366816_comment'></div>其山胜绝。游者忘归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366816_comment'></div>前代亦名稽留山。寺前二十步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366816_comment'></div>跨涧有黄浦桥。桥南五十步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366816_comment'></div>又有黄浦亭。并宋鲍昭送盛侍郎及庾中郎赋诗之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366816_comment'></div>其水自杼山西南五里黄蘖山出。故号黄浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366816_comment'></div>俗亦名黄蘖涧。即梁光禄卿江淹赋诗之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366816_comment'></div>寺东偏有招隐院。其前堂西厦谓之温阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366816_comment'></div>从草堂东南。屈曲有悬岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366816_comment'></div>径行百步。至吴兴太守何楷钓台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366816_comment'></div>西北五十步。至避它城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366816_comment'></div>按说文云。它蛇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366816_comment'></div>上古患蛇。而相问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366816_comment'></div>得无它乎。盖往古之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366816_comment'></div>筑城以避它也。有处士竟陵子陆羽杼山记所载如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366816_comment'></div>其台殿廊庑。建立年代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366816_comment'></div>并具于记中。大历七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366816_comment'></div>真卿蒙刺是邦。时浙江西观察判官殿中侍御史袁君高巡部至州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366816_comment'></div>会于此土。真卿遂立亭于东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366816_comment'></div>陆处士以癸丑岁冬十月癸卯朔二十一日癸亥建。因名之曰三癸亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366816_comment'></div>西北于丛桂之间创桂棚。左右数百步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366816_comment'></div>有芳林茂树。悉产丹青紫三桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366816_comment'></div>而华叶各异。树桂之有支径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366816_comment'></div>以袁君步焉。因呼为御史径。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366816_comment'></div>真卿自典校时。即考五代祖隋外史府君与法言所定切韵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366816_comment'></div>引说文苍雅诸字书。穷其训解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366816_comment'></div>次以经史子集中两字巳上成句者。广而编之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366816_comment'></div>故曰韵海。以其镜照原本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366816_comment'></div>无所不见。故曰镜源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366816_comment'></div>天宝末。真卿出守平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366816_comment'></div>巳与郡人渤海封绍高筼族弟今太子通事舍人浑等修之。裁成二百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366816_comment'></div>属安禄山作乱。止具四分之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366816_comment'></div>及刺抚州。与州人左辅元姜如璧等增而广之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366816_comment'></div>成五百卷。事物婴扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366816_comment'></div>未遑刊削。大历壬子岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366816_comment'></div>真卿叨刺于湖。公务之隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366816_comment'></div>乃与金陵沙门法海前殿中侍御史李㟧陆羽国子助教州人褚冲评事汤某清河丞太祝柳察长城丞潘述县尉裴循常熟主簿萧存嘉兴尉陆士修后进杨遂初崔宏杨德元胡仲南阳汤涉颜祭韦介左兴宗颜策。以季夏于州学及放生池日相讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366816_comment'></div>至冬。徙于兹山东偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366816_comment'></div>来年春。遂终其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366816_comment'></div>前是颜浑正字殷佐明魏县尉刘茂括州录事参军卢锷江宁丞韦宁寿州仓曹朱弁后进周愿颜暄沈殷李莆亦尝同修。未毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366816_comment'></div>各以事去。而起居郎裴郁秘书郎蒋志评事吕渭魏理沈益刘全白沈仲昌摄御史陆向沈祖山周阆司议邱悌临川令沈咸右卫兵曹张著兄谟弟荐蔿校书郎权器兴平丞韦桓尼后进房夔崔密崔万窦叔蒙裴继侄男超岘愚子𩑜顾往来登历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366816_comment'></div>时杼山大德僧皎然工于文什。惠达灵煜味于禅诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366816_comment'></div>相与言曰。昔庐山东林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366816_comment'></div>谢客有遗民之会。襄阳南岘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366816_comment'></div>羊公流润甫之词。况乎兹山深邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366816_comment'></div>群士响集。若无记述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366816_comment'></div>何以示将来。乃左顾以求蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366816_comment'></div>俾记词而蒇事。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366816_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1366816'>夏后南巡。山名是因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366816_comment'></div>梁王东揆。寺榜攸询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366816_comment'></div>形胜天绝。规模鼎新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366816_comment'></div>避它城古。垂钓台堙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366816_comment'></div>棚以桂结。浦由黄申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366816_comment'></div>二庾迢递。三癸嶙峋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366816_comment'></div>径列御史。传纡逸人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366816_comment'></div>纷吾著书。群彦惠臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366816_comment'></div>韵海镜源。自秋徂春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366816_comment'></div>编同贯鱼。学比成麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366816_comment'></div>幸托胜引。亟倍僧珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366816_comment'></div>庶斯见传。金石不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366816_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1366816_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年3月</a>　又宴游诸文士,联唱甚盛,有诗。作品：《竹山连句题潘氏书堂》《修<韵海>毕东溪泛舟饯诸文士》《州中重宴》《修<韵海>毕会诸文士东堂重校》(已佚)<div id='poem_826128' class='_poem'><div class='authorDate'>（774年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_826128")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_826128_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_826128_0'>① 颜真卿、陆羽、李萼、裴修、康造、汤清河、清昼、陆士修、房夔、颜粲、颜颛、颜须、韦介、李观、房益、柳淡、颜岘、潘述。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_826128'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_826128'>竹山招隐处，潘子读书堂<span class='inlineComment2'>（真卿）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_826128'>万卷皆成帙，千竿不作行<span class='inlineComment2'>（陆羽）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_826128'>练容餐沆瀣，濯足咏「沧浪」<span class='inlineComment2'>（李萼）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_826128'>守道心自乐，下帷名益彰<span class='inlineComment2'>（裴修）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_826128'>风来似秋兴，花发胜河阳<span class='inlineComment2'>（康造）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_826128'>支策晓云近，援琴春日长<span class='inlineComment2'>（汤清河）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_826128'>水田聊学稼，野圃试条桑<span class='inlineComment2'>（清昼）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_826128'>巾折定因雨，履穿宁为霜<span class='inlineComment2'>（陆士修）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_826128'>解衣垂蕙带，拂席坐藜床<span class='inlineComment2'>（房夔）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_826128'>檐宇驯轻翼，簪裾染众芳<span class='inlineComment2'>（颜粲）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_826128'>草生还近砌，藤长稍依墙<span class='inlineComment2'>（颜颛）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_826128'>鱼乐怜清浅，禽閒憙颉行<span class='inlineComment2'>（颜须。行当作「颃」）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_826128'>空园种桃李，远墅下牛羊<span class='inlineComment2'>（韦介）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_826128'>读《易》三时罢，围棋百事忘<span class='inlineComment2'>（李观）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_826128'>境幽神自王，道在器犹藏<span class='inlineComment2'>（房益）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_826128'>昼歠山僧茗，宵传野客觞<span class='inlineComment2'>（柳淡）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_826128'>遥峰对枕席，丽藻映缣缃<span class='inlineComment2'>（颜岘）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_826128'>偶得幽栖地，无心学郑乡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_826128'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_826128_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_826128'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_826128_0'>⑴ 潘述　见《三长物斋丛书》本《颜鲁公文集》卷十二，宁乡黄本骥编订。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_826128_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年3月</a>　自去年至本年春,又有起居郎裴郁等文士二十七人来往登历杼山,与颜真卿及其修书诸文士游赏唱酬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年</a>　会皇甫曾自丹阳来游，旋即辞归。有诗记其交游。作品：《喜皇甫曾侍御见过南楼玩月联句》（喜嘉客）《重联句》《同皎然皇甫曾西亭重会<韵海>诸生》《泛舟送皇甫侍御曾》（维舟若许暂从容）<div id='poem_51057' class='_poem'><div href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年8月</a>　秋八月，玄真子张志和自越来访，盛宴待之，从者六十余人，有诗。作品：《观玄真子置酒张乐舞破阵画洞庭三山歌》《落玄真子舴艋舟歌》<br /><a href="javascript: href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年7月28日</a>　此日，杭、苏、湖、越诸州遭大风，海水藩潮，民受其害甚巨。嗣后，散骑常侍萧昕奉命来湖宣谕。有帖。作品：《江外帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　仲秋，至平望驿，有诗。作品：《登平望桥下作》<div id='poem_51042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　张志和戏水而卒，为之撰神道碑称颂之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　秋日，与皎然、李萼游法华寺，皎然有诗志之。题有“游觞屿”三字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年10月</a>　此月，应欧阳崘之请，为其父商州刺史欧阳琟撰书神道碑，立于郑州荥泽县。作品：《游击将军左领军卫大将军兼商州刺史武关防御使上柱国欧阳使君（琟）神道碑》<div id='poem_1366840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游击将军左领军卫大将军兼商州刺史武关防御使上柱国欧阳使君神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（775年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366840")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366840'>使君讳琟。字子琟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366840_comment'></div>渤海人。其先出自帝颛顼高阳氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366840_comment'></div>汉有欧阳伯和。伯和孙高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366840_comment'></div>高孙地馀。并列儒林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366840_comment'></div>晋有坚石。著名文苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366840_comment'></div>贤达继轨。其来邈乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366840_comment'></div>六代祖僧宝。始自渤海徙居长沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366840_comment'></div>五代祖頠。陈山阳郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366840_comment'></div>高祖纥。陈开府仪同三司左屯卫大将军交广等十九州诸军事广州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366840_comment'></div>袭山阳郡公。功业并著于前史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366840_comment'></div>曾伯祖询。皇朝银青光禄大夫给事中率更令崇贤馆学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366840_comment'></div>以词学德行。见重前朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366840_comment'></div>笔法孤标。垂名不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366840_comment'></div>曾祖允。年十七以名门子入侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366840_comment'></div>见赏于太宗。十八加正议大夫鲁王傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366840_comment'></div>奉使和突厥。不拜虏廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366840_comment'></div>朝廷嘉之。回封南海郡公施光二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366840_comment'></div>祖谌。洛州巩县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366840_comment'></div>父机。汉州什邡令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366840_comment'></div>以休懿传世。著闻于家邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366840_comment'></div>使君即什邡之第四子。志尚恬旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366840_comment'></div>颛精于诗易春秋。尤明吏术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366840_comment'></div>所居则理。开元十八年解褐安西大都护府参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366840_comment'></div>充阳<span class='inlineComment2'>（集本作汤）</span>嘉惠节度推勾官。外忧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366840_comment'></div>服阕。补北庭大都护府户曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366840_comment'></div>节度使盖嘉运奏授金满令。仍充营田判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366840_comment'></div>以破贼功当迁。请回授幼弟孤侄者三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366840_comment'></div>教义者称之。二十九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366840_comment'></div>河西节度使奏授晋昌郡户曹参军。摄晋昌令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366840_comment'></div>转张掖郡张掖令。摄司马知郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366840_comment'></div>按吏赃罪。罪人诬讼于使司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366840_comment'></div>百姓苗秀康顺忠等三十人。皆截耳称冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366840_comment'></div>节度使王捶骇焉。奏与上考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366840_comment'></div>转岳州长史。时属荒旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366840_comment'></div>人多莩馁。君以禄奉职田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366840_comment'></div>并率官吏。食饿者千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366840_comment'></div>凡月馀。遂多全活。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366840_comment'></div>剑南节度使杨国忠奏知三峡转运。改衡阳郡长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366840_comment'></div>赐绯鱼袋。天宝末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366840_comment'></div>羯胡作乱。统江湖之兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366840_comment'></div>先至南阳。加赐紫金鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366840_comment'></div>充鲁炅南阳节度副使。摄淮南郡长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366840_comment'></div>充当郡防御使。时南阳为贼所围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366840_comment'></div>诸将选懦。莫敢先救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366840_comment'></div>至德元载。君以当郡防御士至新野芙蓉乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366840_comment'></div>遇贼合战。斩其将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366840_comment'></div>犯围而入。炅壮而德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366840_comment'></div>贼围解。加游击将军左金吾卫中郎将兼南阳郡司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366840_comment'></div>迁右骁卫将军兼上洛郡太守。充武关防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366840_comment'></div>肃宗降玺书云。卿以特达之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366840_comment'></div>抱殊常之略。武关防守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366840_comment'></div>委卿一人。属贼陷商于。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366840_comment'></div>复围南阳。君屯兵于淅川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366840_comment'></div>以保乂人吏。逆贼悉力来攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366840_comment'></div>六十馀日。粮尽救绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366840_comment'></div>遂陷贼庭。贼将甘言怵君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366840_comment'></div>令至城下以绐炅。君忠勇感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366840_comment'></div>舍生徇义。抗声谓炅曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366840_comment'></div>凤翔诸将。已收长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366840_comment'></div>琟不能效死军前。辱大夫所使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366840_comment'></div>愿大夫保守忠义。克终令图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366840_comment'></div>贼以兵刃殴君。君志气弥厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366840_comment'></div>因被执送洛阳。今天子收复两京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366840_comment'></div>仅得脱祸。其事具向城令王潇南阳记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366840_comment'></div>炅又奏君充节度兵马使。君遂辞疾不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366840_comment'></div>税驾于郑之别墅。君所居以清白廉慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366840_comment'></div>闻于朝廷。禄俸之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366840_comment'></div>必赒亲族之贫者。先畴旧业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366840_comment'></div>悉群从。一簪不私于其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366840_comment'></div>又常持诵金刚净名经。向逾三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366840_comment'></div>不茹荤血者十年。至是无担石之储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366840_comment'></div>而处顺安时。不改其度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366840_comment'></div>盖澹如也。识者高焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366840_comment'></div>粤以上元二年秋九月十四日。寝疾而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366840_comment'></div>春秋六十有五。夫人高平徐氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366840_comment'></div>安西都护高平县公钦识之女。妇顺母仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366840_comment'></div>克明休德。以大历二年夏六月二十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366840_comment'></div>终于岳州客舍。享年五十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366840_comment'></div>其孤嵩暨。中子崙少子峰等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366840_comment'></div>衔恤允穷。竭力襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366840_comment'></div>以大历十年冬十月二十四日。合祔君暨夫人于荥泽县广武原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366840_comment'></div>遵理命也。崙不远千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366840_comment'></div>泣而求蒙。敢述无愧之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366840_comment'></div>式扬不朽之烈。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366840_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1366840'>猗那使君。世挹清芬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366840_comment'></div>颛经饰吏。休有令闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366840_comment'></div>天子命我。参卿西军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366840_comment'></div>骤迁大县。克懋殊勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366840_comment'></div>让行亲睦。耳截冤分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366840_comment'></div>縻禄食饿。驰师解纷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366840_comment'></div>孤城再色。罢卒益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366840_comment'></div>麾守商于。移兵淅濆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366840_comment'></div>绸缪宸眷。焜耀天文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366840_comment'></div>力尽寇多。师陷身屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366840_comment'></div>诡词绐贼。解路是群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366840_comment'></div>脱祸归朝。义高天云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366840_comment'></div>乞骸廷阙。税驾洧溱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366840_comment'></div>志敦禅诵。茹绝膻荤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366840_comment'></div>处顺齐终。聊乐我云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366840_comment'></div>刻诸金石。永永不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366840_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_100_1366840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年11月</a>　此月间，有帖。作品：《刘中使帖》<div id='poem_1366775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_1_1366775_comment'></div>舍利将军擒获之。吁足慰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366775_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1366775_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　改孙王庙为吴文皇帝庙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=775&endYear=775')">775年</a>　长子颇自天宝末年质于平卢将刘正臣，至是始归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　春日，副使李萼改任他职，与皎然、张荐、卢綸诸人饯行之，有诗。作品：《送李侍御联句》《玩初月重送联句》<div id='poem_51041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51041' class='poemTitle ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　在湖州，有联句诗。作品：《乐语联句》《谗语联句》<div id='poem_51048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
