ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_51048")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_51048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_51048'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_51048'>苦河既济真僧喜<span class='inlineComment2'>（李崿）</span>，新知满座笑相视<span class='inlineComment2'>（真卿）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_51048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_51048'>戍客归来见妻子<span class='inlineComment2'>（清昼）</span>，学生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_51048", 51048, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>放假</span>偷向市<span class='inlineComment2'>（张荐）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_51048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_51048'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_51048_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_51052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_51052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/51052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七言嚵语联句</a><span class='authorDate'>（776年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_51052")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_51052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_51052'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_51052'>拈䭔舐指不知休<span class='inlineComment2'>（李崿）</span>，欲炙侍立涎交流<span class='inlineComment2'>（真卿）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_51052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_51052'>过屠大嚼肯知羞<span class='inlineComment2'>（清昼）</span>，食店门外强淹留<span class='inlineComment2'>（张荐）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_51052_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_51052'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_51052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年4月</a>　四月，应旧僚御史中丞崔祐甫请托，为其父撰述《崔孝公宅陋室铭》<div id='poem_1366798' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366798' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366798?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通议大夫守太子宾客东都副留守云骑尉赠尚书左仆射博陵崔孝公宅陋室铭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（776年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366798")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366798_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366798'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366798'>公讳沔。字若冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366798_comment'></div>博陵安平人。其先出于齐太公之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366798_comment'></div>自亭伯三世文宗。秘书监六□派别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366798_comment'></div>叔轨季则。俱死王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366798_comment'></div>神谦神通。并高循绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366798_comment'></div>子彭宏度。以武干称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366798_comment'></div>景隽巨伦。以文行著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366798_comment'></div>继方面者累代。列史传者十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366798_comment'></div>奕叶相承。恒为鼎族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366798_comment'></div>曾祖宏峻。隋银青光禄大夫赵王长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366798_comment'></div>祖俨。皇朝益州雒县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366798_comment'></div>父暟。年未四十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366798_comment'></div>为库部员外郎。因择能吏为寿安令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366798_comment'></div>又充江西道廉察使。徙醴泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366798_comment'></div>遂历四邑。盘桓不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366798_comment'></div>以刚正也。累至朝散大夫汝州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366798_comment'></div>封安平县男。赠卫尉少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366798_comment'></div>公即安平之次子也。全德天至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366798_comment'></div>成人玉立。盖圣代之宝臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366798_comment'></div>华宗之孝子。文章之哲匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366798_comment'></div>礼乐之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1366798", 1366798, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>祖师</span>。既不可以一名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366798_comment'></div>又何能以悉数。年二十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366798_comment'></div>举乡贡进士。考功郎李迥秀器异之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366798_comment'></div>王佐才也。遂擢高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366798_comment'></div>其年举贤良方正。对策万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366798_comment'></div>公独居第一。而兄浑亦在甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366798_comment'></div>典试官梁载言陈子昂叹曰。虽公孙晁郤不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366798_comment'></div>召见前殿。拜麟台校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366798_comment'></div>繇是名盖天下。御史张思敬以德行荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366798_comment'></div>久之。以资授陆浑主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366798_comment'></div>平阳王敬晖。宏度外之交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366798_comment'></div>略上官之礼。丁府君忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366798_comment'></div>服除。太夫人勉起之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366798_comment'></div>以所试<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1366798", 1366798, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>超迈</span>。擢拜左补阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366798_comment'></div>迁殿中侍御史。奉敕按窃金者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366798_comment'></div>公得其情。许之不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366798_comment'></div>竟得减论。诸王或恃贵不遵法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366798_comment'></div>举而按之。其不吐茹也如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366798_comment'></div>寻迁起居舍人。当扈从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366798_comment'></div>以亲老抗疏乞退。荐琅琊王邱太原郭潾渤海封希颜等自代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366798_comment'></div>睿宗嘉之。特许留司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366798_comment'></div>以遂其孝养。迁祠部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366798_comment'></div>倖僧有请度人者。公拒不奉诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366798_comment'></div>迁给事中。大理卿韩思复用法小差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366798_comment'></div>权臣致劾。公特宽之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366798_comment'></div>迁中书舍人。省改紫微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366798_comment'></div>其官仍旧。又固辞以亲老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366798_comment'></div>除虞部郎中。开元初摄御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366798_comment'></div>或讼吏曹之不平。公与崔泰之衔命详理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366798_comment'></div>多所收拔。俄而即真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366798_comment'></div>兼都畿按察使。岁或不稔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366798_comment'></div>公请发粟赈贷之。赖全活者以万数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366798_comment'></div>内谒者霍元忠有罪。公执之以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366798_comment'></div>玄宗使以玺书劳之。公之澄清中外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366798_comment'></div>以畿县令长陆景融刘体微卢晖有异政。丞尉宋遥皇甫翼陈希烈宋鼎萧隐之范冬芬杨慎馀刘日正高昌寓州掾李瑱裴旷等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366798_comment'></div>并以清白吏疏而荐之。二十二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366798_comment'></div>置十道采访使。公所举六人在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366798_comment'></div>执事子有不法者。公举之不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366798_comment'></div>移著作郎。寻迁秘书少监修图书使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366798_comment'></div>寻判大理卿礼部侍郎。公既职司典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366798_comment'></div>乃删写疏论数百卷。以备阙遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366798_comment'></div>特加朝散大夫。迁左庶子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366798_comment'></div>丁太夫人忧。徵拜中书侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366798_comment'></div>出为魏州刺史。乃肇移元城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366798_comment'></div>徙置新市。吏人便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366798_comment'></div>乙丑岁。玄宗东封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366798_comment'></div>知顿使奏课第一。赐绢二百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366798_comment'></div>岳下观礼。献庆云颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366798_comment'></div>又赐绢一百匹。明年入朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366798_comment'></div>分掌十铨。公与王邱为选人所歌曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366798_comment'></div>沔人澄明澈底清。邱山介直连天峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366798_comment'></div>时人韪之。还州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366798_comment'></div>以理有异绩。御史大夫崔隐甫中丞宇文融朝服表荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366798_comment'></div>玺书宠慰。无何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366798_comment'></div>徵拜左散骑常侍。上以六宫亲蚕丝赐近臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366798_comment'></div>公献御丝赋。又侍宴别殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366798_comment'></div>赋端午诗。屡蒙锡以缣帛䌽罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366798_comment'></div>兼判国子祭酒。俄充东都副留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366798_comment'></div>十七年。有事陵庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366798_comment'></div>追赠安平公及太君曰安平夫人。驾还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366798_comment'></div>罢留守。二十年春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366798_comment'></div>奉敕撰龙门公宴诗序。赐绢百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366798_comment'></div>延入集贤院。修老子道德经疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366798_comment'></div>行于天下。二十一年迁秘书监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366798_comment'></div>修撰如故。属耕藉田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366798_comment'></div>为居守。赐绢百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366798_comment'></div>迁太子宾客。出兼怀州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366798_comment'></div>二十四年罢州。又以本官充东都副留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366798_comment'></div>累加通议大夫。二十七年冬十一月十有七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366798_comment'></div>寝疾薨于位。春秋六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366798_comment'></div>玄宗震悼。赠礼部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366798_comment'></div>葬日量借手力<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1366798", 1366798, "Clauses/182/Comments/0")'>幔幕</span>。故吏前监察御史博陵崔颂为公行状云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366798_comment'></div>公德充符契。精贯人极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366798_comment'></div>孝爱闻于天下。制作垂于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366798_comment'></div>执太夫人之丧。徒跣吐血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366798_comment'></div>以身为粪土。况乎含宏内恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366798_comment'></div>夷坦外名。德至矣乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366798_comment'></div>今之达者。若以富贵崇德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366798_comment'></div>行藏养高。则老莱阙于荣亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366798_comment'></div>黔娄褊于谋道。又加于古人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366798_comment'></div>故养则致其乐。丧则过乎哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366798_comment'></div>以兄姊之戚亚其亲。甥侄之慈甚其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366798_comment'></div>至于药砭备物。温清异宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366798_comment'></div>手胝杵臼之间。身辱浣濯之伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366798_comment'></div>汲汲然矣。每至宗庙心斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366798_comment'></div>严恭祀事。明发不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366798_comment'></div>翌日馀悲。故声气感人者深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366798_comment'></div>仪形化人者远。躬践五德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366798_comment'></div>退让于恭俭温良。行张四维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366798_comment'></div>加信于仁义礼智。而老骥伏枥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366798_comment'></div>以鲍骢不忘。白鸠巢檐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366798_comment'></div>以家瑞终黔。则非殊伦绝辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366798_comment'></div>拟议乎万一矣。太常博士裴总议曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366798_comment'></div>公醇一诞灵。文明含粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366798_comment'></div>蹈元和以为天性。籍间气以为人师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366798_comment'></div>前后历官。或拜而不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366798_comment'></div>或至而不留。瘠形瞽目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366798_comment'></div>誓尊孝养。可不谓孝乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366798_comment'></div>遂谥曰孝公。凡所著文集二十九卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366798_comment'></div>并嗣子祐甫论次先志一卷。为三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366798_comment'></div>吏部员外郎赵郡李华为集序云。公之侍亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366798_comment'></div>孝达乎神祇。居忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366798_comment'></div>哀贯乎天地。丧期有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366798_comment'></div>而茹荼终身。亲交邻里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366798_comment'></div>饥者待公而炊。寒者待公而裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366798_comment'></div>烝尝之奠。待公而具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366798_comment'></div>故禄廪虽厚。而未常足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366798_comment'></div>传祖祢之美。合于礼经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366798_comment'></div>见公文章。知公行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366798_comment'></div>则人伦之序。理乱之源备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366798_comment'></div>祐甫纯行而文。直清而和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366798_comment'></div>希公门者。谓公存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366798_comment'></div>亡贤数载如此。初太夫人患目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366798_comment'></div>公倾家求医。或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366798_comment'></div>疗之必愈。恐寿不得延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366798_comment'></div>太夫人及公悲恨而罢。自是竭力奉养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366798_comment'></div>不脱冠带者仅三十年。每至良辰美景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366798_comment'></div>胜引佳游。必扶侍左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366798_comment'></div>笑言陈说。亲朋往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366798_comment'></div>莫知太夫人之有苦也。公年官虽高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366798_comment'></div>至于食果蔬菜。与子侄躬自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_140_1366798", 1366798, "Clauses/281/Comments/0")'>植艺</span>溉灌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366798_comment'></div>以申馨洁。暨终丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366798_comment'></div>虽见孩稚者。必设位束带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366798_comment'></div>尽哀以礼之。公与江夏李邕友善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366798_comment'></div>为校书郎时。引邕馆于秘阁之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366798_comment'></div>读书者累年。邕由是才名益盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366798_comment'></div>邕与尚书席建侯尝过公。怪乘马癯羸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366798_comment'></div>曰。何不于厅前自观䬴饲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366798_comment'></div>忽然致殒。何以更之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1366798_comment'></div>公唯而不易。他日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1366798_comment'></div>二公又以为言。公良久则曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1366798_comment'></div>每欲发言。恐涉有疑于厮养者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366798_comment'></div>所以沈吟自愧。二公退而谓人曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366798_comment'></div>每想崔公此言。使人惭恧如醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366798_comment'></div>延和太极之间。公既留司东都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366798_comment'></div>遂鬻所乘马。就故人监察御史张汯子深河南府崇政坊买宅以制居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366798_comment'></div>建宗庙于西南。维先太夫人安平郡夫人堂在宅之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366798_comment'></div>俭而不陋。净而不华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366798_comment'></div>六十馀年。榱栋如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366798_comment'></div>堂东嫂卢夫人所居。堂之东北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366798_comment'></div>郑氏李氏姊归宁所居。堂之北五步之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366798_comment'></div>建瓦堂三间以居之。杂用旧椽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366798_comment'></div>不崇坛。无赭垩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366798_comment'></div>累历清要。所得禄秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366798_comment'></div>但奉烝尝。资嫂姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366798_comment'></div>给孤幼。营甥侄婚姻而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366798_comment'></div>朝服衣马。一皆取其下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366798_comment'></div>唯祭器祭服称礼焉。其室竟不修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366798_comment'></div>暨夫人太原郡太夫人王氏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_168_1366798", 1366798, "Clauses/336/Comments/0")'>捐床帐</span>之后。公徙居他室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366798_comment'></div>或在宾馆。而无常所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366798_comment'></div>为常侍时。著陋室铭以自广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366798_comment'></div>天宝末。子孙洒扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366798_comment'></div>贮书籍剑履而已。逆胡再陷洛阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366798_comment'></div>屋遂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_173_1366798", 1366798, "Clauses/346/Comments/0")'>崩圮</span>。唯檐下废井存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366798_comment'></div>长子成甫。倜傥有才名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366798_comment'></div>进士校书郎。早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366798_comment'></div>祐甫能荷先业。以进士高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366798_comment'></div>累登台省。至吏部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1366798_comment'></div>充永平军节度使尚书李公勉行军司马兼侍御史中丞。永怀先德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1366798_comment'></div>明发不寐。恐茂烈烟沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1366798_comment'></div>罔垂后裔。乃刻陋室铭于井北遗址之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1366798_comment'></div>以抒所志。某夙仰名教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1366798_comment'></div>实钦孝公之盛德。晚联台阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1366798_comment'></div>窃慕中丞之象贤。又能好我不遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1366798_comment'></div>见托论撰。采风猷而莫穷万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1366798_comment'></div>涉泉海而岂究津涯。操笔强名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1366798_comment'></div>退增战恧。时则大历十一年青龙景辰孟夏之月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1366798_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_187_1366798_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　拾遗耿湋充括图书使来吴越，先适湖州，然后赴严、越诸州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　夏秋之间，又经湖州归朝，会杨凭、杨凝兄弟并旧友陆涓等来游，遂与皎然等宴集联唱，有诗。作品：《与耿湋水亭咏风联句》《溪馆听蝉联句》《送耿湋拾遗联句》<div id='poem_51044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_8_51065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　秋日，与皎然游白萍洲。又作八角亭供人游息。又作茅亭，书柳恽《江南曲》于其上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年9月9日</a>　重阳日，与皎然诸人登水楼赏菊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　应姻亲秀州长史康元瓌之请，为其父台州刺史康希铣撰书神道碑，明年立在越州山阴离渚墓左。作品：《银青光禄大夫海濮饶房睦台六州刺史上柱国汲郡开国公康使君(希铣)神道碑铭》<div id='poem_1366841' class='_poem'><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366841_comment'></div>字南金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366841_comment'></div>其先出于周。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366841_comment'></div>补右内率府冑曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366841_comment'></div>应词藻宏丽举甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366841_comment'></div>拜秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366841_comment'></div>转左金吾卫录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366841_comment'></div>应博通文史举高第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366841_comment'></div>授太府寺主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366841_comment'></div>转丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366841_comment'></div>又应明于政理举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366841_comment'></div>拜洛州河清令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366841_comment'></div>加朝散大夫泾州司马德州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366841_comment'></div>转定州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366841_comment'></div>属突厥侵轹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366841_comment'></div>君以偏师抗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366841_comment'></div>迁海州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366841_comment'></div>上功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366841_comment'></div>以敕书赐方岳绣袍一领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366841_comment'></div>杂䌽二百段。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366841_comment'></div>下车未几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366841_comment'></div>诏择政术尤异者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366841_comment'></div>察使奏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366841_comment'></div>恩制褒异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366841_comment'></div>迁濮州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366841_comment'></div>加银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366841_comment'></div>累封汲郡开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366841_comment'></div>策勋上柱国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366841_comment'></div>转饶州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366841_comment'></div>入为国子司业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366841_comment'></div>以言事贬房州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366841_comment'></div>转睦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366841_comment'></div>迁台州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366841_comment'></div>所至之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366841_comment'></div>必闻美政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366841_comment'></div>开元初入计至京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366841_comment'></div>抗表请致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366841_comment'></div>玄宗不许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366841_comment'></div>仍留三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366841_comment'></div>请归乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366841_comment'></div>敕书褒美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366841_comment'></div>赐衣一袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366841_comment'></div>并杂䌽等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366841_comment'></div>仍给<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1366841", 1366841, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>传驿</span>至本州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366841_comment'></div>冬十月二十有二日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366841_comment'></div>不幸遘疾薨于会稽觉允里第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366841_comment'></div>春秋七十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366841_comment'></div>夫人陈郡殷氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366841_comment'></div>太子中舍人闻礼之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366841_comment'></div>右清道率令德之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366841_comment'></div>洛州录事参军子恩之第五女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366841_comment'></div>睿宗先天二年封丹阳郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366841_comment'></div>公薨之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366841_comment'></div>殁于东都章善坊私第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366841_comment'></div>春秋六十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366841_comment'></div>嗣子朝散大夫婺州司马袭汲郡公元瑛会稽县男元瑾宣州司士京兆府奉先尉会稽县男元玚朝议郎前获嘉丞元瑰等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366841_comment'></div>虔以天宝四载七月四日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366841_comment'></div>窆于山阴县篱渚村之先茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366841_comment'></div>卜远日而合葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366841_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366841_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366841_comment'></div>君负不器之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366841_comment'></div>包周身之智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366841_comment'></div>宽仁且惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366841_comment'></div>悫愿而恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366841_comment'></div>金玉其相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366841_comment'></div>敬明其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366841_comment'></div>文意丽藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366841_comment'></div>二雅所祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366841_comment'></div>政事优长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366841_comment'></div>百僚所则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366841_comment'></div>尝撰自古以来清白吏图四卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366841_comment'></div>仍自为序赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366841_comment'></div>以见其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366841_comment'></div>宰相黄门侍郎韦承庆中书舍人马吉甫等美而同述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366841_comment'></div>盛行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366841_comment'></div>赴海州时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366841_comment'></div>君兄德言为右台侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366841_comment'></div>弟为偃师令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366841_comment'></div>俱以词学擅名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366841_comment'></div>时同请归乡拜扫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366841_comment'></div>朝野荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366841_comment'></div>与狄仁杰岑羲韦承庆嗣立元怀景姚元崇友善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366841_comment'></div>至是咸倾朝同赋诗以饯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366841_comment'></div>近代未有此比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366841_comment'></div>君之四代祖至于大父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366841_comment'></div>为诸王掾属者七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366841_comment'></div>历尚书郎给事中侍御史者二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366841_comment'></div>君之先君崇文学士府君有文集十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366841_comment'></div>注駮文选异义二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366841_comment'></div>汉书十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366841_comment'></div>自述文集二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366841_comment'></div>元昆修书学士显府君文集十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366841_comment'></div>撰词苑丽则二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366841_comment'></div>海藏连珠三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366841_comment'></div>累璧十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366841_comment'></div>侄秘书监集贤院侍讲学士□元撰周易异义二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366841_comment'></div>秀州长史元瑰著干禄宝典三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366841_comment'></div>侄刑部员外郎璀男美原尉南华撰代耕心镜十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366841_comment'></div>□□□□□□百二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366841_comment'></div>君之先君至南华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1366841_comment'></div>四代进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1366841_comment'></div>登甲科者七人。<div id='poem_sentence_150_1366841_comment'></div>君之女曰辨惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1366841_comment'></div>盩厔县令陕郡长史郜象釴之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1366841_comment'></div>君之孙台州司户参军□□□先岁而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1366841_comment'></div>汾州司田参军真弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1366841_comment'></div>德州平昌县令辅旻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1366841_comment'></div>崇元学生曙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1366841_comment'></div>怀州武陟尉憺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1366841_comment'></div>宣州南陵尉渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1366841_comment'></div>乡贡明经纬纶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1366841_comment'></div>皆修身践言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1366841_comment'></div>敦诗说礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1366841_comment'></div>绍承馀训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1366841_comment'></div>克禀义方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1366841_comment'></div>及君告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1366841_comment'></div>邹自然陈光璧闾邱景阳陶暹送至越州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1366841_comment'></div>邑子谢务迁僧陆鉴校书郎陈齐卿恒为文酒之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1366841_comment'></div>论者休焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1366841_comment'></div>惬求旧之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1366841_comment'></div>崇乞言之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1366841_comment'></div>天乎不慭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1366841_comment'></div>其恨若何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1366841_comment'></div>大历十一年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1366841_comment'></div>元瑰<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙九字）</span>乞愿言刊勒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1366841_comment'></div>惧没徽猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1366841_comment'></div>求无愧之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1366841_comment'></div>垂不朽之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1366841_comment'></div>顾惟末学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1366841_comment'></div>曷足当仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1366841_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1366841_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_180_1366841'>汲公恂恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1366841_comment'></div>德懋而淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1366841_comment'></div>济济多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1366841_comment'></div>东南有筠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1366841_comment'></div>缉熙代业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1366841_comment'></div>词章发身。<div id='poem_sentence_187_1366841_comment'></div>三擢昆玉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1366841_comment'></div>再司□□鹏翔海汭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1366841_comment'></div>骥展河漘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1366841_comment'></div>骤贰嘉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1366841_comment'></div>锡命斯频。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1366841_comment'></div>绣宠方岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1366841_comment'></div>荣加搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1366841_comment'></div>六登□洽胶庠□□□□□□华墓表申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1366841_comment'></div>□□见节文昭友仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1366841_comment'></div>悬车告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1366841_comment'></div>衣锦颐神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1366841_comment'></div>连璧袭懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1366841_comment'></div>梓泽齐彬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1366841_comment'></div>馈酳未济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1366841_comment'></div>舂濛遽沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1366841_comment'></div>朝廷惋悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1366841_comment'></div>远近悲辛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1366841_comment'></div>季子象贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1366841_comment'></div>恐惧郁堙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1366841_comment'></div>嘉猷鸿伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1366841_comment'></div>千秋不泯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_208_1366841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=776&endYear=776')">776年</a>　又撰有碑铭。作品：《和政公主神道碑铭》<div id='poem_1366843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和政公主神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（776年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366843")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366843'>诗美下降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366843_comment'></div>传书<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1366843", 1366843, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>筑馆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366843_comment'></div>贵其中礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366843_comment'></div>载籍称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366843_comment'></div>汉魏已还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366843_comment'></div>寂寥罕嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366843_comment'></div>以荡陵德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366843_comment'></div>则维其常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366843_comment'></div>皇唐勃兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366843_comment'></div>王道丕变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366843_comment'></div>平阳起娘子之军于司竹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366843_comment'></div>襄城行匹庶之礼于宋公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366843_comment'></div>常乐糺匡复之师于武后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366843_comment'></div>皆前古之所未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366843_comment'></div>其或生知礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366843_comment'></div>周旋法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366843_comment'></div>躬行妇道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366843_comment'></div>以懋大伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366843_comment'></div>克顺天经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366843_comment'></div>光昭懿烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366843_comment'></div>名言之所莫究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366843_comment'></div>书记之所未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366843_comment'></div>聚众美于一身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366843_comment'></div>邻太虚而独立者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366843_comment'></div>其唯和政公主乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366843_comment'></div>公主姓李氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366843_comment'></div>陇西成纪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366843_comment'></div>皇唐玄宗至道大圣大明孝皇帝之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366843_comment'></div>肃宗文明武德大圣大宣孝皇帝之第二女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366843_comment'></div>帝女之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366843_comment'></div>于斯为盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366843_comment'></div>今天子之同母妹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366843_comment'></div>母曰章敬皇太后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366843_comment'></div>后之在襁褓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366843_comment'></div>后父赠太尉吴君曰令圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366843_comment'></div>尝游官蜀中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366843_comment'></div>使道士勾规占之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366843_comment'></div>规惊起曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366843_comment'></div>此女贵不可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366843_comment'></div>是生二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366843_comment'></div>男为人君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366843_comment'></div>女为公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366843_comment'></div>嫁于柳氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366843_comment'></div>其后竟配肃宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366843_comment'></div>生今上及公主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366843_comment'></div>神所命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366843_comment'></div>厥惟旧哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366843_comment'></div>公主三岁而孤。<div showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金紫光禄大夫守太子太傅兼宗正卿赠司空上柱国陇西郡开国公李公神道碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（777年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366835")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366835'>昔周武以二公股肱王室。然而允釐西土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366835_comment'></div>师保万民者。其惟召公乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366835_comment'></div>汉室以二傅羽翼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1366835", 1366835, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>储宫</span>。然而亮采东朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366835_comment'></div>仪型百辟者。其惟萧傅乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366835_comment'></div>则九德之师。六行之傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366835_comment'></div>亲贤既美。亦何代无其人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366835_comment'></div>陇西公才为国之垣翰。位为天之喉舌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366835_comment'></div>德为朝之元老。行为帝之信臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366835_comment'></div>盖所谓宗室之间生。士林之杰出者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366835_comment'></div>公讳齐物。字道用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366835_comment'></div>陇西成纪人。自若水导其灵源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366835_comment'></div>而圣人作。高邱峻其层构。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366835_comment'></div>而才子生。元元为宋帝之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366835_comment'></div>兴圣有勤王之举。盛德弥于百祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366835_comment'></div>灵根固于千叶。太祖景皇帝功高佐魏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366835_comment'></div>庆始封唐。家崇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1366835", 1366835, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>八柱</span>之勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366835_comment'></div>地半三分之业。亦犹殷人之祖契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366835_comment'></div>周室之宗文。公即景皇帝之五代孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366835_comment'></div>郑王亮之元孙。淮安王神通之曾孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366835_comment'></div>淮安王皇朝开府仪同三司尚书左仆射。赠司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366835_comment'></div>磐石开府。介圭锡瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366835_comment'></div>成周之晋郑。西汉之勃平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366835_comment'></div>祖孝锐。盐州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366835_comment'></div>父璟。陇州司仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366835_comment'></div>赠宏农太守。并清白贻范。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366835_comment'></div>仁贤继轨。连华公族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366835_comment'></div>济美专城。公禀乾刚之正性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366835_comment'></div>体坤顺之中德。爰自岐嶷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366835_comment'></div>特钟美秀。俨然王公之量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366835_comment'></div>郁有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_29_1366835", 1366835, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>台鼎</span>之姿。固巳超等夷而出群萃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366835_comment'></div>神龙初起家左右千牛备身。历尚辇直长许州司马华州司兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366835_comment'></div>时方振拔。势已飞腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366835_comment'></div>此则江汉之滥觞。华嵩之覆篑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366835_comment'></div>丁太夫人忧。公有至性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366835_comment'></div>毁瘠过礼。扶杖于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366835_comment'></div>哭不绝声者累月。倚庐于墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366835_comment'></div>衣不解带者终丧。天子特降玺书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366835_comment'></div>就庐慰勉。非常之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366835_comment'></div>近古未闻。服阕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366835_comment'></div>授鸿胪丞。除尚辇奉御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366835_comment'></div>迁北都军器监事。太原为一都之雄镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366835_comment'></div>军器掌五库之禁兵。故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1366835", 1366835, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>乾没</span>之赃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366835_comment'></div>一徵百万。缮完之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366835_comment'></div>费省巨亿。少尹严挺之连奏课最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366835_comment'></div>擢拜长安令。陆海殷凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366835_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1366835", 1366835, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>五方</span>浩剧。公以威禁暴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366835_comment'></div>以恕用刑。邑里之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366835_comment'></div>陶然大化。迁将作少匠殿中少监太府少卿怀陕二州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366835_comment'></div>虽汉之宗室。不典<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1366835", 1366835, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>三河</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366835_comment'></div>而周之懿亲。先分二陕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366835_comment'></div>惟良之寄。实在于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366835_comment'></div>尝以黄河经砥柱之艰。有覆舟之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366835_comment'></div>遂奏疏九派。凿三门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366835_comment'></div>属役而坚冰大合。兴功而烈火潜炽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366835_comment'></div>不愆于素。若有神焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366835_comment'></div>人皆以公至诚之所感也。又于石获古铭曰平陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366835_comment'></div>遂以名县焉。玄宗异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366835_comment'></div>赐貂裘一领。绢三百匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366835_comment'></div>特加银青光禄大夫鸿胪卿。并公之先陇州府君专城之赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366835_comment'></div>上尝赐公玉尺一。诏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366835_comment'></div>谓之尺度。可以裁成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366835_comment'></div>卿实多能。故为此赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366835_comment'></div>识者知公必将金玉王度。代天之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366835_comment'></div>岂惟从容九列而已。拜河南尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366835_comment'></div>仍水陆运使。属左相李公适之尚书裴公宽京兆尹韩公朝宗与公为飞语所中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366835_comment'></div>公遂贬竟陵郡太守。时陆羽鸿渐随师郡中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366835_comment'></div>说公下车。召人吏告之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366835_comment'></div>官吏有簠簋不修者。僧道有戒律不精者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366835_comment'></div>百姓有泛驾蹶弛者。未至之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366835_comment'></div>一无所问。而今而后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366835_comment'></div>义不相容。数年间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366835_comment'></div>一境丕变。熙然若羲皇之代矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366835_comment'></div>哀孤重老有隐逸好道者。常骑马于里巷之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366835_comment'></div>亲自恤问。量移安康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366835_comment'></div>即日上道。老幼遮拥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366835_comment'></div>不得发者三辰。转汉阳蕲春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366835_comment'></div>其政如一。公虚中自牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366835_comment'></div>接下愈恭。与物尽推诚之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366835_comment'></div>正身无气燄之忌。每上春行令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366835_comment'></div>大户阅农。轻里糇粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366835_comment'></div>重烦县道。化流江汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366835_comment'></div>如时雨焉。故郡历数四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366835_comment'></div>课事第一。去思之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366835_comment'></div>人到于今称之。天宝末徵拜将作监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366835_comment'></div>重授鸿胪卿。纵壑巨鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366835_comment'></div>还游旧浦。淩风劲翮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366835_comment'></div>俄返故林。时国忠包藏于内<span class='inlineComment2'>（下阙）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366835_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_87_1366835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　本年又有记。作品：《湖州石柱记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　湖州任上，于谢公塘立《晋谢太傅塘碑》，并撰书碑阴记志之。作品：《谢公碑阴记》<div id='poem_1366805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题湖州碑阴</a><span class='authorDate'>（777年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366805")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366805'>太保谢公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366805_comment'></div>东晋咸和中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366805_comment'></div>以吴兴山水清远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366805_comment'></div>求典此郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366805_comment'></div>郡西至长城县通水陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366805_comment'></div>今尚称谢公塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366805_comment'></div>及迁去郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366805_comment'></div>人用怀思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366805_comment'></div>刻石记功焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366805_comment'></div>历代至皇唐天宝末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366805_comment'></div>群盗起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366805_comment'></div>公之碑志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366805_comment'></div>失于所在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366805_comment'></div>眷求芜没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366805_comment'></div>深为怆然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366805_comment'></div>借旧史遗文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366805_comment'></div>敬刊息石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366805_comment'></div>公之雅量宏度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366805_comment'></div>盖嗟叹之不足。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1366805_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　湖州任上交游者尚有王圆、张严、澄师、裴澄与李纵、樊系。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　颜真卿在湖州日，题有“明月峡”三字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=777&endYear=777')">777年</a>　有《吴兴集》十卷。<br /></div>

-----title
秦淮

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=771&endYear=771')">771年11月</a>　十一月，至白下祭扫祖茔，撰书《颜含大宗碑》立于墓田。<div id='poem_1366820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晋侍中右光禄大夫本州大中正西平靖侯颜公大宗碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（771年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366820")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366820'>公讳含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366820_comment'></div>字宏都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366820_comment'></div>琅琊临沂人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366820_comment'></div>其先出于邾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366820_comment'></div>颜公子友封于郳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366820_comment'></div>是为小邾子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366820_comment'></div>为鲁附庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366820_comment'></div>居于邹邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366820_comment'></div>因以命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366820_comment'></div>孔门达者八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366820_comment'></div>曰路回辛骄祖哙仆何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366820_comment'></div>次有丁阖叔子率躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366820_comment'></div>秦有芝贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366820_comment'></div>汉有肆异安乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366820_comment'></div>魏有斐盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366820_comment'></div>盛字叔台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366820_comment'></div>青徐二州刺史关内侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366820_comment'></div>始自鲁居琅琊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366820_comment'></div>代传恭孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366820_comment'></div>故号所居为孝悌里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366820_comment'></div>生钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366820_comment'></div>字公若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366820_comment'></div>明韩诗礼易尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366820_comment'></div>多所通说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366820_comment'></div>学者宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366820_comment'></div>历大中大夫东莞广陵太守葛绎贞子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366820_comment'></div>生默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366820_comment'></div>字静伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366820_comment'></div>晋汝阴太守护军将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366820_comment'></div>生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366820_comment'></div>少有操行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366820_comment'></div>以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366820_comment'></div>兄畿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366820_comment'></div>咸宁中死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366820_comment'></div>托梦当复生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366820_comment'></div>发棺而气息甚微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366820_comment'></div>阖家营视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366820_comment'></div>母妻不能无倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366820_comment'></div>公乃绝弃人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366820_comment'></div>躬亲侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366820_comment'></div>足不出户者十有三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366820_comment'></div>次嫂樊氏失明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366820_comment'></div>须髯蛇胆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366820_comment'></div>寻求不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366820_comment'></div>忽有青衣童子持囊授公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366820_comment'></div>乃蛇胆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366820_comment'></div>寻出户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366820_comment'></div>化成青鸟飞去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366820_comment'></div>东海王越以为太傅参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366820_comment'></div>元帝过江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366820_comment'></div>为丞相祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366820_comment'></div>东宫初建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366820_comment'></div>公以儒素笃行补太子中庶子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366820_comment'></div>迁黄门侍郎本州大中正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366820_comment'></div>封西平县侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366820_comment'></div>拜侍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366820_comment'></div>除吴郡太守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366820_comment'></div>公所历简而有恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366820_comment'></div>明而能断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366820_comment'></div>然以威风御下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366820_comment'></div>王导叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366820_comment'></div>颜公在事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366820_comment'></div>吴人敛手矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366820_comment'></div>未之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366820_comment'></div>复为侍中国子祭酒光禄勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366820_comment'></div>以年老逊位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366820_comment'></div>成帝美其素行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366820_comment'></div>就加右光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366820_comment'></div>门施行马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366820_comment'></div>赐床帐被褥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366820_comment'></div>敕大官四时致膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366820_comment'></div>固辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366820_comment'></div>时论者欲为王导降礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366820_comment'></div>冯怀以问于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366820_comment'></div>公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366820_comment'></div>吾闻伐国不问仁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366820_comment'></div>向冯祖思问佞于我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366820_comment'></div>我有邪德乎。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366820_comment'></div>卞望之之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366820_comment'></div>馀则吾不知。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_534_1366820_comment'></div>顗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_535_1366820_comment'></div>凤翔参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_536_1366820_comment'></div>颉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_537_1366820_comment'></div>当阳主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_538_1366820_comment'></div>愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_539_1366820_comment'></div>千牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_540_1366820_comment'></div>顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_541_1366820_comment'></div>武功丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_542_1366820_comment'></div>颇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_543_1366820_comment'></div>工隶书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_544_1366820_comment'></div>太子洗马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_545_1366820_comment'></div>颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_546_1366820_comment'></div>颒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_547_1366820_comment'></div>并京兆参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_548_1366820_comment'></div>翾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_549_1366820_comment'></div>岘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_550_1366820_comment'></div>颉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_551_1366820_comment'></div>颛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_552_1366820_comment'></div>须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_553_1366820_comment'></div>䪻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_554_1366820_comment'></div>頩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_555_1366820_comment'></div>盈枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_556_1366820_comment'></div>并未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_557_1366820_comment'></div>通明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_558_1366820_comment'></div>项城尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_559_1366820_comment'></div>韶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_560_1366820_comment'></div>有才气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_561_1366820_comment'></div>工诗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_562_1366820_comment'></div>进士濮阳尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_563_1366820_comment'></div>明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_564_1366820_comment'></div>华阳尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_565_1366820_comment'></div>启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_566_1366820_comment'></div>温江尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_567_1366820_comment'></div>袭华阴尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_568_1366820_comment'></div>亚邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_569_1366820_comment'></div>守道不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_570_1366820_comment'></div>其馀枝派繁衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_571_1366820_comment'></div>不可具载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_572_1366820_comment'></div>于戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_573_1366820_comment'></div>吾祖以志行纯粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_574_1366820_comment'></div>感通神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_575_1366820_comment'></div>贻谋子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_576_1366820_comment'></div>奕叶无改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_577_1366820_comment'></div>其后忠义孝悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_578_1366820_comment'></div>文学才业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_579_1366820_comment'></div>布在青史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_580_1366820_comment'></div>粲然可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_581_1366820_comment'></div>非夫德盛流光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_582_1366820_comment'></div>何能若是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_583_1366820_comment'></div>真卿小子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_584_1366820_comment'></div>惧不克荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_585_1366820_comment'></div>顷自抚州代到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_586_1366820_comment'></div>获展旧山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_587_1366820_comment'></div>虽碑版沈沦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_588_1366820_comment'></div>而邱封俨在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_589_1366820_comment'></div>敢扬不朽之烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_590_1366820_comment'></div>庶竭罔极之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_591_1366820_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_592_1366820_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_593_1366820'>铄吾祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_593_1366820_comment'></div>渡江浦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_594_1366820_comment'></div>孝通神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_595_1366820_comment'></div>名轶古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_596_1366820_comment'></div>凡七叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_597_1366820_comment'></div>葬白下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_598_1366820_comment'></div>本支分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_599_1366820_comment'></div>源流溥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_600_1366820_comment'></div>世忠义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_601_1366820_comment'></div>謺规矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_602_1366820_comment'></div>毣鸾皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_603_1366820_comment'></div>炳龙虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_604_1366820_comment'></div>文雎涣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_605_1366820_comment'></div>学邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_606_1366820_comment'></div>赫才明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_607_1366820_comment'></div>振区宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_608_1366820_comment'></div>亘今昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_609_1366820_comment'></div>难悉数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_610_1366820_comment'></div>嗟末孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_611_1366820_comment'></div>惭下武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_612_1366820_comment'></div>扬耿光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_613_1366820_comment'></div>愧无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_614_1366820_comment'></div>丰碑立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_615_1366820_comment'></div>百世睹。</div><div id='poem_sentence_616_1366820_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
阜阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='896dd76563b04623ab934c3bb3cc17b6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("896dd76563b04623ab934c3bb3cc17b6");'><span id='896dd76563b04623ab934c3bb3cc17b6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>，64岁</div><div id='896dd76563b04623ab934c3bb3cc17b6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　赴京途中，道出汝阴，书十四代祖《颜默碑》旧文，立石于颍州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='984af44807284b9080f6f17cdf92f187_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("984af44807284b9080f6f17cdf92f187");'><span id='984af44807284b9080f6f17cdf92f187_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>，64岁</div><div id='984af44807284b9080f6f17cdf92f187' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年5月8日</a>　五月，至宋州。八日，有八关斋会，因宋州刺史徐向之请，撰书亟颂旧友田神功。田悦篆额。作品：《八关斋功德记》<div id='poem_1366796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有唐宋州官吏八关斋会报德记</a><span class='authorDate'>（772年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366796")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366796'>夫德之所感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366796_comment'></div>沦骨髓而非深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366796_comment'></div>诚之所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366796_comment'></div>去神明而何远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366796_comment'></div>有唐大历壬子岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1366796_comment'></div>宋州八关斋会者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1366796_comment'></div>此都人士暨文武将吏朝散大夫使持节宋州诸军事行宋州刺史兼侍御史本州团练守捉使赐紫金鱼袋徐向等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1366796_comment'></div>奉为河南节度观察使开府仪同三司太子太师左右仆射知省事兼御史大夫汴州刺史上柱国信都郡王田公顷疾良已之所建也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1366796_comment'></div>公名神功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1366796_comment'></div>冀州南宫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1366796_comment'></div>禀元和之粹灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1366796_comment'></div>膺期运以杰出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1366796_comment'></div>含宏厚下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1366796_comment'></div>正直率先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1366796_comment'></div>起孝而德感生人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1366796_comment'></div>竭忠而精贯白日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1366796_comment'></div>和众必资于宽简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1366796_comment'></div>安人务在于抚柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1366796_comment'></div>况乎武艺绝伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1366796_comment'></div>英谋沈秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1366796_comment'></div>所向而前无强敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1366796_comment'></div>日新而学有缉熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1366796_comment'></div>故能殿天子之邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1366796_comment'></div>郁苍生之望有日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1366796_comment'></div>羯戎搆逆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1366796_comment'></div>公以平卢节将佐今右仆射李公忠臣收沧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1366796_comment'></div>攻相州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1366796_comment'></div>拒杏园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1366796_comment'></div>守陈留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1366796_comment'></div>许叔冀降而陷焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1366796_comment'></div>思明惧忠臣图己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1366796_comment'></div>令公佐南德信随刘从谏收江淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1366796_comment'></div>至宋州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1366796_comment'></div>欲袭李铣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1366796_comment'></div>公斩德信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1366796_comment'></div>走从谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1366796_comment'></div>遂并其众而报焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1366796_comment'></div>肃宗大悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1366796_comment'></div>拜公鸿胪卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1366796_comment'></div>再袭敬釭于郓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1366796_comment'></div>加中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1366796_comment'></div>讨刘展于润州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1366796_comment'></div>斩平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1366796_comment'></div>迁徐州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1366796_comment'></div>明年拜淄青节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1366796_comment'></div>属候希逸自平卢至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1366796_comment'></div>公以州让之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1366796_comment'></div>时宋州刺史李岑为贼所围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1366796_comment'></div>副元帅李光弼请公讨平之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1366796_comment'></div>拜御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1366796_comment'></div>加开府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1366796_comment'></div>充兖郓节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1366796_comment'></div>破法子营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1366796_comment'></div>又讨敬釭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1366796_comment'></div>釭归顺焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1366796_comment'></div>史朝义闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1366796_comment'></div>奔下博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1366796_comment'></div>投范阳自缢死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1366796_comment'></div>广德元年授户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1366796_comment'></div>封信都郡王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1366796_comment'></div>上幸陕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1366796_comment'></div>公首来扈从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1366796_comment'></div>都知六军兵马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1366796_comment'></div>每食宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1366796_comment'></div>公皆躬自省视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1366796_comment'></div>上感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1366796_comment'></div>方委以政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1366796_comment'></div>公涕泣固辞而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1366796_comment'></div>二年拜汴宋节度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1366796_comment'></div>迁兵部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1366796_comment'></div>大历二年加右仆射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1366796_comment'></div>封母清河张氏为赵国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1366796_comment'></div>妻信安郡王袆女为凉国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1366796_comment'></div>太夫人慈和勤俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1366796_comment'></div>睦于亲党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1366796_comment'></div>公性纯孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1366796_comment'></div>居常不离左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1366796_comment'></div>阅读书史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1366796_comment'></div>或时疾病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1366796_comment'></div>公辄累月不茹薰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1366796_comment'></div>家中礼忏不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1366796_comment'></div>仍造崇夏宏圣二寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1366796_comment'></div>以祈福祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1366796_comment'></div>五年兼判左仆射知省事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1366796_comment'></div>加太子太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1366796_comment'></div>公德厚量深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1366796_comment'></div>劳谦重慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1366796_comment'></div>功既高而心益下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1366796_comment'></div>位弥大而体益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1366796_comment'></div>故远无不怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1366796_comment'></div>迩无不肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1366796_comment'></div>今夏四月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1366796_comment'></div>忽婴热疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1366796_comment'></div>沈顿累旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1366796_comment'></div>积善降祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1366796_comment'></div>勿药遄喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1366796_comment'></div>鹰犬之玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1366796_comment'></div>悉皆弃舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1366796_comment'></div>群帅感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1366796_comment'></div>无复弋猎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1366796_comment'></div>四履之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1366796_comment'></div>咸怀欢欣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1366796_comment'></div>雎阳之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1366796_comment'></div>踊跃尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1366796_comment'></div>乃咨于州将曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1366796_comment'></div>昔我公之陷贼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1366796_comment'></div>至敝邑而首诛德信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1366796_comment'></div>李岑之见围也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1366796_comment'></div>破其党而克保城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1366796_comment'></div>是即我公再有大造于敝邑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1366796_comment'></div>微我公之救恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1366796_comment'></div>即皆死于锋镝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1366796_comment'></div>入于煎熬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1366796_comment'></div>尚何能保完家室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1366796_comment'></div>嬉戏乡井者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1366796_comment'></div>不资斋明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1366796_comment'></div>何以报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1366796_comment'></div>徐公悦而从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1366796_comment'></div>来五月八日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1366796_comment'></div>首以俸钱三十万设八关大会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1366796_comment'></div>饭千僧于开元伽蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1366796_comment'></div>将佐争承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1366796_comment'></div>唯恐居后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1366796_comment'></div>已而州县官吏长史苗藏实等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1366796_comment'></div>设一千五百人为一会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1366796_comment'></div>镇遏团练官健副使孙琳等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1366796_comment'></div>设五百人为一会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1366796_comment'></div>耆寿百姓张列等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1366796_comment'></div>设五千人为一会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1366796_comment'></div>法筵等供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1366796_comment'></div>仄塞于郊坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1366796_comment'></div>赞呗香花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1366796_comment'></div>喧填于昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1366796_comment'></div>其馀乡村聚落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1366796_comment'></div>来往舟车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1366796_comment'></div>闻风而靡督自勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1366796_comment'></div>耸惠而怵先胥懋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1366796_comment'></div>又不可胜数矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1366796_comment'></div>非夫美政淳深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1366796_comment'></div>德风汪濊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1366796_comment'></div>则何以感人若此其至者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1366796_comment'></div>某叨接好仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1366796_comment'></div>饱承馀烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1366796_comment'></div>睹兹盛美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1366796_comment'></div>益腼求蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1366796_comment'></div>若不垂诸将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1366796_comment'></div>则记事者奚述。</div><div id='poem_sentence_146_1366796_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
许昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4a3d7b37ce14408aa5ec424e501b8049_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a3d7b37ce14408aa5ec424e501b8049");'><span id='4a3d7b37ce14408aa5ec424e501b8049_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>，75岁</div><div id='4a3d7b37ce14408aa5ec424e501b8049' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>　既至许州，李希烈先胁后礼，揖送于馆舍。请上表昭雪，见不从，乃诈以其名，数遣其侄颜岘与从吏表奏，以请汴州。德宗知而寝之。嗣后，大陈宴会，欲送归朝，会原汝州别驾李元平在座，颜真卿斥责之，元平惭而潜通，遂改初衷，拘之于官舍。其与诸子书，仅言严奉家庙，恤诸孤而已。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
汝州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5b7b071773614b7c8c074f78242d47d8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5b7b071773614b7c8c074f78242d47d8");'><span id='5b7b071773614b7c8c074f78242d47d8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=784')">783-784年</a>，75-76岁</div><div id='5b7b071773614b7c8c074f78242d47d8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年3月20日</a>　此日，荆南节度使张伯仪与淮宁兵战于安州，大败之，李希烈以其旌节及所获将士首级夸示于前。愤绝良久，醒后不复与人言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=783&endYear=783')">783年</a>　在囚所，祭奠反正死难烈士，且自撰墓志，以示死志。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=784&endYear=784')">784年1月</a>　本月，李希烈称帝，数逼之，不为其屈节。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=784&endYear=784')">784年1月</a>　夏日，陆长源权领湖州，撰写《颜鲁公去思颂》。其后，杨昱出任湖州刺史，铭石立于州门之外。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
驻马店
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='905fd928f508436b8ca443663783c9de_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("905fd928f508436b8ca443663783c9de");'><span id='905fd928f508436b8ca443663783c9de_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年</a>，77岁</div><div id='905fd928f508436b8ca443663783c9de' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年1月5日</a>　此日，颜真卿自汝州移囚蔡州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年1月19日</a>　此日，作《移蔡帖》<div id='poem_1366774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1366774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1366774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移蔡帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（785年1月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21650, "唐", "颜真卿", "poem_title_1366774")'>颜真卿</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1366774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1366774'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1366774'>贞元元年正月五日。真卿自汝移蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1366774_comment'></div>天也。天之昭明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1366774_comment'></div>其可诬乎。有唐之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1366774_comment'></div>则不朽耳。十九日书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1366774_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1366774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=785&endYear=785')">785年8月24日</a>　此日，遇害于蔡州龙兴寺。<br /></div>
-----end
